# Fulfilment / Expéditions arc — «Expéditions» christens Le Cockpit (LIVE-BUILT 2026-06-07)

> Read when touching: `ord_orders`/`ord_order_lines`/`ord_order_status_events`, `ref_customers`, `ref_transporters`, `public/modules/expeditions.php`, `api/expeditions-status.php`, `app/fg-stock.php` (`fg_stock_compute()`), the Commandes dashboard, customer bootstrap, or the future commandes@ email ingestion. Companion: [sales-commercial-surface.md](sales-commercial-surface.md) (eshop/BC two-source model), [sku-bom-validation-walkthrough.md](sku-bom-validation-walkthrough.md) RULE #3/#4 + Stage-2 tracker, [mother-shell-architecture.md](mother-shell-architecture.md) EXPÉDITION Stage-3 placeholder.

## 🆕 SHOPIFY FULFILMENT-DATE (izyrent rentals) — PM RULED 2026-06-17 (build pending Sonnet)
Operator-urgent: the eshop "Boutique en ligne" board groups by `DATE(iso.created_at)` (= order-placement), useless for "what to prep this week". Kouros's raw-data investigation (verified, no guess): the ONLY orders with a real future fulfilment date are **izyrent portable-tap rentals** (10 in his 250-order window; PM live-probed 19 since 2026-05-01, all `tags LIKE '%izyrent%'`, all currently `fulfilment_mode='review'` except #12968=pickup). Date lives in a Shopify **line-item property `"Date"`** = FR date-range string `"{D} {Mois} {YYYY} au {D} {Mois} {YYYY}"` (Juin/Juillet/Août/Septembre/Décembre seen). Regular retrait-boutique pickups + plain deliveries carry NO date (genuinely no schedule). **PM VERDICT:**
- **(1) SCHEMA — APPROVED order-level.** `fulfilment_date DATE NULL` + `fulfilment_date_end DATE NULL` on `inv_sales_orders` (one rental period per order; board groups orders; lines carry no per-line date). NOT on `inv_sales_order_lines`. `start`=day-operator-must-have-it-ready (the board key), `end`=display range. NULL for every non-dated order.
- **(2) INGEST — APPROVED, parse best-effort.** Add `properties` to `ShopifyLineItem`; parse the `"Date"` prop via FR-month map Janvier..Décembre → start+end. Parse-fail OR no-Date-prop → leave NULL, NEVER crash, NEVER guess a date. **created_at + period STAY AS-IS** (fiscal/COGS/sales period = placement month — agreed; fulfilment_date is OPERATIONAL-display only).
- **(3) BOARD — group-by-fulfilment-date with COALESCE fallback.** Dated (izyrent) orders surface on `COALESCE(fulfilment_date, DATE(created_at))` so they land in the right prep-week; non-dated orders unchanged (fall through to created_at). Add a prominent date-range badge ("Tireuse 18→19 juin") on dated cards. This fits the existing `DATE()`-group structure with one COALESCE swap in the eshop query's group/sort key (expeditions.php ~L1931/2015/2024) — cleaner than a parallel badge-and-sort path.
- **(4) BACKFILL — re-run ingest, BUT one-line guard needed.** The header-upsert is idempotent on `(source,external_order_id)` BUT the existing-row UPDATE path (ingest L486-525) only re-syncs `fulfillment_status/shipping_method_title/fulfilment_mode` — a naive re-run will NOT fill `fulfilment_date` on the 19 existing rows. **MUST add `fulfilment_date`/`_end` to the `existing` SELECT + `mutableChanged` test + UPDATE SET**, then re-run over history fills them. DIVERGENCE FLAG: if that's skipped, only NEW orders get dates → silent split (old izyrent dateless, new dated). No separate backfill script.
- **(5) SCOPE — date-ONLY here; classification stays in task-3.** Do NOT touch `fulfilment_mode` in this slice (leave the 18 izyrent at 'review'). Auto-classifying izyrent→pickup belongs to the queued "review orders" task. Keep this slice tight: schema + parse + board key + backfill.
- **SOT-CHAIN: NO.** `inv_sales_orders` is `schema_meta table_class='source'`, `corrections_policy='blocked_with_redirect'` (raw API pull, "fix in source eshop, re-pull"). `fulfilment_date` is a DERIVED-at-ingest parse of raw API data (same status as created_at/period/fulfilment_mode) — purely an OPERATIONAL DISPLAY attribute, NOT part of the Le Zeppelin commissioning→BOM→COGS chain. The downstream eshop-consumption deriver keys on SKU LINES, not order dates → fulfilment_date never touches COP/COGS/WAC/beer-tax. Because the table is blocked_with_redirect, the column must ONLY ever be re-derived by the ingest, NEVER hand-edited.
- **MIG-NUMBER CAVEAT: parallel sessions live — `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` IMMEDIATELY before assigning** (index banner cites HEAD 391/392; re-probe, don't trust). MySQL 8: `ALTER TABLE inv_sales_orders ADD COLUMN fulfilment_date DATE NULL, ADD COLUMN fulfilment_date_end DATE NULL;` (no IF NOT EXISTS). No new table → no schema_meta row; bump schema_meta.updated_at note on inv_sales_orders if desired. RULE 3 tour: N/A (no ref_pages change). RULE 1 scrap: nothing superseded.
- **EQUIP: coder + sql + ui (+ webapp-testing smoke of the eshop board).** Ingest TS parse = coder; migration = sql; board COALESCE+badge = ui.

## 🆕 STATE-MACHINE AUTOMATION — 2 transitions auto (PM DESIGN RULED 2026-06-17; build pending; Ruling-4 revision PENDING operator mail-investigation)
Kouros wants 2 of the 5 `ord_orders` transitions automated, the other 3 stay manual. Target: création→`entered` (already auto); **mail confirmation client → `entered→confirmed` AUTO**; `picked`=manual; **BC `Completely_Shipped` → `bl_printed` AUTO**; `shipped`=manual.
**🔑 GROUND TRUTH (PM live-probed 2026-06-17 — re-verified, NOT stale):**
- **Ruling-4 is CURRENTLY CLEAN.** The auto-`bl_printed` deviation that B was flagged to fix **IS removed** in the deployed `ingest_bc_sales_orders.py`: it writes `bc_completely_shipped=1` as a **mirror SIGNAL ONLY** (L1913-1917 "signal only"), NO status, NO status_events (L755/806). Target #4 **deliberately RE-OPENS** this — defensible, traced.
- **🔴 CARDINAL INVARIANT that makes #4 architecturally OK: FG depletion arms on `status='shipped'` EXCLUSIVELY** (`fg-stock.php` Step 4, L27/L418). `bl_printed` is PRE-depletion → auto-advancing to it touches NO COGS/FG/WAC/beer-tax. If anyone ever moves the depletion key onto `bl_printed`, the BC auto-advance would fire depletion on a PULL (wrong lane) — the auto-advance code MUST carry a "never extend to shipped" contract-comment + an Opus delta_phys=0 tripwire probe.
- Manual handler `public/api/expeditions-status.php` already has the full machinery (statusRank — NEVER ENUM ordinal; advanceMap; event+cache in ONE txn + log_revision; CSRF-retry). REUSE.
- `ord_order_status_events`: `user_id_fk` NULL-able; **NO `source` col** — origin distinguished via `comment` (imports use `'import:weeklyorders'`). Auto-BC events stamp `comment='auto:bc-shipped'`, user_id_fk=NULL. NO migration for the origin marker.
- **NO confirmation email exists** (zero send in expeditions.php; "confirmation" hits are status labels only). `send_mail()` + `mail_account_template()` (app/services/mailer.php) reusable. status ENUM already has `bl_printed`; `bc_completely_shipped` + `bc_no` cols exist. Only admin user = Kouros id=1 (no system user).
**PM VERDICT:**
- **A. Ruling-4 revision = VALIDATED under 5 guard-rails.** (1) idempotence via `current_status ∈ {entered,confirmed,picked}` AND `completely_shipped` (auto-idempotent, no edge-detect needed); (2) **multi-cran jump ALLOWED** to `bl_printed` from any upstream state, BUT emit the SKIPPED intermediate events at one occurred_at (events=truth, mirrors WeeklyOrders import) — auto-BC is a DISTINCT path from the 1-cran manual handler; (3) **strict monotonic — never recede**: if `current_status ∈ {bl_printed,shipped,cancelled}` do nothing (shipped never recedes; cancelled never resurrects — consistent with `_REFRESH_LINE_STATUSES`); (4) origin marker via `comment='auto:bc-shipped'`; (5) **🆕 depletion invariant as non-regression tripwire** (contract-comment + delta_phys=0 probe). Only advance `source='bc'` orders in the open pull set — pre-cutover SKIP_BACKLOG rows (L142) stay excluded (the upstream-state condition handles this; re-verify at build).
- **B. Mail→confirmed: mail DOESN'T EXIST → build it as a SEPARATE prerequisite** (HTML email-safe template + ref_customers.email resolution + "Envoyer confirmation" button + send_mail). Hook AFTER successful send, OUTSIDE the SMTP step (SMTP not transactional): send → if `true` → ONE txn event(confirmed)+cache+log_revision (reuse manual logic). Monotonic: advance ONLY if `current_status='entered'` (if past confirmed: send mail, do NOT advance/re-stamp). CONFIRMED.
- **C. Independent + separately shippable. ORDER: #4 FIRST** (pure logic in `ingest_bc_sales_orders.py`, **NO migration** — essentially re-adding `should_advance_to_bl_printed()` cleanly with the 5 guard-rails). Then #2 (build mail, then hook). **NO migration in v1**: origin marker via comment; `confirmation_email_sent_at` REFUSED (append-only event carries the fact). Board live-refresh piège: an order self-advancing to bl_printed at `*/15` appears advanced with no operator click → **add a board badge derived from last event `comment='auto:bc-shipped'`** (like the lead-time badge) so the operator distinguishes auto-BC from a colleague's click. Connector SELECT-status FOR UPDATE inside txn to avoid manual-click × cron race.
- **D. `ord_orders` ONLY** — NOT the separate eshop machine `inv_sales_fulfilment`/`_events` (mig 321/322, mode-aware, own API). `bc_completely_shipped` is ord_orders-only; B2B confirmation mail ≠ Shopify write-back. No interaction. CONFIRMED.
- **EQUIP:** #4 → coder+sql (Python connector + DB invariant, no UI). #2a/2b → ui+coder+sql+webapp-testing (email template, board hook, smoke). Board auto-BC badge → ui.
- **STATUS: A validated; B/C/D ruled; awaiting Kouros's mail-existence re-ping to lock the Ruling-4 revision as DEFINITIVE (mail confirmed non-existent by PM probe — so "build it" stands unless Kouros finds one elsewhere).** Trigger "ruling-4"/"auto bl_printed"/"completely_shipped auto"/"mail confirmation"/"entered→confirmed auto"/"automate transition"/"state machine automation" → this section.

## 🆕 ORDER-AWARE COVERAGE (FAST-FOLLOW #1 to the burn engine) — PM RULINGS 2026-06-11 (pre-build; render-only, NO mig)
Kouros flagged a real inconsistency: the seasonal headline `semaines_stock` is pure `physique÷burn` and IGNORES the committed open-order book, while `live_futur` (=physique−open_total) already encodes it. PROOF SKU **ALTF**: physique=40, rythme_base(L)=2.4/wk → semaines=14.4, BUT 45 units on the open book (overdue/near 30+6+6 + a 3 due 07-03) → live_futur=−5 (survendu). 14.4 is arithmetically fine but operationally blind. **DECISION (Kouros): order-aware coverage — the forward sim subtracts committed open orders at their due dates FIRST, then burns the rest at the seasonal rate.** Reconciles `semaines_stock` with `live_futur`. RENDER-TIME ONLY (orders already queried Step 7) — NO migration.
- **RULING Q1 — RECONCILIATION = `max()`, RULED.** Per forward week: `demand[week] = max(L×S[week], open_orders[week])`. Adding double-counts (history `L×S` is already mostly B2B orders; the open book is the *realization* of that same demand). `max()` = take the better-informed estimate per week: a big committed order dominates its week; an order-free week still burns the seasonal baseline. **REJECTED "orders-replace-forecast-for-ordered-weeks, baseline-for-the-rest"** — a small order in a high-baseline peak week would UNDER-burn (false runway = the dangerous direction). Overdue + current-ISO-week orders FOLD into forward-week-1 (mirrors live_futur treating the whole open book as immediately-committed). **GUARD: the fractional-stockout denominator (`($h-1)+$stock/$forecast`) must use the reconciled `demand[week]`, not raw L×S — apply `max()` INSIDE the loop before the `$stock<=$forecast` test.**
- **RULING Q2 — SINGLE BURN PATH = CONFIRMED, with one HARD invariant.** Order-aware logic lives INSIDE `sb_forward_weeks()` (the lone sim consumer) — it gains ONE param `array $openByWeek` passed in; the runway derivation stays single. The bucketed open-orders query (Step 8) **MUST mirror the live_futur query (Step 7, fg-stock.php:558-567) EXACTLY**: same `FROM ord_order_lines l JOIN ord_orders o ON o.id=l.order_id_fk`, same `WHERE o.status NOT IN ('shipped','cancelled')`, **NO upper date bound** (live_futur subtracts the ENTIRE open book). **HARD INVARIANT / build-time assertion: Σ(openByWeek across all buckets per SKU) == that SKU's `open_total_qty` from Step 7.** Ideally derive both from ONE fetch so they can't drift. **AXIS: bucket by weeks-from-today (`FLOOR(DATEDIFF(requested_date,today)/7)` clamped ≥0 for overdue/current), NOT YEARWEEK-of-year** — the sim loops by horizon offset `$h`, so the PHP bucket the sim consumes must be the `$h` axis (SQL may still compute YEARWEEK, convert to offset before feeding the sim).
- **RULING Q3 — MEANING SHIFT = SAFE, no downstream breaks (every consumer traced).** `semaines_stock` shifts from 'burn-runway on physical stock' → 'runway accounting for committed orders + burn'. All consumers take it as opaque `float|null`; a smaller number simply lands a lower (more urgent) health tier = INTENDED. 6-tier `exp_classify_*` (expeditions.php:2577-2624, WEEKS_CRITICAL=1/LOW=3/HIGH=10), `flag_low_stock` (fg-stock.php:677 `<2.0 && physique>0`), `exp_fmt_semaines`, gauge bars — ALL unchanged. **🔴 THE ONE CARE POINT: tier 6 `sans_rotation` = `physique>0 && semaines_stock===null` means 'no burn data / EOL', NOT 'order-depleted'. An order-aware stockout in week 1 must return a small POSITIVE float (or 0), NEVER null. ALTF → ~0 weeks (critique), NOT sans_rotation. Keep null reserved strictly for no-level/EOL (sb_forward_weeks already returns positive on stockout — preserve).** Divergence with live_futur is REDUCED not raised (that's the deliverable): post-change both encode order-awareness → can no longer contradict (one survendu / other 14wk). Invariant: live_futur<0 ⇒ semaines≤~0-1wk (week-1 bucket carries all overdue/current orders > physique). Bands/legend/`sans rotation` logic UNCHANGED — only the number. COPY tweak (ui, not logic): legend/drill may note "couverture (stock − commandes engagées)" so operator reads it as order-aware.
- **RULING Q4 — DRILLDOWN = EXTEND the existing `exp-stock-drill` with a THIRD face "Couverture". NOT a modal, NOT the exp-hist client panel.** The `?view=stock` per-SKU drill is ALREADY a `role=tablist` segmented toggle (commit `711905c` 2026-06-10): Face "Stock" + Face "Activité", delegated `button[data-evt-tab]` scoped `closest('.exp-stock-drill')` + `resetDrillFace()` on collapse. **Add a 3rd tab/face.** Modals are reserved for the Commandes view (`exp-stock-detail-modal`, opened from expeditions.js) — a modal here forks the idiom (UI-level divergence smell). The `exp-hist-*` panel is per-CLIENT (wrong grain). The "Couverture" face carries Kouros's breakdown: physique+flows, open-order book by date (reuse the already-loaded data, no new query), live_futur, rythme de base L + lumpiness note (Q5), the family seasonal curve, and the **week-by-week projection table** (demand=max(L×S,orders) · running stock · week-hits-0 · status) — the high-value artifact making `max()` legible. Feed via the established `window.EXP_*` page-wide injection (sim emits an optional per-week trace), NO AJAX/endpoint (mirrors "Activité récente" + the risk modal). A11y: real `<button role=tab>`/`role=tabpanel`, `resetDrillFace()` resets across all 3 faces on every collapse path, arrow-nav extends to 3.
- **RULING Q5 — CROSTON'S STAYS FAST-FOLLOW (confirmed). SHOW lumpiness, don't change level math.** Kouros chose 'Order-aware' not 'Both' → sporadique/Croston's (ADI>1.32) stays deferred. The "Couverture" face SHOWS `nonzero_weeks/53` + recent-spike note as DIAGNOSTIC context (e.g. "17/53 sem. avec ventes · pic récent"), NOT a recomputed L. **Order-awareness is the load-bearing fix for ALTF, not Croston's** — with the 45 committed units folded in, ALTF reads ~0wk regardless of whether L=2.4 or Croston's-corrected; the lumpy L misreading the spike is 2nd-order. Folding Croston's in now = two level-math paths in one build = scope-creep against single-burn-path discipline. Keep it a clean separate fast-follow.
- **VERDICT + SEQUENCING:** architecturally sound; render-time-only, NO migration (orders already queried). Single-path integrity hinges on ONE query matching live_futur exactly + the Σ(buckets)==open_total_qty assertion. Safe in one arc. No `ref_pages` change → NO tour-steward dispatch.
- **EQUIP: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing.** sql = bucketed open-orders query (mirror Step 7 filter/join exactly) + Σ-reconciliation EXPLAIN/dry-run; coder = `sb_forward_weeks()` order-aware param + Step 8 wiring + per-week trace emission; ui = the 3rd "Couverture" drill face (mirror `711905c` tablist idiom, inline NOT modal) + projection table + lumpiness note; webapp-testing = read-only `?view=stock` prod smoke (ALTF reads survendu/~0, 3rd face opens, projection renders, no 500).

## 🆕 SEMAINES-RESTANTES / BURN-RATE — SCOPE UPGRADED to FORWARD SEASONAL ENGINE (S&OP expert ruling) — PM ARCHITECTURE RULING 2026-06-11 (✅ NOW BUILT — see SHIPPED block above)
Kouros uploaded weekly sales per SKU back to 2021 → wants real "semaines restantes de stock" on `?view=stock`. **The flat trailing-24mo-mean swap is SUPERSEDED.** Kouros consulted an industry S&OP/demand-planning expert; the locked model is a **forward, seasonal, family-pooled depletion engine**: family multiplicative seasonal index `S[family][1..52]`, per-SKU deseasonalized EW level `L[sku]` (λ=0.95, half-life ~13wk), forward week-by-week depletion sim charging `L×S[isoweek]`, status chip (normal/provisoire/sporadique-Croston/EOL), display triad. Full locked model in the consult message of record.
- **KEY FINDING (still holds) — this is a VELOCITY-SOURCE SWAP at the seam, not a new surface.** `semaines_stock` ALREADY EXISTS in `app/fg-stock.php` (Step 8, ~L586), wired into `?view=stock`: 6-tier health (`WEEKS_CRITICAL=1`/`WEEKS_LOW=3`/`WEEKS_HIGH=10`, `exp_classify_*` ~L2447-2494), `exp_fmt_semaines()` "∞" formatter ~L3852, progress bars ~L4278, `flag_low_stock`. Today velocity = trailing-56-day flat mean off `inv_sales_bc`+`inv_sales_order_lines`. The new engine REPLACES the Step-8 numerator/window with `L×S` forward sim; `physique` numerator + all downstream classification/render UNCHANGED (thresholds may need re-tuning to forward semantics — fast-follow).
- **DATA SOURCE = `inv_sales_ledger`** (live-verified 2026-06-11): `posting_date` DATE (idx `idx_sl_posting`), `sku_id_fk` INT UNSIGNED (idx `idx_sl_sku`), `qty_signed`/`qty_invoiced` DECIMAL(14,4) SKU units, `hl_resolved`, `doc_type` ENUM(shipment/invoice/credit/return_receipt). **2021-01-05→2026-06-09, 44,164 rows, 133 SKUs.** ⚠️ **25% NULL `sku_id_fk`** (unresolved sku_code_raw) — coverage-gap surface, NEVER drop. ⚠️ **NO composite (sku_id_fk, posting_date) index — only two single-col idxs; mig must add the covering composite** for the per-SKU 52wk pull + the cron's full decomposition.
- **🔴 FAMILY POOLING DATA TRUTH (live-verified — the expert model assumed `recipe_id_fk`; THE DB DOES NOT HAVE IT):** `inv_sales_ledger` has **NO `recipe_id_fk`** (only `sku_id_fk`). `ref_skus` has **NO `recipe_id_fk` either — the family key is `ref_skus.recipe_id` (INT UNSIGNED, NULLable)**. So **family = `ref_skus.recipe_id`, reached by JOIN `inv_sales_ledger.sku_id_fk → ref_skus.id → recipe_id`** (NOT a direct column, NOT a string). **25 distinct recipe families** in the resolved ledger. **NULL-`recipe_id` rows: 6/182 active SKUs + 146 ledger rows** → these CANNOT pool to a family → **fall back to the GLOBAL brewery seasonal curve** (same path as <2yr-history families). The 25% NULL-`sku_id_fk` rows can't even resolve a SKU → excluded from both S and L (coverage gap, surfaced not dropped).
- **physique = `fg_stock_compute()`** — already the numerator (`$physique`). No change.

### A. CRON + CACHE TABLE — BLESSED (revising the earlier "no cron / materialize only if slow")
The seasonal index `S` genuinely needs precompute: 52×family ratio-to-centered-MA decomposition over 44k rows, STABLE week-to-week, NOT render-cheap. **BLESS a new cache table + weekly cron. This stays SINGLE-HOMED = ONE burn path:** `S` is materialized by the cron, `L` is computed at render, the forward sim (render) consumes both — there is exactly one velocity derivation, no parallel store. Divergence-clean because S is a *materialized projection* of `inv_sales_ledger` (the SoT), recomputed wholesale each cron run (idempotent overwrite — no incremental drift), never hand-edited, never a second authority. This is the SAME materialization pattern already blessed for the daily-recap perf index — heavy stable analytic precomputed, render reads cache.
- **Table name (house convention `kpi_` prefix for materialized analytic caches): `kpi_sku_seasonal_index`.** Grain = ONE row per (family_recipe_id, iso_week 1..52) carrying the multiplicative index + a `is_global_fallback` flag for the brewery-wide curve (store the global curve as its own pseudo-family, e.g. `recipe_id=NULL`/sentinel row-set, so fallback is a lookup not a branch). Columns (sql agent finalizes): `recipe_id` (NULL=global curve), `iso_week` TINYINT, `seasonal_index` DECIMAL, `sample_years` / `n_obs` (provenance for the <2yr fallback decision), `computed_at`, plus a small `kpi_seasonal_index_meta` row OR a `computed_at` MAX read for freshness-chip. `schema_meta` row required (new table).
- **Cron:** weekly (S is stable; daily is wasteful). Wire as a maltyweb cron / scheduled PHP CLI, NOT a maltytask Node script (strangler: new compute homes in maltyweb+MySQL). Recompute wholesale, INSERT-fresh into a temp/swap or TRUNCATE+repopulate in one txn (idempotent). Emit a freshness timestamp so the render can show "indice saisonnier au {date}" and degrade gracefully (if cache empty/stale → fall back to the current flat-mean so the page NEVER hard-fails on a cold cache).
- **L stays at RENDER** (per the model): one indexed aggregate on `inv_sales_ledger(sku_id_fk, posting_date)` for the trailing 52 weeks + EW-mean in PHP. Cheap with the new composite index. This is the part that legitimately belongs in `fg_stock_compute()` Step 8.

### B. DERIVATION-TREE PLACEMENT
- **S (cached family seasonal shape)** = a NEW materialized leaf hanging off `inv_sales_ledger` (SoT) via the `sku_id_fk→ref_skus.recipe_id` family rollup. It is a projection, not a new fact. Upstream: `inv_sales_ledger` + `ref_skus.recipe_id`. Downstream: the forward sim only. It is NOT in the Le Zeppelin commissioning chain and NOT COGS/beer-tax-bearing (it's a demand-shape analytic, unit-counts only) — so it does not touch the SOT chain. Single canonical owner = the cron.
- **L (per-SKU level)** = render-time scalar, lives in `fg_stock_compute()` Step 8, owned by that function. Upstream: `inv_sales_ledger` (sku-grain) + `S` (to deseasonalize). Downstream: the sim.
- **Forward sim + semaines_restantes** = render-time, `fg_stock_compute()` Step 8, owned there. Upstream: `physique` (already computed) + `L` + `S`. Downstream: existing health-tier classification + chip + progress bars (unchanged seam).
- **Pooling collision check (resolved):** family=`ref_skus.recipe_id` does NOT collide with anything — it's the existing recipe-family key already used across the BOM/SKU tree. The ONLY friction is the NULLs (6 active SKUs + 146 ledger rows + the 25% unresolved-SKU rows) → all route to the global-curve fallback / coverage-gap surface; none silently corrupt a family aggregate.

### C. PHASING — AGREED (with one addition)
- **MVP** (delivers the CORRECT forward seasonal number): family seasonal index `kpi_sku_seasonal_index` + weekly cron + render-time `L` (EW λ=0.95, weeks-since-first-sale divisor for new SKUs) + forward depletion sim + net-of-returns (qty_out=−Σsigned_qty floored ≥0/week) + EOL "sans rotation" label + display triad (primary semaines_restantes + secondary "rythme de base" L + status chip with normal/provisoire). **Cold-cache graceful fallback to current flat-mean is part of MVP** (so the page can't 500 on an un-run cron). This is your MVP list — AGREED.
- **Fast-follow:** Croston's level for sporadique SKUs (ADI>1.32) + lead-time-relative bands (needs per-family `L_repl` data **Kouros must provide** — until then bands stay on the current absolute `WEEKS_*` constants) + overstock ceiling + threshold re-tune to forward semantics. **ADD to fast-follow:** the `kpi_sku_seasonal_index` **freshness-chip on the page** (same maltyweb-prefers-live discipline that's still open on the COP tiles — surface "indice au {date}", don't let a silently-stale cron pass as fresh). AGREED.

### D. MIGRATION / EQUIP / SEQUENCING / FLAGS
- **Migration number: `325` is the next free slot** (live-verified 2026-06-11: no `325_*` file local OR on VPS, absent from `schema_migrations`; 326/327 already applied — there is a GAP at 325). 328 also free if a second mig is needed. **RE-RUN `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` at build-start — parallel sessions live; the gap could be claimed.** One mig suffices: `325_kpi_sku_seasonal_index.sql` = CREATE TABLE `kpi_sku_seasonal_index` (+`schema_meta` row) + the composite index `ADD INDEX idx_sl_sku_posting (sku_id_fk, posting_date)` on `inv_sales_ledger` (INSTANT/INPLACE) + the `system_settings` param INSERTs (section e.g. `prevision_stock`). MySQL-8 syntax (no IF NOT EXISTS on ALTER, no bare SELECT).
- **PARAMS → `system_settings`** (the canonical central params table, NOT hardcoded): λ, season=52, horizon=104, clamp[0.2,4.0], ADI cutoff 1.32, EOL K=26wk, provisional thresholds (13wk/6 non-zero/full-summer), smoothing window=3, half-life. Shape fits: `section`/`key_name`/`value_num DECIMAL(10,4)`/`default_num`/`unit_fr`. Per-family `L_repl` lead-times = a SEPARATE keyed set Kouros provides (fast-follow) — likely `commissioning_settings` or a small `ref_*` per-family table, NOT `system_settings` scalars (it's per-family). NB `value_num` is DECIMAL(10,4) — fine for λ=0.95 and clamps.
- **EQUIP: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing.** sql owns mig 325 + the cron query + the composite-index plan + EXPLAIN on the 52wk render pull. coder owns the cron CLI + `fg_stock_compute()` Step-8 rewrite + cold-cache fallback. ui owns the display triad + chip + freshness label. webapp-testing = read-only `?view=stock` prod smoke (semaines renders, chip states, no 500 on cold cache).
- **DIVERGENCE FLAGS:** (i) **family JOIN, never string/name** — pool on `ref_skus.recipe_id` via FK JOIN, NEVER on beer-name (the match-on-recipe_id-not-beer-name rule). (ii) **single burn path** — S=cron-materialized, L=render; the sim must be the ONLY consumer; do NOT let the old flat-mean and the new engine BOTH feed `semaines_stock` except as the explicit cold-cache fallback. (iii) **NULL families → global curve, surfaced** — never silently drop the 6 NULL-recipe SKUs / 146 ledger rows / 25% unresolved-SKU rows; they go to the global fallback + a coverage-gap count, refuse-don't-NULL discipline. (iv) **not COGS/beer-tax** — unit-counts only; the cron must NOT touch `inv_consumption`/`ref_sku_bom`/CHF; it's a demand-shape analytic, outside the SOT chain. (v) **idempotent cron** — wholesale recompute/overwrite, no incremental accumulation that could drift S from the ledger. (vi) **cold-cache must degrade** — page renders (flat-mean fallback) when the cron hasn't run, never 500.

### D2. BURN-QUANTITY SEMANTICS — PM RULING 2026-06-11 (recon-driven; resolves 3 quantity-correctness forks the S&OP expert could not, having no BC-export visibility)
Live recon (2026-06-11): `inv_sales_ledger` 44,164 rows 2021-01-05→2026-06-09, 133 resolved SKUs, 25% NULL `sku_id_fk`. doc_type qty_signed sums: **shipment −1,080,057 (n=31257); invoice −753,202 (n=6309, SAME sign as shipment); credit +526,362 (n=6580, dominated by ±58,206 correction PAIRS w/ invoice); return_receipt +98 (n=18).** Columns: posting_date, doc_type ENUM(shipment/invoice/credit/return_receipt), sku_id_fk, qty_signed DEC(14,4), customer_id_fk, sales_amount_chf, hl_resolved. Composite (sku_id_fk,posting_date) idx CONFIRMED MISSING (two single-col idxs only) → mig 325 must add it.
- **🔴 RULING 1 — SHIPMENT-ONLY: SUPERSEDED FOR BURN 2026-06-11 (escalation-driven reversal; the verify-gate fired exactly as designed).** The original ruling (shipment-only, on a mirror-double-count hypothesis) was REVERSED when its own VERIFY-BEFORE-CODE clause (b) surfaced invoice-only goods-out. **Burn = −SUM(qty_signed) across ALL doc_types** (shipment+invoice outbound − ; credit+return_receipt back-in + ; net naturally via qty_signed sign). EVIDENCE (live re-verified 2026-06-11, sale_class×doc_type net −SUM): **eshop invoice 77,537 vs shipment 4,722 (94% of eshop goods-out is INVOICE-documented); taproom invoice 11,451, shipment 0 (100% invoice, ZERO shipment) → shipment-only DROPS taproom entirely + 94% of eshop.** Mirror hypothesis FALSIFIED: (i) `bc_source_no` is CUSTOMER-grained (~8 docs/source, 1064 distinct vs 8265 shipment docs) — the "252 shared source_no" = 252 customers using both flows, NOT per-order mirrors; (ii) each (doc_type, bc_line_seq) is a DISTINCT BC Item-Ledger movement — credits visibly net against shipments same-week, no shipment+invoice pair narrates one physical line; (iii) eshop literally migrated doc_type ERA (shipment-posting 2021 → invoice-posting later, same goods). The −/− sign agreement encodes DIRECTION (both outbound), not duplication. **b2b CONSISTENCY (make explicit so no one re-restricts b2b later): b2b also posts invoice +664,143 alongside shipment +1,072,632 — same doc_type-era migration, b2b-wide. The all-doc-type rule applies to b2b too; do NOT special-case b2b back to shipment-only.** SAFE DIRECTION: shipment-only under-counts burn on eshop/taproom-heavy SKUs → over-states weeks-remaining → false runway on the fastest-growing channels (the dangerous direction Kouros flagged). All-doc-type = honest/slightly-conservative runway. **Shipment-only REMAINS correct as the B2B-DISPLAY lens (mig-326 `v_sales_ledger_order_lines`, Commandes surface) — a legitimately different question (one-shipment-per-order-line for display); the two coexist by design. Do NOT point burn at that view.**
- **RULING 2 — channel scope = OPTION (a): ledger, ALL physical-stock sale_classes (incl. taproom + eshop where present), accept pre-2024 eshop-history gap as a NAMED FAST-FOLLOW (not MVP blocker).** [NB 2026-06-11: "shipment-only" qualifier here is OBSOLETE — RULING 1 reversed to all-doc-type; channel scope itself stands, now even more so since taproom/eshop are invoice-documented.] Rejected (b) eshop-splice from inv_sales_orders = a 2nd burn path across two stores/grains/temporal-seam → violates single-burn-path flag (ii). Rejected (c) strict-canonical B2B-only = OVER-states weeks-remaining on taproom/eshop-heavy SKUs (the dangerous direction: false runway on core beers). Burn universe must MATCH the `physique` numerator's depletion universe (b2b+taproom+eshop). Family-pooled S already absorbs eshop's seasonal shape wherever eshop hits the ledger; eshop-only L precision = fast-follow. VERIFY-BEFORE-CODE: `SELECT c.sale_class,l.doc_type,COUNT(*),ROUND(-SUM(l.qty_signed)),MIN/MAX(posting_date) FROM inv_sales_ledger l JOIN ref_customers c ON c.id=l.customer_id_fk GROUP BY 1,2` → proves which sale_classes/eshop are in the ledger + date-span → decides if eshop-splice fast-follow is even needed.
- **RULING 3 — sale_class universe = DENY-LIST `customs_artifact` ONLY (REFINED 2026-06-11 to what's actually in the ledger).** Filter = `sale_class IS NULL OR sale_class NOT IN ('customs_artifact')`. Live ledger sale_classes present: b2b, eshop, taproom, event, giveaway, staff, customs_artifact, + 1 NULL-customer shipment row. INCLUDE everything physical: b2b/taproom/eshop + giveaway/staff/event (each unit physically left FG stock = real depletion) + the NULL-customer row (+228, physical goods-out; NULL = coverage-gap to surface, refuse-don't-drop). EXCLUDE only customs_artifact (fiscal artifact; nets to 0 anyway, but exclude explicitly so a future non-zero customs row can't leak). **`transfer`/`sample` are NOT present in `inv_sales_ledger`** (they live elsewhere, operator-confirmed) → dropped from the deny-list to keep it honest to the table; if a transfer/sample row EVER appears in this ledger that's a schema surprise → ESCALATE, do NOT pre-emptively sweep it. ⚠️ sales-side `sale_class='giveaway'` is WHOLLY DISTINCT from `inv_side_stock_ledger movement_type='giveaway'` (mig 303) — burn reads the SALES ledger ONLY.
- **🔴 NET DERIVATION (one line, CORRECTED 2026-06-11):** Burn = **−SUM(qty_signed) over inv_sales_ledger WHERE sku_id_fk IS NOT NULL AND (sale_class IS NULL OR sale_class NOT IN ('customs_artifact'))** — **ALL doc_types** (shipment+invoice+credit+return_receipt net via sign) — floored ≥0/week, family-pooled sku_id_fk→ref_skus.id→recipe_id (S) / sku-grain (L). **DELIBERATE DIVERGENCE from `v_sales_ledger_order_lines`: that view is the B2B shipment-only DISPLAY lens; burn is all-doc-type all-physical-channel. DO NOT reuse the B2B view as the burn source — burn needs its own SELECT over the base table. Comment this in cron+Step-8 so a future reader doesn't "fix" the discrepancy by pointing burn at the view.** (Prior shipment-only NET DERIVATION superseded — see RULING 1.)
- **VERIFY-GATES — RESOLVED 2026-06-11 (the gate worked: R1(b) surfaced invoice-only goods-out → escalated → RULING 1 reversed).** R1 mirror-check: mirror hypothesis FALSIFIED (bc_source_no customer-grained, not order-mirror; doc_types are distinct Item-Ledger movements). R2 channel-presence: b2b/eshop/taproom/event/giveaway/staff + 1 NULL present; transfer/sample absent. R3 ENUM: deny-list narrowed to customs_artifact only. All three CLOSED — no remaining pre-code blocker on the burn-source leg. **EQUIP for the verify+burn-source leg: sql + coder** (ui+webapp-testing stay equipped for the render/smoke legs of the broader build).

## 🔑 D2 ECHO-FIELD RULING — credit-memo write-back (PM ruling 2026-06-15, BC-probe-backed)
**Context:** D2 (credit-memo write spine, disarmed, nothing committed) surfaced a surface-split conflict. The avoir (credit memo) entity is NOT on the OData v4 web-service surface D1 uses (`/ODataV4/.../SalesCreditMemo*` → 404). It lives ONLY on **BC API v2.0** (`/api/v2.0/companies(<uuid>)/salesCreditMemos`), where `Your_Reference` does NOT exist — the only filterable echo field is **`externalDocumentNumber`** (= `External_Document_No`), the field RESERVED in the D1 ruling for SalesOrders.

**LIVE BC PROBE (2026-06-15, read-only, NEBULEUSE company id `e2b691c6-8393-ed11-bff5-002248f307ee`):** 3,800 credit memos total; **155 (4%) have `externalDocumentNumber` populated**; sample values = free-text human refs (`RETOUR DOWTOWN LAUSANNE`, `COMMANDE 127596`, `CMD: N° 4031§`, `ERREUR QUANTITE`, bare invoice numbers). **ZERO start with `mt:`** → namespace collision-free. `$filter=externalDocumentNumber eq 'mt:cm:<n>'` confirmed OData-filterable → GET-before-create idempotency works.

**RULING (option 3 + 2a hybrid):**
1. `externalDocumentNumber='mt:cm:<order_id>'` is **ACCEPTABLE as the echo for CREDIT MEMOS** (NOT for sales orders — the D1 reservation stands unchanged on the OData SalesOrder surface). Three reasons: (a) the D1 reservation was framed around `External_Document_No` as KOUROS'S split-order key — that key lives on the SALES ORDER flow, not on credit memos; on the CM entity the field is a free-text human ref, sparsely used (4%), and our namespaced `mt:cm:` prefix is provably disjoint from every existing value AND from the order namespace `mt:` (bc_echo.py enforces the disjointness in code: `bc_echo_parse` returns None for `mt:cm:…`, `bc_cm_echo_parse` returns None for `mt:…`). (b) it is the ONLY filterable echo field on the v2.0 CM entity, so GET-before-create idempotency has no alternative anchor on the BC side. (c) namespacing makes accidental collision with a human-typed order ref structurally impossible.
2. **BUT the echo field is the SECONDARY idempotency guard, not the primary.** Primary = the `ord_bc_credit_memos` tracking table (mig 366): a local row keyed on the source order means "we already issued an avoir for this." The BC-side GET-before-create on `externalDocumentNumber eq 'mt:cm:<id>'` is the cross-process safety net (catches a tracking-table/BC divergence — e.g. tracking write failed after BC create). Both must agree before a CREATE; either one matching = skip-and-rekey, never double-issue. (This is option-2a's tracking-table idempotency layered UNDER option-3's namespaced echo — belt and suspenders, because a credit memo is financially irreversible.)
3. **SURFACE-SPLIT IS FINE — no reader/echo-loop problem.** The reader (`ingest_bc_sales_orders.py`) pulls ORDERS only and never pulls credit memos back; nothing in maltytask consumes the avoir on a later pull. So the CM "echo" exists SOLELY for GET-before-create idempotency, NOT a read-loop — which is exactly why the field choice is low-stakes (no downstream parser keys on it). The re-invoice (document #2) continues through D1's OData SalesOrder path with `Your_Reference='mt:<id>'`; the avoir (document #1) goes through API v2.0 with `externalDocumentNumber='mt:cm:<id>'`. Two surfaces, two disjoint namespaces, one tracking table — coherent. The ONLY thing that must hold: `bc_cm_echo_parse` must never be fed to the order reader and vice-versa (already structurally guaranteed by bc_echo.py).

**CONFIRMED UNCHANGED from prior D2 scope:** CREATE-only, NEVER POST/post (avoir + re-invoice stay in draft/unposted). Disarm = dry-run default + two-flag live (`--apply` AND `--i-have-kouros-go`) + NO cron. The COGS verification Opus owes BEFORE any write (the DGDF-wrong-vs-DGDB-right line depletes correctly) is STILL REQUIRED — run it as the rolled-back-txn probe, same discipline as D1's id=365 no-double-deplete check. Live proof = ONE synthetic fixture (create→verify→delete), NEVER the real already-invoiced Pepitium doc.

## 🆕 PER-ORDER DEPARTURE-SITE — TWO-TIER "learn-default + per-order exception" MODEL (P1 chip+override SHIPPED 2026-06-16; P2 learning-write PM-SCOPED, NOT built)

> ⚠️ **STATUS RECONCILED 2026-06-16 (was stale below "NOT built"):** P1 (board chip 📍auto/✎override + inline `<select>` + endpoint `public/api/expeditions-set-site.php` + JS `expeditions-set-site.js`) IS **SHIPPED** (repo files dated 06-16; chip render `expeditions.php` L4205-4225, resolver call L4103, board query carries `fulfilment_site_id_fk`+`customer_default_site_id` L1838-1840, fg_stock_compute consumes resolver Step 4 L451 + snapshot L1210). Endpoint writes ONLY `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk` + log_revision. The §BUILD SCOPE / DIVERGENCE FLAGS / EQUIP blocks BELOW describe P1 as-shipped (kept as the build record).

### THE REFINED TWO-TIER MODEL (Kouros verbatim intent, 2026-06-16) — P2 build target
**Tier 1 = customer's VALIDATED ship-from = `ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk`** (the durable client-fiche fact; vast majority = Zeubi/warehouse id2, correct). **Tier 2 = per-order one-off = `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk`** (exception for THIS order only, must NOT touch the customer default). **"maltytask n'invente pas":** a customer with NO validated default must be FLAGGED ⚠ à renseigner, not shown an invented site. The logistics operator's FIRST site-input on an order **auto-establishes the customer default** (learning write); subsequent orders pre-fill from it; per-order override is the exception layer on top; permanent change = edit the client fiche.

**LIVE DATA (probed 2026-06-16):** ord_orders site-overrides: import=71 (all site2/Zeubi, **62 of those customers have NO default**, 0 override==default), web=0, bc=0. Only **15 of 2665** active customers carry a `default_delivery_site_id_fk`. Sites holds_fg_stock: 1 Zgeg(production) / 2 Zeubi(warehouse) / 3 Taproom(pos) / 4 Nausikraft(consignment). `ref_customers` governance = **only `needs_review` tinyint** — NO draft/lock/verify gate on the master → cross-table write from the order endpoint to `default_delivery_site_id_fk` collides with NO ownership rule.

**A. RESOLVER 3rd UI STATE — NO depletion change.** `fg_stock_compute()` Step 4 (L451) + snapshot (L1210) call `resolve_fulfilment_site()` per order, which ALWAYS returns a non-zero site (warehouse fallback at the bottom) → stock math never breaks even with no customer default. The ⚠ "à renseigner" state is **pure UI**, derived from `customer_default_site_id IS NULL AND fulfilment_site_id_fk IS NULL AND order_type='customer'` (not eshop/taproom which have hard channel defaults). Warehouse STAYS the compute fallback; the flag is display-only, zero depletion impact. Eshop stays hard-wired warehouse (unchanged).

**B. THE LEARNING WRITE (core new behavior) — endpoint branch logic.** On operator pick via the inline control, the endpoint decides which column:
  - customer default IS NULL → write pick to **`ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk`** (establish validated site; order then resolves via customer default; per-order override stays NULL).
  - customer HAS default AND pick ≠ default → write **`ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk`** (per-order exception).
  - customer HAS default AND pick == default → clear any per-order override (no-op exception, set fulfilment_site_id_fk=NULL).
  - explicit "clear override" → set `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk=NULL` (back to auto).
  **Both writes log_revision (two audit targets: ref_customers AND ord_orders).** RECOMMENDED UX = **EXPLICIT intent, not pure inference** when establishing a default: when customer-default IS NULL, the control offers two confirmable actions — "définir comme défaut du client" (writes ref_customers, the expected path) vs "juste pour cette commande" (writes the per-order override even with no default). Inferring purely from default-presence is too magic for a COGS-adjacent location fact and gives the operator no escape hatch for a genuine one-off on a defaultless customer. When customer HAS a default, the control is the plain override (single action) + a clear-to-auto. Endpoint response must carry which table was written + the new resolved name + the new UI state so the chip re-renders 📍/✎/⚠ correctly.

**C. PERMANENT-CHANGE PATH — ALREADY SHIPPED.** No "Carnet clients" module exists; customer-master `default_delivery_site_id_fk` editing already lives at **`reglages-generaux.php?sec=delivery_sites`** (admin assign/remove, holds_fg_stock whitelist validation + log_revision, L890-957). This IS Kouros's "changement permanent" path — verified. P2 may add a convenience "Lieu de départ par défaut" dropdown to a per-customer fiche later, but the canonical write surface exists; do NOT build a parallel one.

**D. P2 BUILD PLAN (minimal diff atop shipped P1):** (1) endpoint `expeditions-set-site.php` — add branch logic (read customer default in the already-present order-fetch JOIN; route write to ref_customers vs ord_orders per B; second log_revision target); add an `intent` param ('default'|'order') for the explicit-UX when default IS NULL. (2) board chip — add the ⚠ "à renseigner" 3rd state (derive from the columns already in the board query L1838-1840; pure render). (3) JS — when chip is ⚠/defaultless, present the two-action choice; otherwise plain override+clear; consume the endpoint's table-written + state fields. **MIGRATION: NONE** (both columns exist). RULE 3: no ref_pages change → no tour card. RULE 1: nothing scrapped (additive on P1). **EQUIP: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing.** SMOKE: new-customer first-input writes the default (ref_customers row updated + order resolves 📍 via default, override stays NULL); 2nd order on that customer pre-fills 📍 auto; per-order override on a defaulted customer writes ord_orders ONLY (customer default untouched); clear-to-auto re-resolves; fiche edit at reglages changes the default. Both audit targets verified in audit_row_revisions.

**E. LEGACY 71 IMPORT-OVERRIDES — PM RECOMMENDATION = OPTIONAL dry-run migration, needs Kouros's OK (do NOT auto-run).** Under the two-tier model these 71 (all site2/Zeubi, source='import', from the retired WeeklyOrders importer) sit in the EXCEPTION column but are really "normal Zeubi" → they render ✎ (manual) when they should read 📍 (auto). Clean fix: for rows where `fulfilment_site_id_fk == would-be channel-default(warehouse=2) AND customer.default_delivery_site_id_fk IS NULL`, **move override→customer-default (set ref_customers.default=2) then clear ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk=NULL** → they read 📍 and the customer gains its validated default (which is correct — these clients DO ship from Zeubi). 62/71 qualify (no customer default). 🔴 **FG-ATTRIBUTION CAVEAT: clearing the override on a SHIPPED/historical order changes nothing in fg_stock attribution** because the resolver returns the SAME site (override 2 → now customer-default 2 → identical resolved id); Σ-by-site unchanged. Safe. The 9 non-qualifying rows (customer already has a default, or default≠2) stay as-is. **Kouros's stance = leave them; PM concurs leaving is acceptable** (majority Zeubi is correct, just mislabeled ✎). Offer the dry-run migration as a cosmetic+data-hygiene nicety only if the ✎/📍 mislabel bothers the operator. Dry-run first, count qualifying rows, Opus-verify resolver returns identical site pre/post before any apply.

**Ask (Kouros, original P1):** orders enter via BC→ord_orders cron (source='bc'), NOT the maltytask saisie form. On maltytask he wants (a) the resolved departure site VISIBLE per order on the Commandes board, and (b) an inline override (e.g. MKK normally Nausi → this time Crissier) usable directly on BC-sourced rows. ── P1 below as-shipped.
- **WHERE IT SITS:** override field `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk` (already exists, mig 290-era) → `resolve_fulfilment_site()` (`app/fulfilment-site.php`, THE single authority: override > `_customer_default_site_id`/`customer_id_fk`→`ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk` > channel-default warehouse/pos). Whitelist = `ref_sites WHERE holds_fg_stock=1 AND is_active=1` (the 4 sites). Downstream of the field: `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` site attribution. THIS IS THE SOT CHAIN — feature reuses it end-to-end, adds NO parallel store.
- **CURRENT DISPLAY STATE (code-verified 2026-06-16):** resolved site is **NOT** on the Commandes board. Board query (`expeditions.php` ~L1826) selects NO `fulfilment_site_id_fk` / `customer_id_fk` / customer-default-site, never calls the resolver; B2B row renderer (~L4122) renders chips for overdue/stock-risk/backorder/divergence/BC-shipped/lead-time but NO ship-from chip. AND source='bc'`. **`fulfilment_site_id_fk` is in NO BC write path** → a manually-set override SURVIVES every `*/15` re-pull.   - **(b) Inline override control:** new JSON endpoint `public/api/expeditions-set-site.php` — **direct clone of `public/api/expeditions-line-status.php`** (the proven sibling pattern): POST `{csrf, order_id, fulfilment_site_id_fk}`; guards = `require_login` + `require_page_access('expeditions')` + `can_write_expeditions($me)` 403 + `csrf_verify` (fresh-token echo); validate `order_id>0` + site_id ∈ holds_fg_stock whitelist OR =0/'' (= clear override → "Automatique", writes NULL); ONE txn: `UPDATE ord_orders SET fulfilment_site_id_fk=? WHERE id=?` + `log_revision`; respond `{ok, order_id, fulfilment_site_id_fk, resolved_site_name, is_override, csrf}` (recompute resolved name server-side so the chip re-renders correctly even when cleared-to-auto). Rationale: a commande = a delivery; credits/invoices are separate correction *documents* that cannot net *within* a document-grouped order and would clutter a browse view. **`allnet` stays the AUDIT-total basis** (the reconciliation report); **shipment-doc grain is the DISPLAY basis** for browsing past commandes. Both coexist cleanly — display ≠ audit, by design.

### ASK 1 — Tap-machine (T7) PICKUP orders must surface on the Commandes board ✅ SHIPPED
**AS BUILT (render-only, this session's expeditions.php change set):** eshop line render now reads `inv_sales_order_lines.title` (pill fallback `sku_code ?? title ?? '?'`) with a "matériel" badge when `sku_id_fk IS NULL` — 65× "Tireuse Portable" + 65× "Caution" now show readably instead of `?×1`. NO schema, NO ingest change, NO stock effect; T7 stays OUT of `ref_skus`. Playwright-smoke-verified. Pre-build probe below for provenance.
**LIVE-VERIFIED render behaviour (expeditions.php Commandes / `exp_render_eshop_row`):**
- Eshop order HEADER comes from `inv_sales_orders` (Query 3a, L1715) with **NO SKU-existence filter** → an order whose lines don't resolve to a SKU **IS shown** (header, customer, 🏬/🚚/⚠ badge, Shopify tag). The order is NOT dropped.
- Lines (Query 3b, L1733) = `inv_sales_order_lines isol LEFT JOIN ref_skus s` → NULL `sku_id_fk` keeps the row; render pill = **`isol.sku_code` (raw), falling back to `'?'`** when `sku_code` itself is NULL; family colour = `exp_format_family('')` (NULL `s.format`). **The line is shown but uninformative.**
- 🔑 **ROOT GAP (the load-bearing finding):** the ingest (`scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts` L317) maps **Shopify's SKU field → `sku_code`** and the **line TITLE → a SEPARATE `title` column** (L327). Tap-machine lines have a BLANK Shopify SKU → `sku_code=NULL` → render as bare **`?×1`**, EVEN THOUGH the descriptive `title` ("Tireuse Portable", "Caution") IS persisted in `inv_sales_order_lines.title` — **the render NEVER reads `title`.** Live: 65× "Tireuse Portable" + 65× "Caution" + Gobelets/Pack-de-Noël/Beer-des-Rosses/Carte-cadeau all sit in `title` with `sku_code=NULL` (263 NULL-sku lines / 2646 qty total). **NO order carries a "Tireuse"/"TAP"/"T7" sku_code** — they are ALL title-only.
- **DERIVATION-CORRECT FIX (no phantom SKU, no stock touch):** render pill fallback chain = `sku_code ?? title ?? '?'`; when `sku_id_fk IS NULL` add a **"non-stock / matériel" badge** on the pill (greyed, distinct from beer families). T7 stays OUT of `ref_skus` (correct — it's non-stock equipment), so it never enters `fg_stock_compute()` and never depletes. This is RENDER-ONLY (expeditions.php + .css), NO mig, NO ingest change (title already captured). The Phase-3c `ref_skus.is_non_stock` flag (mig 323) is INERT here — it only matters for SKUs that EXIST in ref_skus; T7 isn't one, so the discriminator is simply "`sku_id_fk IS NULL` → non-stock line". Reuse that predicate, don't invent a parallel flag.
- **Re "③ tap machine soon integrated as Shopify sales":** that note is the SALES/COGS lane (does a tap-machine sale post revenue / become a sellable line), NOT FG-stock. It does NOT change the fulfilment surface: even if T7 becomes a revenue line later, it stays NON-STOCK equipment (no liquid/packaging BOM, no FG depletion). Fulfilment-only display is the right scope now; a sellable-T7 path is a separate later question (would touch `inv_sales_ledger` sale_class + possibly a non-FG `ref_*` equipment catalog, NOT `ref_skus` inventory). Surface for fulfilment now; do NOT pre-build a sellable path.
- **VERDICT: BUILD (no Kouros decision needed) — render-only, SOT-safe, no phantom SKU, no depletion.** Only judgement call = the badge label ("matériel" vs "non-stock" vs "retrait matériel") — a copy choice, fine to pick + show Kouros. **EQUIP: ui + coder + webapp-testing** (sql NOT needed — zero schema/query change; the `title` column is already selected if we add it to Query 3b, which is a one-column add, still no schema). NB: add `isol.title` to the Query-3b SELECT (it's not currently selected) — that's the only backend touch.

Pre-build probe below for provenance.

> ✅ **SHOPIFY INGEST CADENCE BUMP `*/15`→`*/1` + flock — SHIPPED+VERIFIED LIVE 2026-06-17 (PM-approved earlier same day; mirrors the BC-orders `*/1` ruling at line ~1061).** `db/cron/maltytask-shopify-ingest.cron`: cadence `*/15`→`*/1`, command WRAPPED in `flock -n /tmp/maltytask-shopify-ingest.lock bash -c '…'` (flock execs bash DIRECTLY — no nested `-c` quote collision; `HOME`/`NVM_DIR` exported explicitly INSIDE the `bash -c` since the cron env is bare; comment block updated mirroring the bc-orders cron). 🔴 **MANDATORY flock single-flight reasoning (same as BC-orders `*/1`): at 1-min cadence a slow run (token refresh + 2-day trailing window) can exceed 60s → two ingests race the same line-`row_hash` UPSERT; `-n` skips if a run is still going, next minute catches up.** Idempotency already proven (line `row_hash` UNIQUE + `INSERT IGNORE`, header upsert keyed `(source, external_order_id)`) so flock is belt-and-braces, not the sole guard. **Committed maltyweb `cdb19a5` (SINGLE file by pathspec — the dirty parallel-session files expeditions.php/kpi-handlers.php/mig392 were NOT swept in; pathspec-commit discipline honored). NOT pushed yet.** **Deployed SURGICALLY** (scp + `sudo install -m 0644 -o root -g root` → `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-shopify-ingest`) because the shared tree was dirty under a parallel session — did NOT run `bin/deploy.sh --apply` (would have pushed the foreign dirty tree). **VERIFIED LIVE:** cron RELOAD logged 08:38 UTC, fires every minute (08:38/08:39/08:40) each with the new flock command; `/var/log/maltytask/shopify-ingest.log` updates each cycle; exact-command-shape dry-run succeeded first. **🔴 STILL-OPEN follow-up (PM-flagged, NOT done): the "Dernier import Shopify" freshness chip threshold is HARDCODED 90 min** (`expeditions.php` ~L4527) — too loose at 1-min cadence (90 min stale would mean ~90 missed runs before the chip even ambers). **PM rec = tighten to ~10–15 min AND move it into `system_settings 'fulfilment'`** (do NOT re-hardcode a new literal — same never-hardcode-a-threshold discipline as the lead-time `order_lead_time_*` keys already in that section). Left for a SEPARATE edit once 1-min cadence is proven stable. EQUIP for the chip follow-up: ui + coder + sql (settings key) + webapp-testing.

> ✅✅ **SHOPIFY IMPORT DATA-LOSS BUG FIXED + LIVE 2026-06-17 (maltytask `665b335`, PUSHED).** Operator's "l'import shopify ne marche pas" was a REAL data-loss bug, not just cron cadence. ROOT CAUSE `scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts` (deployed `/opt/maltytask-pipeline`): Shopify Orders API `created_at_max=${UNTIL}T00:00:00Z` where UNTIL defaulted to TODAY → upper bound = today **00:00 UTC** → **every order created during the current day silently excluded** (Mon/Tue fine because yesterday's orders land next day; the board showed only Mon+Tue). Confirmed 8 orders today on Shopify, 0 in `inv_sales_orders` pre-fix. FIX: default upper bound now = current INSTANT (full ISO timestamp, L60/L67); explicit `--until DATE` now includes the WHOLE named day (`T23:59:59Z`). Deployed surgically to `/opt/maltytask-pipeline/scripts/` (md5 parity, owner maltytask:www-data 644); live-ran to backfill today's 8 (#13638–#13645). `*/1` cron keeps today current near-real-time. maltyweb hotfix `6995146` (eshop hoist) + cron `cdb19a5` CONFIRMED on origin/main (auto-sync pushed). **🔴 DURABLE BUG CLASS — "same-day exclusion via midnight-truncated upper bound": any date-window ingest whose `*_max`/`until` defaults to TODAY's date and gets coerced to `T00:00:00` silently drops the whole current day. Default upper bounds to the current INSTANT; explicit single-day windows must span `T23:59:59`. Check this FIRST when an importer 'misses recent rows'.**

> 🟢🟢 **FRESHNESS-CHIP HEARTBEAT — PM RULED 2026-06-17 (endorse heartbeat, REJECT naive threshold-tighten). PENDING BUILD.** The chip's `$isStale` keys on `MAX(imported_at)` (channel='eshop'), and `imported_at` is `DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP` → advances ONLY on INSERT → it measures "time since last NEW order", NOT "time since last successful poll". Naively tightening 90→10-15 min would make the chip cry wolf every quiet eshop night (no new orders for hours → amber while the `*/1` poller is healthy) — strictly WORSE; trains the operator to ignore it. **RULING: make the chip a POLLER HEARTBEAT, decoupled from order recency.** (1) `ingest-shopify-orders.ts` UPSERTs a heartbeat on EVERY successful LIVE run (even 0-insert) at the END of `main()`, inside the `!DRY_RUN` guard (a mid-run throw leaves it stale → correct amber; dry-run must NOT write). (2) Heartbeat home = `system_settings` (NOT a new `ops_*` table — single last-writer-wins scalar, settings-row weight is right): **`section='fulfilment'`, `key_name='shopify_ingest_last_run_at'`, written to `value_text`** (datetime string), `is_active=1`, `description_fr` noting "écrit automatiquement — ne pas modifier" (NOT operator-editable, NOT surfaced on Données générales). 🔴 LIVE SCHEMA NOTE: `system_settings` keys on `(section, key_name)`, NO `scope` column; value in `value_num`/`value_text`. (3) STALE THRESHOLD is the operator-tunable knob, ALSO in system_settings: **`section='fulfilment'`, `key_name='shopify_ingest_stale_minutes'`, `value_num=10`, `unit_fr='min'`** — editable on Données générales (real operational threshold, same class as `order_lead_time_*`). Read with `?? default THEN validate`, clamp to a sane floor (a 0 must not pin the chip amber). (4) Chip: `$isStale = (NOW − heartbeat) > stale_minutes`; **null heartbeat (pre-first-run) → NEUTRAL, not amber**; keep `MAX(imported_at)` as INFORMATIONAL "dernière commande HH:MM" text only — no longer drives amber. THRESHOLD = **10 min** (cron `*/1`, tolerates ~9 consecutive misses before alarming — separates hiccup from dead poller; 5 too twitchy). Existing chip markup/CSS already present → no `ui` build, logic+settings+smoke only. SEQ: mig (seed 2 settings rows; MIG HEAD 392→next free 393, re-`--status` at build-start, parallel sessions live) → ingest heartbeat UPSERT (deploy surgically to `/opt/maltytask-pipeline/scripts/`, md5 parity, owner maltytask:www-data 644; `php`/tsx not `php8.1 -l`) → expeditions.php chip read both keys (`php8.1 -l` the DEPLOYED file before php-fpm reload) → webapp-testing prod-readonly smoke 3 states: fresh→green / aged-heartbeat→amber / quiet-night (old imported_at + fresh heartbeat)→GREEN. **EQUIP: coder + sql + webapp-testing** (NO ui — chip already rendered).

**LIVE-VERIFIED cadence/host (pre-build probe — now superseded by the VPS rehome above):** ingest is a **`*/15` USER-CRONTAB job on the LOCAL WSL box** (`crontab -l`: `flock -n /tmp/shopify-ingest.lock npx tsx scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts --since $(date -d "2 days ago")`), writing to MySQL **over a manually-established SSH tunnel on 13306** (`ssh -f -N -L 13306:... maltyweb`, ServerAliveInterval=30). BOTH cron AND tunnel are local-box-resident = the exact fragility recorded (memory was right). It already runs every 15 min, so "several times a day" is ALREADY met IF the box+tunnel are up.
- **The real thing to fix is NOT frequency — it's the host/transport fragility.** Bumping frequency on a local-box/tunnel cron buys nothing; the failure mode is "WSL asleep / tunnel dropped → board silently stale," not "not frequent enough." **DERIVATION-CORRECT TARGET: move the ingest to the VPS** (where MySQL is local, no tunnel) as a real `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-shopify-ingest` entry — same strangler discipline as the recipe-profile + seasonal-index crons (compute homes on the VPS). Cadence on the VPS: every 15–30 min is fine ("several times a day" satisfied with margin). Secrets: `secrets/shopify.env` must land on the VPS (not committed). Runtime: `npx tsx` exists where the maltytask repo is — confirm the repo (or just the script + lib) is deployable to the VPS, or wrap as a maltyweb PHP CLI that shells the existing TS (prefer keeping the TS, just rehome the cron).
- **Idempotency: SAFE to run more often.** Line-level `row_hash = sha256("shopify|order|line|sku|qty")` UNIQUE + `INSERT IGNORE` (L321/L503-553); header upsert keyed on `(source, external_order_id)` with a real UPDATE branch (L447-472). The earlier line-idempotency bug (recorded in §0a11 Phase 0) is FIXED. Re-running over an overlapping `--since` window = no-op on unchanged rows, UPDATE on changed status. No double-ingest concern.
- **VERDICT: small Kouros decision, then BUILD.** The build (rehome cron to VPS) is sound + low-risk, but it needs (a) Kouros OK to install a VPS cron + put `shopify.env` on the VPS, and (b) confirming the maltytask repo/script is present/deployable on the VPS (today the ingest only runs from the local clone). If Kouros would rather NOT put the Node toolchain on the VPS, fallback = harden the local path (autossh + a cron-health/freshness chip on the board surfacing "dernier import Shopify: {time}" so staleness is VISIBLE — same maltyweb-prefers-live discipline as the COP/seasonal freshness-chip debt). **PM rec: VPS-rehome is the clean target; the freshness-chip is worth doing EITHER WAY** (so a stalled ingest can't masquerade as "no new orders"). **EQUIP: coder + sql** (cron/CLI + host migration) **+ ui + webapp-testing** if the freshness-chip is included.

## 2026-06-08 — TASK #10 Stock PF board: PM ANCHOR+FLOW MODEL RULING (PRE-BUILD; resolves R4)
PM ruling delivered to orchestrator before delegating the Stock PF rebuild. Live state confirmed: loc1 = 41 April (`month_closed='2026-04'`) + **4 June** (06-08) rows; loc2 = 28 June; loc4 = 26 June; loc3 (Taproom) EMPTY (counted 06-09). Model P in force (global-pool depletion, no per-order/per-production location tag).

**THE LOAD-BEARING CALLS (canonical):**
1. **Per-location CARD = that location's latest-count-DATE snapshot only.** loc1 Production card shows the **4 June SKUs, NOT the 37 April-only leftovers** (pre-split bootstrap; a fresh full physical is a complete statement of what's standing there). Card query: per (sku, location) take rows where `counted_at = MAX(counted_at) for that location`. **Do NOT delete/tombstone the 37 April rows** — card *visibility* ≠ anchor *membership* (see #3).
2. **Cards STATIC (frozen Monday snapshot) / TOTAL LIVE.** `TOTAL physique = Σ_loc(latest-count qty) + global production since anchor − global shipments/eshop/taproom since anchor`. The Σ-anchor term and the flow window MUST be the same count rows. The 2 derived lines (−semaine-open, −all-open) come off the live TOTAL only. Orders are global (no location tag) → subtract from TOTAL, never from a card.
3. **🔴 R4 RESOLVED — anchor is PER (sku) = SKU's latest count across all locations, NOT one global `MAX(month_closed)`.** The current `fg_stock_compute()` does global `MAX(month_closed)` → picks `2026-06` → **silently ZEROES the 37 loc1 April-only SKUs** (no June row → anchor 0). THAT is the concrete R4 bug. Correct model: `anchor_qty(sku) = Σ_loc(qty at that loc's latest count of that sku)`; `flow_window_start(sku) = MAX(counted_at) over the rows feeding that anchor`. SKUs only in April bootstrap anchor on April + deplete by prod/ship since April (NOT zeroed); SKUs counted 06-08 anchor on June. Staggered counts (Taproom 06-09) advance per-SKU automatically. **This per-SKU anchor fix is a CORRECTNESS fix to fg_stock_compute() independent of the board — do it regardless.** "Stop showing April on the Production card" ≠ "stop summing April into the anchor".
4. **Taproom empty → graceful-zero** ("pas encore compté", contributes 0, NEVER blocks). Its SKUs anchor on whatever other location last counted them (or April) until 06-09.

**ARCHITECTURE (B): two functions, clean split.** Keep `fg_stock_compute()` GLOBAL for TOTAL + derived lines + per-SKU live table (**but fix to per-SKU anchor model #3**). ### ✅ PF-STOCK BUILD — FULL-BOX FLOORING + PER-LOCATION PRODUCTION ATTRIBUTION SHIPPED 2026-06-09 (committed `d71d890`, pushed, live; NO migration — data + PHP: `app/fg-stock.php` + `public/modules/expeditions.php`; EQUIP coder+sql+ui +webapp-testing)
**Built per the design we consulted; supersedes the `566b9d3` production-leg fix with the operator's full-box PF rule + per-location production crediting. No mig (data + PHP).**

1. **FULL-BOX FLOORING (operator PF rule).** production = `SUM(FLOOR(prod_total_units / units_per_pack))` — floored **PER EVENT then summed** (NOT sum-then-floor). **Operator rule: PF = full boxes only; loose units from a partial run are NOT PF** — they are the future "mini side-stock" (item E below). DIV4 9901 → **412 boxes** (was 412.54). kegs/cuv `units_per_pack=1` → floor is a no-op. `prod_qty` + `physique` are now INTEGERS.
2. **PER-LOCATION PRODUCTION ATTRIBUTION.** `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` now credits floored production-since-prod-site-count to the **production-site card** (DB-derived `site_type='production'`, gated by `$isProdSite`). Renens DIV4: 37 count → **449** (37 + 412). Other sites are anchor-only. **New invariant: Σ(locations) == physique when sales=0** (verified 449+39+23 = 511).
3. **SINGLE-SOURCED (drift-proof — the Q2 requirement).** New private helper **`fg_prod_since_anchor(PDO, $globalAnchor)`** returns `{prod_site_ids, by_sku:{prod_qty:int, prod_events:int}}`; **BOTH `fg_stock_compute()` AND the snapshot call it**, so the SKU-total card and the per-location card cannot drift.
4. **INTEGER DISPLAY (Q5 #4).** unit/box columns render 0-decimals; **HL stays decimal**.
5. **STOCK ORDER.** `$stockFamilyOrder` now **Keg → Bot → Can → Can33 → multipack → Cuve**; single-unit SKUs (`sku_code` suffix `/(BU|CU)$/`, taproom-only) bucketed into **"À l'unité (taproom)" rendered LAST**. Applied to total table, filter chips, AND per-location snapshot grouping.

**Q1 verdict held: NO new setting, NO `receives_packaging` column — `site_type='production'` remains the single SoT.**

**✅ ITEM 2 / item E — MINI SIDE-STOCK / GIVEAWAYS TRACKER — SHIPPED + PUSHED 2026-06-10 (maltyweb `1c95e23` on origin/main; mig 303; UNIT-COUNTS ONLY, NEVER COGS).** Packaging loose-unit remainder = `bd_packaging_v2.prod_total_units MOD ref_skus.units_per_pack`. Lives between `bd_packaging_v2` and beer-tax. As-built:
- **mig 303 `inv_side_stock_ledger`** — append-only, tombstone-only, `table_class='source'`, `corrections_policy='allowed'`. Per-SKU keyed (`sku_id_fk` INT UNSIGNED FK→`ref_skus` RESTRICT). `movement_type` ENUM(`accrual`+ / `complete_box`− / `giveaway`− / `year_end_offered`− / `adjustment`±) with enforced `chk_ssl_sign`. `bd_packaging_id_fk` BIGINT UNSIGNED FK→`bd_packaging_v2` SET NULL. `fiscal_year` CHAR(4). `submitted_by_user_fk` FK→`users` SET NULL.
- **DEVIATION (recorded):** `accrual_key` is a PLAIN nullable VARCHAR(48) written by PHP (`"$bdPkgId:$skuId"`), NOT a STORED generated column — MySQL 8.0.46 returns err 1215 when ALTER-adding a STORED generated col whose expr references a FK column that has ON DELETE SET NULL (`bd_packaging_id_fk`). `uq_ssl_accrual` UNIQUE on it gives idempotency (NULLs don't collide). *(Generalizes the mig-288/mig-292 generated-column lessons — here the SET-NULL FK was the blocker, not the FK type.)*
- **DISTINCTNESS (critical):** this is the PACKAGING-remainder fact, wholly distinct from the SALES-side `sale_class='giveaway'` (migs 300/301, sales-commercial-surface arc). NOT COGS (unit counts only; never `inv_consumption` / `ref_sku_bom` / CHF). Production-site-homed. OUT of `fg_stock_compute()` FG legs — `app/fg-stock.php` byte-unchanged (verified).
- **Writer (`form-packaging.php`):** accrual banked per-format row, hung off the per-format `resolve_packaging_sku_id()` result `$rSpec['sku_id_fk']` → **mig-265-safe parallel -4/-B attribution** (each leg shares session recipe_id, differs by format_suffix → own SKU). `complete-a-box` draw field (`side_stock_complete_box`) with refuse-don't-NULL balance check (French error, rollBack). `units_per_pack=1` (keg/cuv) → remainder 0 → no accrual.
- **Re-save / edit idempotency = TOMBSTONE-PRIOR-THEN-REINSERT** (caught + fixed on RULE-2 review; first build had 3 lifecycle bugs): on every packaging-row write, prior live `accrual`+`complete_box` rows for that `bd_packaging_id_fk` are tombstoned + `accrual_key` NULLed, then fresh rows inserted. Fixes: complete_box no longer double-inserts on edit; accrual qty updates when prod_total edited; tombstone frees the key. `giveaway`/`year_end_offered`/`adjustment` rows UNTOUCHED (distinct real-world events, not run-derived).
- **Surface (`expeditions.php ?view=side-stock`):** per-SKU live balances + ledger breakdown; operator giveaway entry (CSRF + balance-checked refuse-don't-NULL); admin tombstone (CSRF + `is_admin` gated; UPDATE sets `accrual_key=NULL` + `log_revision`); 60s live-refresh JS (maltyweb-prefers-live-visibility canon). CSS in `/public/css/`, JS in `/public/js/`.
- **Operator decisions baked in:** per-SKU keying; giveaways accumulate + settle year-end; parallel-run attribution.
- **Verification:** 22 assertions incl. full A–F edit lifecycle (B no double-insert on re-save; C accrual qty updates; F tombstone re-bank); render-smoke 302 (not 500); idempotency confirmed; clean tree.
- **🔴 OPEN DOWNSTREAM (the remaining Item 2 work) = YEAR-END-SETTLE CRON, DOCUMENTED-NOT-BUILT.** Beer-tax hook inline-JOIN shape recorded in mig 303: `SELECT sku_id_fk, SUM(qty_units) FROM inv_side_stock_ledger WHERE movement_type='year_end_offered' AND fiscal_year=? AND is_tombstoned=0` → units→HL via `ref_skus.hl_per_unit`. No-double-count rationale included (accruals untaxed; `complete_box`→FG via normal path; giveaways net into year-end residual, taxed once). NOT YET BUILT: a year-end-close cron that WRITES the `year_end_offered` draws + feeds beer-tax. **Canonical balance: Σ(prod MOD upp) − Σ(complete_box) − Σ(giveaway) − Σ(year_end_offered) ± Σ(adjustment).**

### ✅ FG-STOCK CARRY-OVER FIX — PER-LOCATION CENSUS-DATE ANCHOR SHIPPED + LIVE 2026-06-16 (maltyweb `5b9858e`, pushed to origin/main; read-fix, NO mig, NO schema change, NO correction rows; EQUIP sql+coder)
**SUPERSEDES the anchor key documented in §TASK #10 (line ~282) — the per-`(sku_id_fk, location_id_fk)` latest-COUNT anchor (`ROW_NUMBER() OVER (… ORDER BY counted_at DESC)`, i.e. each SKU carries forward its own last count regardless of date) is REPLACED by a per-LOCATION latest-CENSUS-DATE anchor.**

🔴 **DURABLE DERIVATION RULE (operator-confirmed verbatim intent):** *"We NEVER carry over stock. Every stocktake is a COMPLETE census of a location. If a SKU isn't in the latest stocktake at a location, it's 0 there."* → The anchor keys on **each location's latest census DATE (any `count_type`)**; a SKU absent from that location's latest census = **0** at that location; a SKU's value is NEVER carried across census dates. This is now the canonical FG-stock anchor semantics.

- **WHAT (`app/fg-stock.php`):** the new per-location census-date anchor is applied **IDENTICALLY to all 4 anchor windows** to preserve the **Σcards==Σphysique** invariant: (1) `fg_stock_compute()` Step 1; (2) `fg_stock_location_snapshot()`; (3) `fg_site_sku_anchor_map()`; (4) the production-cutoff `pa` subquery in `fg_prod_since_anchor()` — cutoff = the production site's census date (sku-independent), `prod_anchor_ts` set NULL → the same-day `submitted_at` tiebreak is disabled (conservative).
- **🔴 `count_type` is DELIBERATELY NOT FILTERED on the board** — a `month_end` census IS a complete census and must be allowed to be the freshest anchor. This **REVERSED my own earlier ruling** (I had said hard-filter the board to `count_type='operational'`); Kouros flagged that filtering `month_end` would HIDE the freshest full count on month-close day = a new misread. Resolution: **`month_end` is a COGS-only SUPER-TAG, invisible to the board's anchor logic.**
- **COGS ISOLATION (Opus-verified, the divergence guard):** `_cogs_fg_compute()` in `app/cogs-fiche-compute.php` reads a SEPARATE path doubly-pinned `WHERE month_closed=? AND count_type='month_end'` (likewise the basis-adjustment compute). A weekly **operational** count CANNOT leak into a month's COGS even while unsealed — blocked on BOTH `count_type` AND `month_closed` (derived from `counted_at`, so a July count stamps `2026-07`). Saisie defaults `count_type='operational'` (`expeditions.php:737`; only the `month_end_census` checkbox sets `month_end`). `row_hash=sha256("fgct|{sku}|{loc}|{counted_at}")` → one count per sku/loc/day (upsert), so no same-day rival rows.
- **BLAST RADIUS (the bug being fixed):** 16 phantom carried cells across all 4 sites. Symptom = DIVF (Diversion keg, sku 17) showed 35 at Renens (site 1 production) carried from the 05-31 `month_end` census; physically 0. Total live FG overstated **7797→6972 units (−825** = 540 stale anchors + ~285 phantom production piled on the stale dates). Group A (month_end leak, site1): MOO4C 130 / STIF 110 / EPH4B 70 / DIVF 35 / ZEP4 4. Group B (operational carry-over): site1 ZEPB 15/DOAF 8/SPYB 5/DOA4 1; site3/Taproom PD8 110/EPH4BU 30/ESTBU 12/DIBB 2/DGDF 1/DOAF 1; site4 DIVF 6.
- **OPUS-VERIFIED read-only on live (own harness, not the agent's word):** DIVF Renens 35→0 (site2=10 real unchanged, site4 6→0); anchor rows 136→120 (**exactly the 16 removed, 0 added**); every legitimately-counted SKU byte-unchanged; COGS path untouched. NO schema change, NO migration, NO correction rows — the read-fix zeroes phantoms by construction, so Kouros's earlier "explicit 0 rows" decision became UNNECESSARY.
- **KNOWN PRE-EXISTING (NOT introduced, NOT in scope):** Σcards==Σphysique still carries a **−2 gap from cage SKUs DIVX/EMBX** (compute=1 vs snapshot=0) — IDENTICAL in baseline and fixed. This is the cage-attribution rounding (relates to the Shopify arc's noted ~22-unit FG gap), separate from this carry-over bug.
- **SITES (canonical labels):** id1 "Zgeg (Production)" = Renens; id2 "Zeubi (Logistique)" = warehouse; id3 Taproom; id4 Nausikraft consignment.
- **FOLLOW-UPS: none required.** Optional future: a saisie UI affordance making the `month_end` checkbox explicit; the cage −2 gap cleanup (separate).

**STILL-OPEN CARRYOVERS:** sales-leg per-location settlement (stock-movement-saisie arc). **⛔ NO DATE→DATETIME migration to do — REDUNDANT, do NOT dispatch one.** Same-day settlement is ALREADY fully solved with NO migration: prod-leg via Option-2 tiebreak (`d3fb954`), and ESHOP + cross-site TRANSFER legs via **Task A** (`2192153`, 2026-06-10, `app/fg-stock.php`, NO mig). Mechanism = the EXISTING `inv_fg_stocktake.created_at` (already a `timestamp` — live-verified 2026-06-10; `counted_at` STAYS `date` = business truth) used purely as the same-day tiebreak. The only same-day gaps that REMAIN are **B2B** (no ship-time finer than `requested_date`) and **taproom** (month-grained period). Nothing is gated on the Mon 2026-06-15 cage count for this — the cage count just lands an anchor. **🔴 CORRECTION 2026-06-10: the B2B gap is NOT "intentional/safe" — it is a REAL computation bug (global anchorDate pollution drops legitimate same-day ships); reclassified + ruled in §B2B EXPEDIE LEG = REAL COMPUTATION BUG below. The taproom month-grained gap is still genuinely deferred.**

### ✅ TWO PF-STOCK FIXES SHIPPED 2026-06-09 (committed + pushed + deployed; outage fix `ae297c2`, production-leg fix `566b9d3`; EQUIP coder+sql)
**Both on origin/main (afe1dcd..566b9d3), deployed (selective rsync + chown www-data). No migration — data + PHP only.**

1. **Expéditions OUTAGE FIX (`ae297c2`) — 500 on the whole PF-stock page.** `exp_dow_fr()` (the French-weekday helper added in `afe1dcd`, the fresh-chip feature, an earlier same-day session) was defined NESTED inside the stocktake render function → undefined at the EARLIER call site (~L2824, the "✓ compté" fresh-chip branch). PHP nested function defs are **runtime-declared in call order**, so a helper used before its (later) nested definition fatals. That branch only fires when a count EXISTS this week → today's stocktake tripped "Call to undefined function exp_dow_fr()" → 500. **Fix: hoisted `exp_dow_fr` to the top-level date-helper section** (compile-time hoisted; also kills a latent cannot-redeclare on double render). **DURABLE LESSON: keep page helpers TOP-LEVEL — never nest a helper inside a render function if any earlier code path may call it.** (Convention candidate for the `coder`/`ui` skill if it recurs.)

2. **`fg_stock_compute()` PRODUCTION-LEG FIX (`566b9d3`) — partial count poisoned the global cutoff, dropped same-day production.** The bug PM predicted: R4 anchor SUM is per-(sku, location) but the flow windows still ran off a single global `$anchorDate`. A partial count (today: Taproom/pos-site only, 2026-06-09) advanced the global cutoff → same-day production-site packaging vanished from physique (DIV4 9901 btl, DIVB 2592 btl invisible). **Fix applied exactly as consulted:**
   - **Production site id(s) DB-derived** from `ref_sites WHERE site_type='production' AND is_active=1` (id=1 Zgeg/Renens today; **set-valued, no hardcode**).
   - **Per-SKU production cutoff = MAX(counted_at) for that SKU at the production site(s)**; `COALESCE` fallback to global `$anchorDate` for SKUs never counted there.
   - **`run_type='cuv'` EXCLUDED from the prod leg** (cuve-de-service = filled-at-client = sold, never FG stock). Three independent guards make cuv SKUs (EMBV/MOOV/ZEPV) vanish from the computed FG table with no negatives: cuv has no anchor + no `ord_order_lines` depletion path + `stocktake_scope='none'`.
   - **Sales legs (expedie/eshop/taproom) STILL on the global cutoff** — per-location settlement DEFERRED to the stock-movement-saisie arc; documented inline with a SCOPE NOTE near `$anchorDate` (prod-fixed ≠ all-fixed; taproom period>anchorMonth can exclude the current month on partial-count days).
   - **Verified live (www-data probe):** DIV4 prod_qty=412.54 (9901/24), DIVB=108 (2592/24), ZEPV absent; non-production-anchored SKUs (DIB4/DIVF/EPH4B) compute prod_qty=0, no crash.

**DURABLE — packaging-inflow site model:** packaging inflow ALWAYS lands at the **production site (Renens, DB-derived)**. Inter-site moves (Renens→Crissier→Nausikraft→Taproom) = the future **stock-movement saisie arc** (NOT built). `ref_sites` today: id1 Zgeg/Renens (production, holds_fg), id2 Zeubi/Crissier (warehouse, holds_fg), id3 Taproom/Renens (pos, holds_fg), id4 Nausikraft (consignment, holds_fg, customer_id_fk=1).

**OPEN / DEFERRED (flag at stock-movement-saisie arc):**
- **Sales-leg per-location settlement** — expedie/eshop/taproom legs still use the global `$anchorDate`; per-location settlement deferred to the stock-movement saisie arc (the prod leg is now per-SKU-per-site; the sales legs are NOT). Documented inline as a SCOPE NOTE.
- **Same-day count+package edge — `counted_at` is a DATE with strict `>`** → a SKU counted AND packaged on the same date can mis-settle (the count and the production happen on the same calendar day; DATE granularity + `>` cannot order them). Needs **DATETIME granularity on `counted_at`** — **worth doing before/with the Monday 2026-06-15 cage count** (cage anchor is the next big partial-count event that could re-trip this class).
