## ✅ SAME-DAY TIEBREAK SHIPPED 2026-06-09 — same-day count+package carryover CLOSED via Option 2 (surgical tiebreak, NO migration; committed `d3fb954`, pushed, live; data-layer only — `app/fg-stock.php`; EQUIP coder+sql)
Closes PF-stock carryover (1) WITHOUT the DATE→DATETIME migration. The bug: a beer counted AND packaged on the SAME date (e.g. EMBF 2026-06-08) had its same-day production-site packaging DROPPED, because the per-SKU production anchor used a strict `event_date > prod_anchor` cutoff against a DATE `counted_at` — the same-day packaging tied the cutoff and fell out.

**Implementation (`fg_prod_since_anchor()`):**
- Per-SKU production anchor now uses a single **`ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY sku_id_fk ORDER BY counted_at DESC, id DESC)`** window pick (rn=1), exposing the WINNING production-site count's BOTH `counted_at` (→ `prod_anchor`) AND `created_at` (→ `prod_anchor_ts`). **NOT two blind MAXes** — the PM-flagged gotcha (two independent MAX() could pair a `counted_at` from one row with a `created_at` from another). One window row = one coherent count.
- Cutoff predicate: `event_date > COALESCE(prod_anchor, $globalAnchor) OR (prod_anchor IS NOT NULL AND event_date = prod_anchor AND submitted_at > prod_anchor_ts)`.
- **Primary ordering on business `event_date`**; `submitted_at > prod_anchor_ts` (created_at) only breaks SAME-DATE ties. NULL-safe for never-counted SKUs (collapses to pure `$globalAnchor` cutoff). Empty-prodSites fallback unchanged. All prior guards kept (cuv-exclude, tombstoned, white_label, FLOOR-per-event, COALESCE).
- SINGLE helper → both `fg_stock_compute()` AND `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` inherit the predicate; card vs SKU-total can't drift.

**OPUS INDEPENDENT VERIFICATION (old-vs-new predicate diff across ALL SKUs):** exactly ONE SKU changed — **EMBF**, the genuine 2026-06-08 collision (prod-site count `created_at` 13:54:13; EMBF packaging `event_date` 06-08 submitted 14:53:07 → after the count → tie-broken IN → **OLD dropped=0, NEW=300 kegs recovered**). NO other SKU perturbed: DIV4=412 / physique=511, DIVB=108, ZEPV absent, never-counted (DIB4/DIVF/EPH4B)=0. **Σ(locations)==Σphysique=8312.**

**Decisions LOCKED (durable):**
- `counted_at` STAYS DATE — business-truth column, mirrors `bd_packaging_v2.event_date`.
- `created_at` is canonically "when counted" for maltyweb-form / manual rows.
- `form_timestamp` NULL = latent Google-Form-era gap; NOT fixed now.
- **NO DATETIME migration** — rejected for blast radius on every DATE-equality consumer.
- Sales legs (expedie/eshop/taproom) STILL deferred to the stock-movement-saisie arc.

**ACCEPTED RESIDUAL (inline SCOPE NOTE in `app/fg-stock.php`):** a run physically-before but submitted-after a same-day count → rare double-count, left un-clamped ON PURPOSE. If it ever bites, the fix is an explicit count timestamp — NOT a clamp.

**Smoke:** 302 login-redirect (no page creds in this context); change is data-layer only, both stock functions proven non-throwing + data hand-verified → accepted. **NO migration number consumed** (293/294/295 are parallel sessions'). MIGRATION HEAD = 295; NEXT FREE = 298 (296/297 pending on VPS, BBT-vide arc) — re-check `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` before assigning.

## 2026-06-08 — Multipack display-family split (mig 287; SHIPPED+verified+committed `f97bcb9` local-only; PM-verified live)
**Stocktake (`expeditions.php` `?view=stocktake`) now groups curated/assortment gift packs under their own "Multipacks" header, split away from Bouteille.**

**CONFIRMED TAXONOMY (Kouros via AskUserQuestion 2026-06-08) — Multipacks = the curated/assortment gift packs ONLY:** Pack Découverte (PD8, format_id **19**), Xmas Pack (XMASPACK, **20**), Pack Louis (PAL, **21**), Pack du Chef (PAC, **23**), + future DGD pack when it exists. **The 6×4 packs (-4 SKUs) STAY under Bouteille/Canette** — a 6×4 is a presentation of the same-beer 24-pack, not a multipack. The 24-pack carton itself stays Bouteille (that's the "bottle" the multipacks are split away from). Rule of thumb: multipack = **cross-beer assortment**; -4/-B = same-beer presentation.

**Mechanism (the PM-recommended one — a per-format display-grouping column, NOT a hardcode):**
- **Mig 287 `287_ref_packaging_formats_display_family.sql` (APPLIED, head=287, 0 pending; PM live-verified — NEXT FREE = 288):** `ALTER TABLE ref_packaging_formats ADD COLUMN display_family VARCHAR(32) NULL` (placed after `derived_from_format_id`; `run_type` is not the last col — no functional difference) + `UPDATE … SET display_family='multipack' WHERE id IN (19,20,21,23)`. All other formats keep `display_family NULL`. **Live-confirmed 4 seed rows = 19/20/21/23.**
- **`expeditions.php` (view=stocktake):** `$stAllSkus` LEFT JOINs `ref_packaging_formats` and selects `COALESCE(f.display_family, s.format) AS display_family`; family-grouping groups by `display_family` (fallback to format); `'multipack'` added to `$stFamilyOrder` (after Keg) + label "Multipacks"; `exp_format_family()`/`exp_family_label()` gained the `'multipack'` case. **Cage extraction (suffix -X) and `stocktake_scope` visibility logic UNCHANGED.** JS is DOM-driven (`data-family`) — no JS change.
- **Practical render today:** only **PD8 + XMASPACK** appear under "Multipacks" (both `stocktake_scope='base'`); **PAC/PAL are `scope='none'` → stay hidden** until activated (matches "packs découvertes et xmas currently are the ones we have activated").
- **Verified:** 153 active SKUs (count unchanged after the JOIN), `php -l` clean, curl 302. **ZERO COGS/SOT impact** — `fg_stock_compute()` keys on `sku_id`, untouched.
- **Commit `f97bcb9` on maltyweb main — NOT pushed (local only).**

**FORWARD COUPLING (carry into the cited future builds):**
- **Task #12 (Stock-config admin section):** `ref_packaging_formats.display_family` is now the **editable per-format display-grouping field**, alongside `ref_skus.stocktake_scope` — BOTH get exposed in that config UI.
- **Task #10 (Stock PF board rebuild reading `fg_stock_compute`):** the Stock PF tab's OWN format-family grouping was **deliberately NOT changed** in this commit — **multipacks must be split there too** when `fg-stock.php`'s query is rebuilt; carry `display_family` into `fg_stock_compute()` then. (This is the one place the new grouping is not yet honored — flag at Stock PF rebuild time.)

---
*(The pre-build spec below is retained as the model reference; the candidate-set / create-path / scope-lever reasoning is now as-built above.)*

**Context:** Olivier inputting taproom inventory. Taproom counts singles (-BU bottle / -CU can). Some beers have a 24-box (-B, `format_id=1`) but NO single-unit SKU → operator stopgap entered fractional packs (e.g. 21/24 against DGDB) to make HL come out right. Kouros: create the missing single SKUs (so they appear in taproom stocktake going forward) — NO hardcoding, reroute from the SKU master.

**THE SKU MASTER + VOLUME DERIVATION (verified live):**
- **`ref_skus` is the SKU master.** Key cols: `recipe_id`(→ref_recipes.id), `format_id`(→ref_packaging_formats.id), `format`(display label e.g. 'Bot'/'Can'), `hl_per_unit`(DECIMAL — COPIED from the chosen format's hl_per_unit at create), `units_per_pack`(NOT NULL DEFAULT 1), `stocktake_scope` ENUM('base','cage','single','none') DEFAULT 'none', `is_packaging_line`, `is_direct_sales`, `row_hash`.
- **Single-unit ≠ a column on the pack — it is its OWN `ref_skus` row** on the SAME recipe but a DIFFERENT `format_id`. A pack and its single are siblings under one recipe, NOT parent/child. Bottle pack = `format_id=1` (B, 24×33cl, hl_per_unit 0.0792). Bottle single = `format_id=5` (BU, "Bottle unit single 33cl", hl_per_unit 0.0033). Can single = `format_id=14` (CU, single 50cl, hl_per_unit 0.005). So DGDBU = a NEW ref_skus row: recipe 31, format_id 5, format 'Bot', hl_per_unit 0.0033, units_per_pack 1, stocktake_scope 'single'.
- **Volume auto-derives, NEVER hardcoded:** `ref_skus.hl_per_unit` is copied from `ref_packaging_formats.hl_per_unit` of the chosen format (itself = units_per_format × `dbc_container_types.hl_per_unit`, zero-drift chain — volume-dimension.md). A new DGDBU created via the canonical path inherits 0.0033 from format 5 automatically.

**WHAT MAKES A SKU APPEAR IN TAPROOM STOCKTAKE = `ref_skus.stocktake_scope` (the channel flag — NO hardcoding needed).** `expeditions.php` `exp_st_scope_allowed($scope,$siteType)` (the visibility matrix, ~L1626): `base`→all sites; `cage`→production+warehouse; **`single`→pos ONLY (= Taproom)**; `none`→never. So a single-unit SKU **MUST be `stocktake_scope='single'`** to show for Olivier at Taproom (site_type='pos'). This is also the **DOCB exclusion lever**: DOCB/DOCF are `scope='base'` today; we simply do NOT create a DOCBU (or if created, leave scope≠'single') — no hardcode, the absence of a 'single'-scoped Docks SKU keeps it out of taproom count. The 26 existing 'single'-scope SKUs are exactly the BU/CU singles.

**THE GAP (verified live 2026-06-09) — recipes with a bottle/can PACK but NO single sibling, active SKUs:**
- **r31 DGDB (DrunkBeard - Galactic Drift)** → missing **DGDBU** (THE live problem; DGDB has stocktake rows incl. the 8/24 + 121 stopgaps at loc1).
- **r20 BAMB (Chien Bleu - Bamse, Contract)**, **r21 JASPB (Chien Bleu - Jasper, Contract)** → missing BU. **Contract beers — likely NOT taproom-sold; confirm with Kouros before creating + scoping 'single'.**
- **r29 DOCB (Docks - NEIPA)** → **EXCLUDED per Kouros (not sold in taproom).**
- The `recipe_id NULL` group (COLLAB12/COLLAB4PACK/PAC/PAL/PD8/XMASPACK) is a FALSE POSITIVE — composites/multipacks, not single-beer packs; ignore.
- **So the real "create a single" candidate set = DGDBU (now/deferred), + BAMBU/JASPBU IFF Kouros confirms Chien Bleu sells singles at taproom.** All core Neb beers already HAVE their BU/CU (the 26 'single' SKUs). DOC excluded. Verify the list with Kouros — do NOT auto-create contract singles.

**CANONICAL CREATE PATH = format-activation in Salle de contrôle (`public/modules/salle-de-controle.php` ~L262, action that INSERTs ref_skus).** Operator picks recipe + format → INSERT `(sku_code, recipe_id, format_id, format, hl_per_unit FROM the format, is_active=1, row_hash=sha256(recipe_id|format_id|sku_code), bom_template_id, last_modified_by='web', last_seen_at, imported_at)` + `log_revision` + post-commit `sdc_recompile_recipe_packaging($recipeId)`. **⚠️ GAP in that action: it does NOT set `stocktake_scope` (defaults 'none') or `units_per_pack` (defaults 1).** For a single, units_per_pack=1 is correct, but **scope stays 'none' → the new single would NOT appear in taproom until scope is set to 'single'.** Two clean options: (a) one-shot direct SQL after creating via SDC (set scope='single'); (b) better/durable — the planned **task #12 stock-config admin** exposes `stocktake_scope` (alongside `display_family`) as an editable field, which is the proper home for flipping a SKU's channel visibility. PM rec: create DGDBU via SDC format-activation (auto-correct hl_per_unit + audit + BOM recompile), then set scope='single' (direct SQL one-shot now; task #12 UI later). `sku_code` is operator-chosen ('DGDBU'); UNIQUE collision-guarded on (recipe,format).

**COGS / derivation implications:** a single-unit SKU is a REAL packaging line (`is_packaging_line=1` like its siblings) and gets a BOM via `sdc_recompile_recipe_packaging` — it = 1× (bottle+cap+label+TEA+liquid), the INTRINSIC single-bottle BOM (walkthrough RULE #3). It maps to the **SAME recipe** as the pack (recipe 31 for DGDBU) → same liquid/COGS basis; only the format (and thus units_per_pack=1, hl_per_unit=0.0033) differs. NOT a pure count surface — it flows into BOM/COGS like any SKU. Double-count guard (walkthrough cardinal invariant): a bottle is produced+consumed ONCE — selling a single vs selling it in a box are different sale events drawing the same physical bottle; no double-count AT SALE.

**STEP 1 (deferred, AFTER stocktake input) — correct the DGDB stopgap → DGDBU:** counts live in **`inv_fg_stocktake`** (cols: sku_id_fk, location_id_fk, counted_at, month_closed, qty DECIMAL(10,4), source ENUM, is_active, **`row_hash` = STORED GENERATED** `sha256(fgct|sku_id_fk|location_id_fk|counted_at)` since mig 288 — location & hash can't diverge). Correcting = (i) create DGDBU; (ii) the stopgap row was qty=8 (or 21) recorded against DGDB sku_id at the 24-box scale — to "move into DGDBU as 21 units": INSERT/UPSERT a DGDBU row qty=21 at the same location/counted_at AND zero-out (or delete via is_active=0 + audit) the fractional DGDB stopgap row. **Do it via the EXISTING edit feature** (`expeditions.php` FG-stocktake date-scoped edit, manager/admin) NOT ad-hoc SQL — the row_hash incident (2026-06-08, see §INCIDENT) proves ad-hoc UPDATEs that touch sku/location WITHOUT going through the form/generated-hash path corrupt the dedup key. The generated row_hash now makes a sku-change auto-rehash, but route through the audited edit path regardless. Snapshot + log_revision.

**SEQUENCING:** (a) NOW = identify gap (done above) + confirm the create-list with Kouros (DGDBU yes; BAMBU/JASPBU only if Chien Bleu taproom-sold; DOC excluded). (b) Create the singles via SDC format-activation + set scope='single'. (c) DEFERRED to after taproom input = the DGDB→DGDBU count correction via the edit feature. **EQUIP for the build: sql + coder + ui + webapp-testing** (the create touches SDC PHP + a scope flip + a stocktake correction via the UI edit path; smoke ?view=stocktake at Taproom shows the new single).

## 2026-06-08 — INCIDENT + DURABLE FIX: `inv_fg_stocktake.row_hash` divergence (hash-keyed row mutated without rehash)
**INCIDENT (root cause understood, data ALREADY repaired+verified by operator):** the 06-08 misfile *correction itself* corrupted 28 rows. The stocktake dedup/upsert key is `row_hash = sha256("fgct|{sku_id_fk}|{location_id_fk}|{counted_at}")`, app-written, `UNIQUE uniq_row_hash`, INSERT … ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE (qty only, NOT location). The ad-hoc SQL `UPDATE location_id_fk 1→2` did **NOT recompute row_hash** → 28 rows sat at loc2 still hashed as loc1; the operator's later loc1 (Production) submit hash-COLLIDED with them and overwrote qty. **Repaired** in one txn from `audit_row_revisions` (before=Crissier/batch1, after=Production/batch3): restored 23 Crissier + recreated 23 Production + fixed 5 stale hashes; final loc1=27/550u, loc2=28/5976u, loc4=26/554u; **row_hash integrity 0 mismatch across all 81 June rows.** Data clean.
**DURABLE FIX — PM RULING 2026-06-08 (APPROVED, with one mandatory amendment): convert `row_hash` to a STORED GENERATED column** `CHAR(64) AS (SHA2(CONCAT_WS('|','fgct',sku_id_fk,location_id_fk,counted_at),256)) STORED`, UNIQUE preserved → location_id_fk and hash can NEVER diverge again (fix-by-construction; the "remember to recompute hash on location change" lesson is thereby MOOT). Generated col, NOT a trigger (a trigger is bypassable by direct UPDATE exactly as this incident was; generated col is structural). STORED not VIRTUAL (UNIQUE index stability). **PM-VERIFIED LIVE before ruling:**
  - **SOLE writer = `expeditions.php:746` INSERT.** Every other ref to `inv_fg_stocktake` (warehouse.php, warehouse-export.php, app/fg-stock.php, maltytask lib/inventory*.{js,ts}, mysql-inventory.ts) is **read-only SELECT**. `sync-stocktake.js` writes BSF Sheets, never MySQL. **`source='bsf-stocktake'` has ZERO code writers** (appears only in mig 066's ENUM def). → converting is safe from rejected-INSERT; the form INSERT drops `row_hash` from its column list, ON DUPLICATE KEY fires off the generated UNIQUE.
  - **🔴 MANDATORY AMENDMENT — the premise "data is 100% hash-consistent" is FALSE for 41 rows.** `WHERE row_hash <> SHA2(CONCAT_WS('|','fgct',sku_id_fk,location_id_fk,counted_at),256)` = **41 rows**, ALL the `source='bsf-stocktake'` **April anchor** (`month_closed='2026-04'`, `counted_at IS NULL`), hashed by the OLDER legacy-import formula. June (81) is consistent; April (41) is NOT. On DROP+ADD, those 41 silently re-mint to `fgct|sid|loc` (CONCAT_WS SKIPS NULL counted_at — note PHP `sha256` would emit a trailing `|`, so PHP-formula ≠ generated-formula in the NULL case; generated col is the more-correct canonical). **Tolerable ONLY because nothing re-derives those hashes** (no bsf-stocktake writer). **Collision check PASS: all 122 rows → 122 distinct generated hashes (0 collisions); 2nd UK `uniq_sku_month_location_response` also 122/122 distinct.** Build must do this KNOWINGLY + document it in the migration comment; verify post-convert: 0 rows where `row_hash <> SHA2(...)`, 122 distinct, April-2026 active anchor still 41 rows.
  - **BUILD: own migration (confirm next free # via `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` — parallel sessions take numbers, the 278 collision is precedent; local index showed head 287). DDL = DROP INDEX uniq_row_hash → DROP COLUMN row_hash → ADD generated STORED (collation `utf8mb4_unicode_ci` to match, or mixed-collation throw) → ADD UNIQUE uniq_row_hash. No new schema_meta row (existing table). `expeditions.php` edit: drop row_hash from INSERT col-list + binding (~L748/749/763/782); KEEP the `$rowHash = hash('sha256',…)` compute — still used by the before-snapshot `SELECT … WHERE row_hash=?` at L767; ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE stays (counted_at no-op since match is BY the hash). EQUIP: sql + coder (NO ui — pure backend). Proof: dry-run 0 mismatch; idempotent double-submit → 1 row; UPDATE location_id_fk auto-shifts hash; self-clean test rows.**
  - **🔗 FORWARD COUPLING for task #12 stock-config admin + task #10 Stock PF:** once row_hash is generated, any admin UI editing `location_id_fk` on a stocktake row AUTO-REHASHES — desired, but it can now collide into an existing (sku,loc,date) row → the UNIQUE rejects/the ON DUPLICATE merges. The admin edit path MUST handle the UNIQUE-violation/target-exists case (the exact scenario that caused this incident). Note in the #12 brief.

**✅ SHIPPED + LIVE (mig 288, 2026-06-08 — agent conn dropped mid-run; PM live-verified + reconciled).** Generated col IS live and working: `row_hash CHAR(64) GENERATED ALWAYS AS SHA2(CONCAT_WS('|','fgct',sku_id_fk,location_id_fk,counted_at),256) STORED NOT NULL`, `UNIQUE uniq_row_hash`. 122 rows / 122 distinct hashes / 0 collisions; June repair intact (loc1=27/550u, loc2=28/5976u, loc4=26/554u); April anchor 41. Form deployed (row_hash dropped from INSERT). 0 orphan + 0 NULL sku_id_fk.
  - **FK RULING (PM, decisive): `fk_fg_sku` re-added as ON DELETE RESTRICT.** To add the generated col referencing sku_id_fk the agent had to DROP `fk_fg_sku` (was sku_id_fk→ref_skus.id ON DELETE **SET NULL** — MySQL 8 forbids SET NULL/CASCADE on a generated-col input) and did NOT re-add it ("app-level integrity"). PM ruled: RESTORE the FK as **ON DELETE RESTRICT** (MySQL 8 ALLOWS RESTRICT/NO ACTION on a generated-col input; 0 orphans/0 NULLs → clean; strictly stronger than the moot SET NULL; a NULL sku_id_fk on a count row is a corrupt fact, not a tolerable orphan — aligns w/ FK-discipline + minimize-NULL). `fk_fg_stocktake_location` (location_id_fk→ref_sites ON DELETE RESTRICT) was KEPT throughout (RESTRICT always allowed on gen-col inputs). **Both FK columns are now BOTH FK-enforced (RESTRICT) AND row_hash inputs** — fully-wired canonical state; any future mig touching either column's type/nullability must account for both the FK and the generated expression.
  - **RECONCILIATION (schema_migrations drift — DDL live but unrecorded; agent applied DDL without recording).** Ruled: (1) EDIT the 288 file so it fully describes live = gen col + uniq_row_hash + `DROP FOREIGN KEY fk_fg_sku` + `ADD CONSTRAINT fk_fg_sku … ON DELETE RESTRICT` (fold the FK re-add into 288, NOT a separate 289 — the FK drop+re-add is a consequence of the gen-col DDL, one atomic migration matching live exactly). (2) Run ONLY the missing ALTER on live (gen col + UNIQUE + DROP already live; only the RESTRICT re-add outstanding): `ALTER TABLE inv_fg_stocktake ADD CONSTRAINT fk_fg_sku FOREIGN KEY (sku_id_fk) REFERENCES ref_skus(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT;`. (3) `INSERT INTO schema_migrations (filename, applied_at) VALUES ('288_inv_fg_stocktake_row_hash_generated.sql', NOW());` (the known drift pattern; confirm exact on-disk filename first). (4) `migrate.php --status` must show 288 no longer pending + nothing to apply — migrate.php must NOT re-run 288 (would error re-DROPping/re-ADDing). schema_meta needs no new row (existing table); verify the existing row is present (don't duplicate). EQUIP sql+coder.

## 2026-06-09 — WeeklyOrders SHEET INGESTION arc: PM PRE-BUILD RULINGS (dry-run→match-report→Kouros reviews unmatched→apply)
Goal: ingest the live WeeklyOrders sheet (Production/Logistic Masterfile, Google Sheet `1WA-GfwrD-lgMiWJ2ejg-92zq1Ps0CZaK6Sn11isbXyI`, tab WeeklyOrders, row-6 SKU header, per-week blocks) into `ord_orders` so operators continue on the web "where they left off." Revenue/fulfilment-bearing → never-speculate rule applies HARD; dry-run-first, flag-over-decide.

**LIVE STATE VERIFIED (PM-probed 2026-06-09):** `ord_orders`=12 / `ord_order_lines`=56 / `ord_order_status_events`=39. **The "12 test orders" ARE NOT throwaway — they are real KW24 customer orders, `source='web'`, requested_date 2026-06-08/09, all BC-matched (ids 3-14; e.g. 6=AlloBoissons BC1393, 7=Bevanar BC1579, 8=Marché Flag Aubonne shipped, 9=Département Marketing BC1807, 14=Sophie Degrauwe privé no-BC).** They have full event cascades (entered+confirmed+picked stamped at one timestamp). **NO `source_ref`/dedup column on ord_orders; NO UNIQUE business key** — only PK + non-unique indexes (requested_date, status, customer, source+review_status). This is the crux of Q6.

**THE 7 RULINGS (decisive):**
1. **SCOPE = AGREE.** Import KW24 full current week (incl. already-delivered Mon/Tue) + ALL future booked (next-Monday + coming-weeks, through last dated future row before the Feb archive). **EXCLUDE the KW6/Feb archive** (delivered months ago = not operational handoff; "past" is satisfied by KW24's delivered rows). No bounded recent-past window — the handoff is "continue where you left off," not "rebuild history." If Kouros wants a longer past tail for the Commandes range-view, that's a SEPARATE future-history-backfill arc, not this ingestion.
2. **STATUS = rightmost-checked-wins AGREE; emit EVERY reached stage as an event (events=truth), NOT just final.** Same pattern the 12 web rows already use (entered+confirmed+picked all stamped). occurred_at = requested_date (00:00) for ALL reached stages — we have no per-stage timestamps from Excel; stamping reached stages at the order date is the honest reconstruction (collapsing to final-only would LOSE the audit fact that the order passed through them). Mark imported events `comment='import:weeklyorders'` so they're distinguishable from operator-driven transitions. Cache `status`=rightmost stage. (`user_id_fk` NULL on import events — matches the existing 12.)
3. **INTERNAL CHANNELS = SKIP Taproom/Eshop/samples/Marketing-as-internal/privé-marketing notes — DO NOT import as ord_orders.** This is the R1 one-fact-one-depletion rule. Eshop depletes via `inv_sales_orders`, Taproom via `inv_sales_bc` (the `fg_stock_compute()` legs) — creating ord_orders for them = DOUBLE-DEPLETION on the board. WeeklyOrders Taproom/Eshop rows are operational notes, not the depletion truth. **CAVEAT (verify, don't assume): "(Marketing)"/"Département Marketing" is AMBIGUOUS — order id 9 is already a `customer` order to "Département Marketing (BC 1807)" (a real BC sold-to that depletes via ord_*), NOT an internal channel.** So the skip-list is: rows whose CLIENT cell is literally Taproom / Eshop / "échantillons TS"/samples — the internal-consumption channels that have their OWN depletion source. A BC-numbered Marketing sold-to is a customer order (keep). When in doubt → match report, never auto-skip a BC-numbered row.
4. **CUSTOMER MATCHING = AGREE, with the canon already established (no-fuzzy-links).** Precedence: parens BC# → `ref_customers.bc_customer_no` (exact); else name → exact, then `'alias:'`-noted rows from the merge pipeline, then **STOP** — **NO fuzzy auto-link** (the §2026-06-07 LATE item-2 + §OVERNIGHT canon: «Arches»→«Marchés» 0.92 false match proves it). Fuzzy ≥ threshold = SUGGESTION in the match report ONLY, never an auto-link. Unmatched/below-threshold/privé-not-validated → SURFACE in match report, NEVER auto-create or guess (revenue-bearing). Point the agent at the EXISTING infra: the merge-suggestion engine (`scripts/` merge pipeline, `9803849`) + the Carnet-clients typeahead ranking (bc-linked first, ⚠-à-valider last) — REUSE that resolver, don't write a new one. privé individuals → match to validated private customers (the 89 privés bucket from §OVERNIGHT) else flag.
5. **CITÉ MULTI-LOCATION FESTIVAL = AGREE, N separate ord_orders.** One customer (BC 1823), ~13 distinct delivery rows = 13 ord_orders, each its own `requested_date` + line(s) + sub-location (Courtine/Grand Canyon/Pierre Viret/Stock F&B…) in `comment`. The order grain is the delivery event, not the customer — distinct dates/locations are distinct fulfilment obligations. (No festival-grouping entity needed in v1; comment carries the sub-location string verbatim.)
6. **DEDUP/IDEMPOTENCY = the real architectural decision. RULING: ADD a `source_ref VARCHAR` column to `ord_orders` capturing the sheet-row identity, with a UNIQUE/idempotency guard — do NOT rely on a (customer,date,line-hash) heuristic.** Rationale: (a) the 12 existing rows are `source='web'` real orders that OVERLAP KW24 — a content-hash dedup would either falsely-merge a legit second same-day order to the same client or fail to recognise the operator-entered twin; (b) line-hash is brittle (qty edits on the sheet, parallel -4/-B). **`source_ref` = stable sheet coordinate** e.g. `weeklyorders:{tab_gid}:{week_label}:{row_index}` (or a sheet-row content fingerprint if row indices shift). New mig: `ALTER TABLE ord_orders ADD COLUMN source_ref VARCHAR(190) NULL` + `UNIQUE uniq_ord_source_ref (source_ref)` (NULL allowed → web/email orders unaffected; only import rows carry it) → re-run = INSERT…ON DUPLICATE KEY skip/update, structurally idempotent. **The 12 web rows: do NOT reconcile/replace/import-over them.** Match report flags any KW24 sheet row that collides with an existing web order (same customer_id_fk + same requested_date) as "⚠ possible duplicate of existing web order #N — operator decides keep-both / skip-import." NEVER auto-delete an operator's web order; NEVER auto-merge. The 12 are the operator's ground truth for the rows they already entered; the importer fills the REST of KW24 + the future book around them.
7. **OFF-TRADE = AGREE, customer attribute not order attribute.** The col2 OFF flag is `ref_customers.trade_channel` (already bootstrapped by explicit-ID list, §2026-06-07 LATE item-4 — Cobra-channel, substring-UNSAFE). Ignore it on the order; trust ref_customers. If a sheet row's OFF flag DISAGREES with the customer's stored trade_channel, that's a data-quality signal → surface in the match report (don't silently override either way).

**DIVERGENCE FLAGS for this build:** (i) double-depletion if Taproom/Eshop become ord_orders (ruling #3 prevents); (ii) fuzzy auto-link corrupting a revenue-bearing customer FK (ruling #4 — flag-only); (iii) the 12-web-row overlap silently double-creating KW24 (ruling #6 — source_ref UNIQUE + collision-flag); (iv) a BC-numbered Marketing/privé sold-to wrongly skipped as "internal" (ruling #3 caveat). **SEQUENCING:** mig (source_ref col + UNIQUE) → parser/dry-run producing match report (matched / fuzzy-suggested / unmatched / internal-skipped / web-overlap-collision buckets) → Kouros reviews unmatched+collisions → `--apply` (single txn per order; ord_orders + lines + cascaded events; log_revision; idempotent on source_ref). **EQUIP: sql + coder + xlsx-or-sheets-read** (the source is a live Google Sheet — service-account read; the existing bootstrap used a downloaded xlsx, mirror that or read via the sheets client; NO ui unless a match-report viewer page is wanted — recommend a plain markdown/CSV report first, like the bootstrap report). Mig number: re-run `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` first (parallel sessions; head was 290, next free likely 291 — VERIFY).

### 2026-06-10 — WeeklyOrders AUDIT-RESIDUALS RULINGS (privé double-deplete · empty-order/event-material · week-scoped search). PM-ruled, LIVE-DB-VERIFIED, pre-build.
**Three audit residuals after the import. All verified against live prod 2026-06-10.**

**① PRIVÉ / SHOPIFY-PICKUP ORDERS — ruled SAFE TO WRITE AS CUSTOMER ORDERS; NO double-deplete on these two rows.** The two sheet rows (r285 Joël Golinucci ZEPF×2 EMBF×2; r298 Alice Buache ZEPF×2 MOOF×1) are **NOT in `inv_sales_orders`** (LIVE-VERIFIED: surname search Golinucci/Buache = 0 hits; only same-first-name strangers) → they are **manual sheet click&collect entries, NOT Shopify-synced** → writing them as `ord_orders` (order_type='customer') has **no eshop-leg twin → no double-deplete**. So 1c sub-option **(ii) is the correct one for these rows.**
  - **a. NO canonical "Privé" fold-account exists** — Kouros's "fold to one account" premise is NOT current reality. Live: **83 `is_private=1` rows, one per individual, all `trade_channel='on_trade'`, no `bc_customer_no`** (the 89-privé needs_review bucket largely became these). **RULING: do NOT invent a single shared Privé account in this build** — it would CONTRADICT the existing per-individual model + the no-fuzzy-link/never-guess canon, and there's no operator-confirmed merge map. Per-individual privé rows ARE the convention; create the 2 missing ones as their OWN `is_private=1` rows (name as on sheet, `is_active=1`, `trade_channel='on_trade'`, `bc_customer_no=NULL`) — exactly like the 83 that exist. If Kouros truly wants ONE fold-account, that's a SEPARATE merge-decision arc (reuse the Carnet merge tool → tombstone individuals `merged_into:`), not a side-effect of this import. FLAG the contradiction to Kouros; do not resolve it by guessing.
  - **b. Individual name preservation:** the per-individual `ref_customers.name` already IS the name (no fold). If Kouros insists on folding, the name lives in the **`ord_orders.comment`** free-text (there is **NO `contact_name` column** on `ord_orders` — LIVE-VERIFIED schema) — do NOT add one for 2 rows.
  - **c. 🔴 THE DOUBLE-DEPLETE MECHANISM (durable, generalized):** `fg_stock_compute()` eshop leg depletes **ALL `inv_sales_orders WHERE channel='eshop' AND DATE(created_at) >= anchor`** — it does **NOT filter `fulfillment_status`** (LIVE-VERIFIED query in `app/fg-stock.php` ~L482). So pickup-vs-ship is INVISIBLE to depletion: any eshop order in `inv_sales_orders` already depletes. **THE GATING RULE (canonical): an order belongs in `ord_orders` (B2B/expedie leg) XOR `inv_sales_orders` (eshop leg) — NEVER both. The discriminator is membership in `inv_sales_orders`, not a flag we invent.** For THESE two rows: absent from `inv_sales_orders` → ord_orders write is safe. **FORWARD HAZARD (the ④ Phase-2 gate, still ON HOLD):** once the Shopify pickup-signal rework lands and pickup orders DO sync into `inv_sales_orders`, writing the SAME pickup order to `ord_orders` for the picking workflow WOULD double-deplete. The clean solution at that time = pickup orders deplete via the eshop leg (already do), and the Expéditions picking view READS them from `inv_sales_orders` (like the existing muted read-only eshop/taproom rows on the Commandes board, expeditions.php ~L1591) — it does NOT re-create them as depleting `ord_orders`. Do NOT solve this now; it's gated on the Shopify rework. (Note: `internal_channel` ENUM already carries `'cage','shop'` beyond taproom/eshop — but internal_channel is for `order_type='internal'`, a different fact; a privé pickup is a real customer sale, not internal.)
  - **d. Write path:** these 2 rows resolve to NO customer today → the importer bucketed them UNMATCHED (it has no "fold to Privé" path — confirmed by the privé-not-validated→flag ruling #4). Convention-correct write = **create the 2 `is_private=1 ref_customers` rows first (Kouros-authorized, name-as-stated = NOT speculative), THEN re-run `import_weeklyorders.php --apply`** (idempotent on `source_ref`; resolver now matches the new rows; lines DGDF/ZEPF/EMBF/MOOF all resolve). Do NOT hand-write ord_orders bypassing the importer/resolver/event-cascade path.

**② EMPTY-ORDER ALLOCATION — split: ONE is a real FG order, the rest are NON-PRODUCT event/marketing material that must NOT become FG order lines.**
  - **a. `DGDF` EXISTS** (LIVE-VERIFIED `ref_skus` id=9, recipe 31 DrunkBeard "Galactic Drift", format 15 = keg/Fass, is_active=1). So **r80 Street Cellar "3 Galac fûts" → DGDF×3 IS a valid FG order line** (Galac = Galactic Drift = the keg). Kouros's "Galac fûts = DGDF" is CONFIRMED correct. This one row becomes a normal customer order.
  - **b. `Cuves`, `T7`, `Galac` are NOT sku_codes** (LIVE-VERIFIED: T7/CUVES/GALAC exact + substring = 0 hits in `ref_skus`). "Cuves" (r102 Jardins de Louis) and "T7" (r199 Gotham/Marketing, r223 Gotham + "1 pack dec gratuité") do NOT resolve to any SKU.
  - **c. 🔴 RULING — event/serving/marketing material does NOT live in `ord_orders` and must NOT deplete FG.** "T7" (a serving-tank / tap-tower style equipment loan), "Cuves" (serving cuves = equipment, NOT the -V cuv SALE SKU), and marketing giveaways are **non-product / equipment / promo**, not Neb FG beer. Forcing them into `ord_orders` lines = wrongly depleting beer SKUs (the never-guess-a-mapping + one-fact-one-table rule). **DO NOT allocate T7/Cuves to beer SKUs.** Options to put to Kouros (do not guess which): (i) these are equipment loans → out of scope for `ord_orders` entirely (skip; they have no FG depletion fact); (ii) the "1 pack dec gratuité" on r223 IS a real product giveaway → route to the **`inv_side_stock_ledger` `movement_type='giveaway'`** path (mig 303, the unit-count giveaway ledger §ITEM 2) keyed to the actual SKU, NOT an ord_orders line — that's the canonical home for "offered/gratuité" units. The "3 Galac fûts" (DGDF) is the ONLY one of the 4 empty-orders that is a real product order. **Keep the other 3 in the held-out bucket pending Kouros: equipment-loan-skip vs giveaway-ledger; never auto-allocate as beer SKUs.**

**③ WEEK-SCOPED SEARCH (Blind Tigers) — CONFIRMED root cause; fix = drop the date window when a client search term is present. In scope as a quick follow-up.**
  - **Root cause LIVE-VERIFIED** (`expeditions.php`): Commandes defaults `mode=week` / current ISO week (L1205); the Commandes query ALWAYS seeds `$where=['o.requested_date BETWEEN ? AND ?']` (L1475) and ANDs `c.name LIKE` onto it (L1479-1481). Blind Tigers #84/#85 are req_date 2026-06-29 (~3 wk out) → current-week window returns nothing despite a name match. (NB the Carnet-clients directory search L1884-1886 is already date-unscoped — only the Commandes ORDER list is week-trapped.)
  - **HOUSE-PATTERN RULING: when a client search term is present, the client-name filter spans ALL dates — suppress the `requested_date BETWEEN` clause (or widen to an all-time bound) for that query.** Rationale: a name search is an intent to FIND a specific client's orders, not to browse a week; the date window is a browse affordance, not a search constraint. This matches Kouros's expectation and the already-date-unscoped Carnet search. Keep the week/range nav for the no-search browse case. Preserve the SKU/statut/canal filters as-is. Small, surgical, low-risk; **YES in scope as a quick follow-up.** Do NOT build a separate global-search surface — reuse the existing Commandes `client` filter, just un-gate the date window when it's non-empty. **EQUIP: coder + sql + ui + webapp-testing** (read-only prod smoke: search "Blind Tigers" with no kw → #84/#85 appear).

**SEQUENCING:** ① + ② are data + a re-run of the existing idempotent importer (no new build needed beyond creating the 2 privé rows + DGDF allocation + putting the T7/Cuves/giveaway question to Kouros). ③ is the only code change — a surgical edit to one query's WHERE assembly in `expeditions.php`. None are gated on each other. ① forward-hazard (pickup double-deplete) stays PARKED behind the Shopify rework (④ Phase 2).

**CONVENTION CONFIRMED — privé = individual `is_private=1` rows** (Kouros option A), NOT a single fold-account. This ratifies ruling ①a: the per-individual model stands; #3058/#3059 created exactly like the existing 83. (Kouros separately wants a Shopify-integration plan-mode later — distinct future arc.)

**🆕 NEW CONVENTION — marketing giveaways (order-attached):** a 100%-rebate giveaway is booked as an `ord_orders` line to the central **Département Marketing account (id 673, BC 1807)**, with the actual recipient named in the **order comment**, the **real SKU at real qty**, so that **Σ(that account's lines × SKU value) = the annual marketing-giveaway total.** This **SUPERSEDES** the earlier ②c suggestion to route order-attached giveaways to `inv_side_stock_ledger movement_type='giveaway'` — that ledger remains the home for loose-unit/non-order giveaways, but an order-attached giveaway is booked on the Marketing customer order. **`ord_order_lines` has NO price/rebate column** — the 100% rebate is expressed via `line_comment='gratuité 100%'`; the value is DERIVABLE from SKU cost, not stored.

**SKU NOTE — `PACKDEC` → `PD8`:** `PACKDEC` is an INACTIVE Shopify alias of the canonical active SKU **PD8 (id 137)** "Pack Découverte 8×33cl" — use PD8.

**③ SEARCH FIX SHIPPED + DEPLOYED** (NOT committed — parallel-session tree; `expeditions.php` Commandes): when a find-intent is active (client-name search, OR `status='ouvertes'`/`'expediees'`), the `requested_date BETWEEN <week>` clause is DROPPED so results span ALL dates; added a new **"Expédiées (toutes dates)"** status option; a **"Résultats — toutes dates · N"** banner + greyed-out week-nav when find-intent active; `LIMIT 500` surfaced. Browse-mode (no filter) unchanged. Fixes the "can't find Blind Tigers" symptom (#84/#85 dated 2026-06-29 were week-trapped). Matches the ③ house-pattern ruling above (un-gate the date window on search-intent; reuse the existing Commandes filter, no separate global-search surface).

**🔴 IMPORTANT BUG RECORDED — `import_weeklyorders.php` line-level idempotency is BROKEN (latent data-integrity risk).** `scripts/import_weeklyorders.php` (~L665) does a plain `INSERT INTO ord_order_lines (order_id_fk, sku_id_fk, qty)` with **NO `ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE` and NO UNIQUE on (order_id_fk, sku_id_fk)**. The HEADER is idempotent on `source_ref`, but the LINES are NOT → **re-running the importer DOUBLES every order's lines.** This actually bit us: an idempotency re-run doubled lines on #101/#102/#103 (DGDF×3 became 2 rows, etc.); detected on verification and **deleted the dup line ids 314–318 — final state now correct.** **⚠️ This corrects the PM's prior "re-running import `--apply` is safe/idempotent" guidance — that is WRONG at the LINE level** (only the header is idempotent). **RECOMMENDED FIX (do NOT apply yet — needs team confirm):** add `UNIQUE KEY (order_id_fk, sku_id_fk)` + `ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE qty=VALUES(qty)`. **CAVEAT:** only safe if NO legitimate order ever carries the same SKU on two lines (different lot/tier/split) — confirm with the team first. **Also note:** `log_revision` has no `'delete'` action (ENUM is insert/update only — see migration-discipline canon), so the dup-line deletes were NOT audited.

### 🔒 DURABLE RESOLVER RULE — customer resolution MUST follow merge-tombstones to the canonical active record (REUSABLE — all customer-resolving ingests inherit it)
**Generalizes the supplier-alias resolution rule to `ref_customers` + merge-tombstones. Record prominently — this is a recurring-craft rule, candidate for the `sql`/`coder` skill if it bites a third surface.**

**RULE:** ANY customer resolution — the WeeklyOrders importer, the future **commandes@ email-order ingest**, AND the **BC sales-ledger ingest** (the one ruled on in §ITEM 1 / sales-commercial-surface) — MUST:
1. **Follow `ref_customers.notes` `merged_into: N`** to the canonical record (depth-capped to avoid cycles), and
2. **REFUSE tombstoned (`is_active=0`) matches** — never point an order/sale at a dead stub.

**WHY (the bug this prevents, observed in the original importer):** the first importer matched **tombstoned alias stubs** directly. Because a stub's id ≠ its canonical's id, the `(customer_id_fk + date)` collision check **silently missed 7 of the 12 KW24 web-overlap duplicates** (stub-id never equals the web order's canonical customer_id_fk → no collision detected) AND would have written orders pointing at dead records. The merge-tombstone follow-through is what makes the collision check correct AND keeps FKs on live customers. **The BC sales-ledger ingest you ruled on (§ITEM 1) MUST inherit this exact rule when resolving N° origine → ref_customers** — same tombstone-follow, same refuse-dead-stub discipline.

**A. SCHEMA (types verified: `ref_customers.id` + `ref_sites.id` both `INT UNSIGNED`; `ord_orders.id` BIGINT UNSIGNED):**
- **`inv_stock_movements`** (NEW table) — inter-site transfers: `id` BIGINT UNSIGNED PK; `sku_id_fk` INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL FK→ref_skus(id) RESTRICT; `from_site_id_fk` + `to_site_id_fk` INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL FK→ref_sites(id) RESTRICT (CHECK from≠to); `qty` DECIMAL(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK>0 (SKU units, mirror ord_order_lines); `moved_on` DATE NOT NULL; `comment` TEXT NULL; `is_tombstoned` TINYINT(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 (admin tombstones, NEVER delete — mirrors event-table discipline); `created_by_user_id` INT UNSIGNED NULL FK→users(id) SET NULL; created_at/updated_at. + schema_meta row (table_class='transactional', corrections_policy: tombstone-only). Both sites must `holds_fg_stock=1` (validate in handler, not CHECK).
- **`ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk`** INT UNSIGNED NULL FK→ref_sites(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT (mirror `transporter_id_fk` nullability/FK-action). NULL = historical/pre-feature → resolver falls back to channel default at read. Separate migration from 294 — no contention.
- **`ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk`** INT UNSIGNED NULL FK→ref_sites(id) ON DELETE SET NULL (mirror `default_transporter_id_fk` exactly). This IS the "Nausikraft list" mechanism: Nausikraft-delivered clients = `ref_customers` rows with this set to the Nausikraft site (id4). NO separate flag/table — a nullable default-site FK is the minimal, single-homed mechanism (mirrors the transporter default already proven). NULL = no client default → resolver uses channel default.

**B. RESOLVER (single source — ONE helper both order-create-default AND snapshot-sales-attribution call):** `app/fulfilment-site.php` `resolve_fulfilment_site(PDO, $order_row): int` returning a ref_sites.id. **Precedence CONFIRMED (Kouros's inferred order is correct):**
  1. **per-order override** — `ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk` if NOT NULL (operator's explicit pick wins).
  2. **client default** — `ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk` (the Nausikraft list) if order_type='customer' and set.
  3. **channel default** — wholesale/B2B (order_type='customer', no client default) → Crissier (warehouse, id2); internal eshop → Crissier (id2); internal taproom → Taproom (id3). (Kouros: eshop default=Crissier, taproom base=Taproom.)
  Channel-default site ids come from `ref_sites` (DB-derived by site_type/role, NOT hardcoded — eshop/wholesale→warehouse site, taproom→pos site; if multiple, the canonical default is config — recommend a `commissioning_settings` row or the lowest-sort warehouse). The resolver is PURE (no writes); used at order-create time to seed the selector default AND at fg-stock snapshot time to attribute sales.

**C. fg_stock_location_snapshot() sales attribution:** per-site sales = Σ(sales legs) WHERE `resolve_fulfilment_site(order)` = this site. MUST reuse the ONE resolver (no inline channel→site map). Keep the Σ(cards)==physique invariant: the prod leg already credits the production site; sales legs now SUBTRACT from the resolved ship-from site (today they subtract globally per §PRODUCTION-LEG FIX OPEN/DEFERRED — THIS build closes that "sales-leg per-location settlement" carryover). Historical orders with NULL fulfilment_site → resolver returns channel default (step 3) — never errors, always attributes. eshop=`inv_sales_orders`, taproom=`inv_sales_bc`, B2B=`ord_*` (R1 source map unchanged).

**D. DISPATCH SEQUENCE (Kouros's order CONFIRMED, one reorder note):** (1) migrations [inv_stock_movements + ord_orders.fulfilment_site_id_fk + ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk — 3 ALTERs/CREATE, can be ONE migration file or three; recommend ONE]; (2) **resolver helper `app/fulfilment-site.php`** (build BEFORE both consumers — it's the single-source spine); (3) order-creation ship-from selector in expeditions.php (defaulted by resolver, overridable) — **do this BEFORE snapshot attribution** so test orders carry real sites; (4) snapshot sales-attribution rewire (consumes resolver); (5) Nausikraft-client admin list on reglages-generaux.php (sets `ref_customers.default_delivery_site_id_fk`); (6) Mouvements transfer tab on expeditions.php (operators+ record; admin tombstone). **EQUIP per sub-build:** (1) sql+coder; (2) coder+sql; (3) coder+sql+ui+webapp-testing; (4) sql+coder+webapp-testing; (5) coder+sql+ui; (6) coder+sql+ui+webapp-testing.

NEXT FREE = **299** for this build (re-verify `migrate.php --status` + `ls db/migrations` AT DISPATCH — parallel sessions lead; 294-298 all parallel/untracked). **F. LANDMINES:** (i) **ord_orders contention** — do NOT touch 294's source_ref; your ADD COLUMN is independent; never re-ALTER in a way that re-declares their column. (ii) **single-resolver** — order-create default and sales-attribution MUST call the same `resolve_fulfilment_site()`; an inline duplicate map = the divergent-store anti-pattern → cards/total drift. (iii) **beer-tax neutrality** — site attribution is a LOCATION fact, not a quantity fact; total packaged-HL and beer-tax base unchanged (Σ across sites = same total). (iv) **no parallel FG-depletion path** (R1) — `inv_stock_movements` is a TRANSFER (moves stock between sites, net-zero to global physique), NOT a sale; it must NOT enter the global depletion legs, only shift the per-site split. fg_stock_compute() global total ignores transfers; ONLY fg_stock_location_snapshot() applies them (+to_site, −from_site). (v) **Nausikraft identity** — Nausikraft is BOTH a `ref_sites` row (id4 consignment, customer_id_fk=1) AND its delivered clients are `ref_customers` — don't conflate; the client list sets `default_delivery_site_id_fk=4`. (vi) **import_weeklyorders.php** must also resolve+set fulfilment_site_id_fk (else bulk-imported orders all NULL→channel-default, acceptable but flag). (vii) **transfers vs cuv** — cuv (serving-tank) is filled-at-client = already excluded from FG; a transfer of FG between sites is distinct, don't let cuv leak into inv_stock_movements.

## ✅ TASK A SHIPPED 2026-06-10 — same-day cutoff fix (eshop symmetric + transfer net-zero unit-gate); commit `2192153` origin/main; NO migration; data-layer only (`app/fg-stock.php`); EQUIP coder+sql
Closes KNOWN LIMITATION 1 of ITEM 1 for the **eshop + transfer** legs — built to the PM (A)-corrected ruling exactly. The bug class: `fg_stock_compute()` (the consumption-stock derivation Tap&Shop + others call) and `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` (the per-site card view) used DIVERGENT same-day cutoff logic on the eshop leg → Σcards could drift from Σphysique inside the same-day window; and the snapshot transfer leg admitted +to/−from per-side, so per-site anchor divergence could break per-row net-zero.

**FIX 1 — eshop leg made SYMMETRIC (compute now mirrors snapshot).** `fg_stock_compute()` Step 5 (eshop) now uses the IDENTICAL per-(sku, warehouse-site) `>=` + `created_at` tiebreak as the snapshot eshop leg: built `fg_site_sku_anchor_map()` + one `resolve_fulfilment_site(['channel'=>'eshop'])` call at the top of Step 5; per-row pass test against that map; **fallback = strict `> $anchorDate`** for SKUs with no warehouse count. Symmetric by construction → Σcards==Σphysique holds under the same-day window.

**FIX 2 — snapshot transfer leg = atomic per-row UNIT-GATE.** `$fromPass`/`$toPass` still computed per-side from each site's per-SKU anchor, but admission is atomic: `$rowPass = ($fromPass || $toPass)`; both +qty(to) and −qty(from) apply together or neither → per-row net-zero GUARANTEED regardless of per-site anchor divergence. Compute stays transfer-exempt by construction (no transfer term — correct; transfers are net-zero to global physique per ITEM 1 landmine-(iv)).

**FIX 3 — SCOPE NOTE at top of `fg_stock_compute` rewritten** to the as-built PER-LEG cutoff table: eshop = per-site symmetric; B2B = strict-global symmetric; taproom = month-grained (deferred); transfers = unit-gate net-zero, compute-exempt.

**Intentionally UNCHANGED:** B2B leg (strict-global symmetric) + taproom leg (month-grained). These are NOT the same-day class.

**⚠️ ACCEPTED TRADE-OFF (PM-ruled acceptable):** the transfer unit-gate sacrifices per-site precision in the rare case of a same-day INBOUND transfer to a `to_site` that was ALSO counted later that same day → that card transiently OVERCOUNTS by qty until its next count, in exchange for the HARD global net-zero invariant. Per-site same-day-transfer settlement remains the DEFERRED stock-movement-saisie refinement.

**VERIFICATION (real, not empty-window):** synthetic same-day fixture — eshop order (SKU60 qty5, today after warehouse anchor_ts) + a **DIVERGENT-ANCHOR transfer** (SKU39: from site2 counted 06-08, to site3 counted 06-09 12:43, moved_on 06-09 08:00 → fromPass=T / toPass=F). **10/10 assertions:** baseline 8599==8599; with fixtures Σcards==Σphysique held; eshop physique −5 exactly; transfer global unchanged (74) + cards ±5 net-zero; teardown restored baseline; no stray scripts. **The divergent-anchor transfer fixture WAS constructible** (PM-flagged to confirm) — site2 warehouse vs site3 taproom anchors give the T/F split.

**Status:** Task A had NO migration → MIGRATION HEAD stays **299**. KNOWN LIMITATION 1 (eshop+transfer same-day) now CLOSED. Remaining deferred: per-site same-day TRANSFER precision (unit-gate trade-off) + taproom month-granularity.

## 🟠 OUT-OF-ORDER TRANSFER ANALYSIS (2026-06-15, PM trace; analysis only) — ⚠️ ITS "self-healing / RISK LOW / no defect" CONCLUSION IS SUPERSEDED 2026-06-17 → see §TRANSFER LEG = REAL COMPUTATION BUG below. The unit-gate net-zero reasoning here is correct ONLY for rows that reach the loop; it MISSED that the global-anchorDate SQL prefilter (`moved_on >= $anchorDate`) drops the movement entirely when any site has a newer census → source not decremented (EMBF/Renens live proof). Read the bug section, not this conclusion.
**Scenario:** team records a Renens→Crissier transfer of a beer being packaged the SAME day, BEFORE the packaging form lands. As-built reaction (VERIFIED against live VPS code, not theory):
- **Movement form is NOT stock-gated.** `add_movement` (expeditions.php L989+) validates ONLY: active SKU, both sites `holds_fg_stock=1`, from≠to, qty integer >0, `moved_on` sane (not future / not <2020). **NO source-stock check** — any active SKU/qty moves regardless of recorded on-hand. The `EXP_MOV_STOCK_MAP` over-transfer hint (L6458, JS) is **advisory amber only, NEVER blocks** (overselling/over-moving is legal — production may be planned). So the move is NOT blocked.
- **It does NOT drive stock negative or strand.** The inter-site transfer leg lives in `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` ONLY (compute() is transfer-EXEMPT, transfers net-zero to global physique — ITEM 1 landmine-(iv)). It applies as an **atomic per-row UNIT-GATE** (Task A FIX 2): `$rowPass = ($fromPass || $toPass)` → BOTH +qty(to_site) and −qty(from_site) apply together or neither → **per-row net-zero GUARANTEED**, Σcards==Σphysique HELD regardless of which/whether the packaging exists yet. Cards CAN read negative (intentional honest signal, explicit `SCOPE NOTE: do NOT clamp to 0`, fg-stock.php ~L1391) but global is never corrupted.
- **No replay-ordering dependency.** Transfer gate is `moved_on >= anchorDate` + per-site DATE/created_at tiebreak — date-keyed, NOT insert-order. Production credit lands at the **production site (Renens, DB-derived `site_type='production'`)** via `fg_prod_since_anchor()` keyed on packaging `event_date`. So **same-day input order does not matter to the end state.**
- **END STATE after packaging lands = CORRECT, self-healing, no defect.** Sequence: (1) transfer entered first → Renens card shows −qty (the moved units not yet produced), Crissier card +qty, Σ unchanged; (2) packaging form lands later same day → `fg_prod_since_anchor` credits +production to Renens → the transient −qty nets back up. No double-count (transfer is net-zero, never enters depletion legs), no strand (qty is at Crissier as intended), no global negative. The ONLY artifact is a **transient negative Renens card visible in the window between the two entries** — cosmetic, self-resolving, honest.
- **Guards/visibility:** no review-queue flag, no negative-stock alert fires for this; the operator sees the advisory amber over-move hint on the movement form (if qty>live_futur) and the transient negative card on the Stock-PF snapshot. Both are signals, not errors.
- **RISK RANK: LOW / non-defect.** The architecture (transfer in snapshot-only + atomic net-zero unit-gate + production keyed on event_date not insert-order) makes the out-of-order case self-correct. **Lightest "fix" if the transient-negative cosmetics ever bother the operator:** none needed for correctness; could soften the snapshot card to annotate "en attente de conditionnement" when a negative is fully explained by same-day transfers exceeding counted+produced — pure display, no model change. Do NOT add a hard stock-gate to the movement form (would break the legal "move planned production" workflow + contradict the never-block-overselling ruling).

## 🔴🔴 TRANSFER LEG = REAL COMPUTATION BUG — GLOBAL-anchorDate PREFILTER DROPS INTER-SITE MOVEMENTS (2026-06-17, PM live-traced + reproduced on VPS; CORRECTS the 2026-06-15 OUT-OF-ORDER analysis above which wrongly ruled this leg "self-healing / no defect")
**OPERATOR REPORT (Kouros 2026-06-17):** EMBF 129u at Renens (site1) Mon 2026-06-15; a 120u Renens→Zeubi transfer was entered the same Monday; Stock-PF still shows **129 at Renens** (source NOT decremented). PM reproduced LIVE: `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` returns site1 EMBF **qty=129, transfer_in=0, transfer_out=0** — the −120 leg is NOT applied. (NB EMBF sku 26 is a **Keg**, not the bottle; operator's "format bouteille" was a mislabel — the keg is the one with the live transfer mv#48.)
**ROOT CAUSE (CONFIRMED, same class as B2B below).** The transfer leg's fetch SQL (`app/fg-stock.php` ~L1446-1454) is `SELECT … FROM inv_stock_movements WHERE is_tombstoned=0 AND moved_on >= ?` bound to the **GLOBAL `$anchorDate`** (snapshot-local, = `MAX(counted_at)` across ALL anchorRows = the latest census date of ANY location). On 2026-06-17 site3 Taproom was counted 2026-06-16, so global `$anchorDate=2026-06-16` → the prefilter drops EVERY movement with `moved_on < 2026-06-16`, incl. mv#48 (EMBF 1→2 120u, moved_on 2026-06-15) and 45 of 63 non-tombstoned rows. The per-site UNIT-GATE tiebreak (L1466-1481, `$rowPass=$fromPass||$toPass`) is CORRECT but **never runs** — the row is already excluded by the coarse global prefilter before the loop. (Replayed: `$fromPass` for mv#48 = TRUE on the gate math — census id=440 counted 06-15 07:30:54, mvTs 06-15 09:48:58 → same-day `mvTs>anchor_ts` TRUE; the gate WOULD admit it; only the SQL prefilter kills it.)
**WHY THE 06-15 ANALYSIS MISSED IT:** that trace reasoned the gate was `moved_on >= anchorDate + per-site tiebreak` and concluded net-zero/self-healing — but treated `$anchorDate` as benign. It is the **global polluted max census date**, identical to the production-leg pollution `566b9d3` fixed and the B2B pollution ruled below. The transfer leg is the **3rd instance of global-anchorDate pollution**, NOT solved by Task A (Task A added the per-site tiebreak *inside* the loop but left the global `moved_on >= $anchorDate` prefilter on the fetch). 🔴 The "transient-negative self-heals, RISK LOW / non-defect" conclusion (§OUT-OF-ORDER, L663-670) is **SUPERSEDED** — when any site has a newer census than the move date, the transfer is silently dropped on BOTH legs, so it never even shows the transient negative; the source just stays overstated. Σcards==Σphysique still HOLDS (both +to and −from dropped together → net-zero), which is exactly why the invariant gate is BLIND to it — only operator ground-truth catches it (same blindness as B2B).
**RULING — the fix mirrors the B2B/eshop/prod fixes: remove the global-anchorDate prefilter; gate purely on the per-(site,sku) anchor map.** Replace `WHERE is_tombstoned=0 AND moved_on >= $anchorDate` with a date floor that does NOT use the polluted global max — fetch movements `moved_on >= MIN(per-site census across the two sites)` OR simplest+safest: fetch ALL non-tombstoned rows (66 today, trivially small) and let the existing per-side `$fromPass/$toPass` map gate decide admission. The UNIT-GATE atomic `$rowPass=$fromPass||$toPass` already preserves per-row net-zero → Σcards==Σphysique stays held. **Keep the SAME `siteSkuAnchorMap` + same-day created_at tiebreak already in the loop — only the fetch's coarse prefilter changes.** A movement whose moved_on is strictly before BOTH sites' per-sku anchors correctly contributes nothing (both `$fromPass`,`$toPass` false → row skipped in-loop) — so dropping the SQL floor does NOT resurrect genuinely-pre-anchor moves.
**FIX LOCUS:** `app/fg-stock.php` `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` transfer leg `$mvStmt` (~L1446-1488). NO compute() change (compute is transfer-EXEMPT by construction — transfers net-zero to global physique, ITEM 1 landmine-(iv)). NO migration, NO schema change (read-fix, same shape as `5b9858e`/`2192153`/B2B). **INVARIANTS:** (1) Σcards==Σphysique — unit-gate already guarantees per-row net-zero, preserved; (2) genuinely-pre-anchor moves stay un-applied via the in-loop per-site gate, not the SQL floor; (3) beer-tax neutrality (transfer is a location fact, net-zero qty); (4) no new store / single-home R1. **VERIFY:** after fix, EMBF site1 must read 129−120=9 (+ any same-day production credit), site2 +120; re-run the live snapshot probe (site1 EMBF transfer_out must become 120). **EQUIP: sql + coder (+ webapp-testing read-only smoke of ?view=stock).** ⚠️ This is the SAME bug class as B2B (below) — consider fixing BOTH global-anchorDate-pollution remnants in one pass; they share the root cause and the per-site-anchor remedy.

## 🔴 B2B EXPEDIE LEG = REAL COMPUTATION BUG (2026-06-10 — SUPERSEDES the earlier "label-only" / "intentionally-deferred B2B remainder" finding)
**The earlier ruling that the B2B same-day case was a benign deferred remainder ("count already reflects the shipment, double-count-safe") was WRONG.** Operator + live DOAF (sku 20) raw data confirm a genuine miscomputation. RECLASSIFIED: this is a CORRECTNESS bug in `fg_stock_compute()` Step 4 (and symmetrically in `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` Leg 1), NOT a label issue and NOT acceptably-deferred.

**ROOT CAUSE (CONFIRMED).** Step 4 deducts shipped B2B orders with `o.requested_date > $anchorDate` where `$anchorDate` = the **GLOBAL `MAX(counted_at)` across ALL sites** (fg-stock.php L276). The anchor SUM is correctly per-(sku,location), but the B2B cutoff is global. DOAF anchors: loc1 Production 06-08 (8), loc2 Warehouse 06-08 (36), loc3 Taproom 06-09 (1) → global anchorDate = **06-09** (polluted by Taproom counting a day later). ord#4 (req 06-08, shipped, 6u) fails `06-08 > 06-09` → NOT deducted → physique stuck at 45. Reality: warehouse+production were counted 06-08, the 6 shipped from them on 06-08 is NOT in those 06-08 counts → it MUST come off. **This is the exact production-leg pollution class that `566b9d3` already fixed for the production leg — the B2B leg is the LAST surviving global-cutoff leg that has a per-site finer anchor available** (eshop closed by Task A; prod by 566b9d3/d3fb954).

**RULING — the canonical fix is per-(sku, ship-from-site) anchor cutoff on the B2B leg, mirroring how the prod + eshop legs already settle.** Use the SAME `fg_site_sku_anchor_map()` the eshop leg + snapshot already build. The ship-from site = `resolve_fulfilment_site()` for the order (fulfilment_site_id_fk → customer default_delivery_site → channel default), which the snapshot Leg 1 ALREADY computes per order. Predicate becomes per-row: deduct when `requested_date > siteAnchorDate(ship-from)`, with **COALESCE→global `$anchorDate`** for SKUs uncounted at that site (mirrors prod-leg COALESCE fallback). For DOAF: ord#4 ships from warehouse (loc2, anchor 06-08) → `06-08 > 06-08`? NO under strict `>`. → SAME-DAY BOUNDARY MUST BE RULED (below).

**SAME-DAY BOUNDARY RULING — option (a): per-location anchor + INCLUSIVE `requested_date >= siteAnchorDate` for the B2B leg.** Operator needs the same-day-as-warehouse-anchor shipment (ord#4, req 06-08 == warehouse anchor 06-08) deducted. The created_at tiebreak the eshop leg uses is NOT available here — the existing comment is correct that `ord_orders.created_at` is ENTRY time (back-datable), so it can't order a same-day ship vs count. Two sub-cases at the same calendar day: (i) order shipped from a site BEFORE that site's count that day → already in the count, must NOT re-deduct; (ii) shipped AFTER the count → not in count, must deduct. With only DATE granularity we cannot distinguish (i) from (ii). **OPERATOR'S OPERATIONAL MODEL resolves the tie: a same-day shipment is NOT yet reflected in that day's count (the count is a morning/point-in-time snapshot, shipments flow after) → default to DEDUCT same-day → inclusive `>=` on the SHIP-FROM site's anchor.** This does NOT reintroduce the genuine "shipped strictly BEFORE an earlier count" double-count: an order with `requested_date < siteAnchorDate` still fails `>=` and stays in the count (correct — a 06-05 shipment is already absent from a 06-08 count). Option (b) (keep `>` but de-pollute the global max) would still drop the legitimate same-day ord#4; option (c) (explicit ship timestamp) is the eventual real fix but needs a SOURCE column (no DATETIME ship-time exists) — DEFER, not required now. **CANONICAL = (a).**

**ACCEPTED RESIDUAL (inclusive `>=` trade-off, PM-ruled OK).** A B2B order shipped from a site on the same calendar day, where that shipment WAS already physically captured in that day's count, will be double-deducted (counted-out AND deducted). This is the symmetric inverse of the eshop residual and is rare (same-site count + same-day pre-count ship). Accept it for the operator's stated default (count = point-in-time, ships flow after). The only true fix is a ship timestamp (option c) — log as the deferred precision item, same bucket as taproom month-granularity.

**Q3 — SNAPSHOT IS NOT ALREADY RIGHT; both functions share the SAME global-cutoff B2B leg → they are SYMMETRIC, so there is NO Σcards != Σphysique divergence today.** Verified in code: snapshot Leg 1 (L859-884) uses identical `o.requested_date > ?` against the same global `$anchorDate` (L832-836). So the invariant Σcards==Σphysique HOLDS through this bug (both under-deduct ord#4 identically) — which is precisely why the bug is invisible to the invariant gate and only the operator's ground-truth catches it. **CONSEQUENCE: the fix must land in BOTH legs in lockstep (compute Step 4 AND snapshot Leg 1) to PRESERVE symmetry.** Fixing only one breaks Σcards==Σphysique. This is a both-functions fix, NOT compute-only.

**FIX LOCUS (precise).** `app/fg-stock.php`: (1) `fg_stock_compute()` Step 4 (~L370-390) — the `o.requested_date > ?` global predicate; (2) `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` Leg 1 (~L859-884) — the matching `o.requested_date > ?`. Snapshot Leg 1 ALREADY resolves the per-order ship-from site (`resolve_fulfilment_site`, L887) and ALREADY builds `fg_site_sku_anchor_map()` (L842) — so the snapshot has every input; compute Step 4 must add the same per-row resolve + map lookup (compute currently SUM/GROUPs in SQL — it will need to fetch per-order rows like the snapshot does, or resolve ship-from per (order) before aggregating). Update the SCOPE NOTE B2B bullet (L300-303) from "strict-global > (symmetric)" to "per-(sku, ship-from-site) anchor, inclusive >= same-day, COALESCE→global; symmetric across both functions". Adjust comments at L859-864 (which currently justify the strict-`>` no-tiebreak as correct) to the new ruling.

**INVARIANTS THAT MUST NOT BREAK (canonical stock SoT):** (1) Σcards==Σphysique — fix both legs in lockstep; (2) the genuine "shipped strictly before a count" guard — orders with requested_date < ship-from anchor stay un-deducted (the `>=`/`>` boundary only changes SAME-day behavior); (3) eshop + transfer same-day handling untouched (Task A); (4) beer-tax neutrality (location/cutoff fact, not a quantity fact — total deducted qty changes only by genuinely-missed same-day ships, which is the correct correction); (5) no new FG-depletion path / single-home (R1) — this is a predicate change inside the one existing B2B leg, no new store.

**THE 36-vs-39 GAP: NOT mine to resolve — operator ground-truth.** Operator: "45 − 6 on Monday → 36 today" but 45−6=39. The 3-unit gap is invisible in the DB (no June flows: physique=45=anchor exactly). DO NOT invent a flow to close it. Orchestrator reconciles with operator (hypotheses: operator tracks warehouse loc2=36 as the operational number with 6 shipped from production loc1; or the 45 aggregation itself is being read differently). The compute fix makes physique = 45 − 6 = **39** (ord#4 deducted), which is the architecturally-correct number; the operator's "36" is a separate reconciliation, NOT a target the code should hit.

**EQUIP: sql + coder + webapp-testing.** BOTH compute + snapshot (not compute-only). No migration (predicate change, data-layer `app/fg-stock.php` only — DATETIME ship-time is the DEFERRED option-c, not this fix). Verification gate: synthetic divergent-anchor B2B fixture (warehouse 06-08 + taproom 06-09, shipped order req 06-08) → ord#4-class order DEDUCTED; Σcards==Σphysique held; an order req < ship-from anchor NOT deducted (guard intact); teardown clean. DOAF live check: physique 45→39 after fix.

### ✅ SHIPPED + OPERATOR-CONFIRMED 2026-06-10 — B2B expedie per-(sku, ship-from-site) anchor fix is LIVE and SETTLED
**The fix landed and is CORRECT per the operator.** Operator's verbatim ruling: *"inventory take is always at start of week. following orders, even same day, must deduct."* → the start-of-week count is the baseline; same-day-and-later shipments deduct. **LIVE-VERIFIED: DOAF (sku 20) physique = 39** (Zeubi warehouse 36 − 6 Monday ship = 30; Production 8; Taproom 1); deployed + Σcards==Σphysique held 7455==7455.
- **🔧 AS-BUILT = THREE-tier predicate (CORRECTS the earlier 2-tier ruling above; the 2-tier `>=`/COALESCE→global model is SUPERSEDED).** Implemented IDENTICALLY in BOTH `fg_stock_compute()` Step 4 AND `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` Leg 1 (symmetric, lockstep — invariant preserved):
  - **(a) SKU counted at the ship-from site** → `requested_date >= site_anchor_date` (INCLUSIVE — operator's same-day-deducts model).
  - **(b) SKU counted elsewhere but NOT at this site** → `requested_date >= global anchorDate` (INCLUSIVE).
  - **(c) SKU NEVER counted anywhere** → `requested_date > global anchorDate` (STRICT `>`). Needed to keep Σcards==Σphysique for never-counted SKUs (e.g. ZEPV sku 61): their anchor-date shipments would otherwise deduct ASYMMETRICALLY — in the snapshot (→ negative row) but NOT in compute (dropped via `!isset($byId)`). Tier (c) preserves the pre-fix behaviour for untracked SKUs and restores symmetry.
- The earlier "label-only / double-count-safe / intentionally-deferred remainder" finding (above §B2B EXPEDIE LEG header) is **FULLY SUPERSEDED** — the bug was real, the fix is per-(sku,ship-from-site) anchor, and tier (c) is the symmetry-preserving addition the 2-tier ruling missed for never-counted SKUs. The ACCEPTED RESIDUAL (same-day pre-count ship double-deduct, option-c ship-timestamp the eventual real fix) STILL stands and is unchanged. Only same-day TRANSFER precision + taproom month-granularity remain deferred.

**PM RULING 2026-06-12 (Opus-relayed status + new operator instruction "differentiate weekly operational stocktake vs end-of-month COGS stocktake"):**

Repack leg LEFT UNGATED as live (out of scope). Post-deploy: webapp-testing smoke `?view=stock` + per-(sku,loc) >1-active spot-check; Opus verifies INDEPENDENTLY (FG/COGS-adjacent).
- **#2 DISCRIMINATOR DESIGN (durable, the operator's real ask) — gated follow-up, BEFORE any June COGS run:**
  - **The hazard, PM-probed live 2026-06-12:** `inv_fg_stocktake` has NO weekly/month-end discriminator. `cogs-monthly-compile.ts` (maltytask, 2 sites: L~323 + L~734) reads `SELECT sku,sku_id_fk,qty FROM inv_fg_stocktake WHERE month_closed=? ORDER BY sku` — **NO is_active filter, NO location aggregation, NO latest-pick**. May 2026 = 34 rows / 34 sku / **1 location** / 1 date → COGS correct BY ACCIDENT (single-site census). June 2026 = 109 rows / 52 sku / **4 locations** / 2 dates (06-08:81 + 06-09:27 active, different SKUs — NO sku×loc has >1 June row today, so no current double-count). **TWO defects the discriminator must close: (a) weekly counts carry the current month_closed tag → when the real June-30 census lands IN ADDITION, the WHERE month_closed query sums weekly+monthly ≈ doubles FG; (b) even one census now spans 4 locations → COGS must aggregate cross-site per SKU (today it happens to sum all rows, which IS the right cross-site total, but is unguarded against the weekly contamination).**
  - **Canonical model = add `count_type ENUM('operational','month_end') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'operational'` to inv_fg_stocktake** (NOT a separate table — one fact, one table; the count IS an FG census row, its PURPOSE is the new attribute). Durable-modeling honored: NOT NULL + DEFAULT (no NULL fall-through), ENUM vocabulary not free-text. NEW migration (338, RE-VERIFY --status; head currently 337) — NO new table so NO schema_meta row needed (ALTER on existing).
  - **Writer:** the Saisies PF-card / `expeditions.php?view=stocktake` entry path sets `count_type`. Default path = 'operational' (weekly). Month-end census = an explicit operator affordance (toggle/"Clôture mensuelle" mode on the form) that writes 'month_end'. Confirm the exact entry-point with operator — do NOT guess which form writes the census.
  - **Backfill (mig 338 DML, evidence-based, NOT guessed):** May 34 rows (counted_at=2026-05-31, the census May COGS correctly consumed) → `count_type='month_end'`. June 109 rows (06-08/06-09 weekly) → stay `'operational'` (the DEFAULT). April 41 inactive rows → leave default (already excluded by is_active=0; seeded period, immutable). This is seeding from existing canonical state = NOT guessing.
  - **COGS query change (both sites in cogs-monthly-compile.ts):** `WHERE month_closed=? AND count_type='month_end'` AND pick latest-per-(sku,location) within the period (ROW_NUMBER ORDER BY counted_at DESC,id DESC) THEN SUM across locations per sku. Mirror the is_active handling already there (April seeded rows are is_active=0 — keep the no-is_active-filter ONLY if month_end rows are reliably the census; safer: filter is_active=1 for computed months, but April-seed rows would break that → PM note: keep the existing "no is_active filter" but rely on count_type='month_end' as the discriminant; VERIFY April seed rows are NOT count_type='month_end' OR are intentionally included). 🔴 Opus verifies the May fiche reproduces TO THE CENT after the query change (regression invariant — May is immutable/published; the new query MUST still yield 47 701.56 FG).
  - **EQUIP: sql + coder** (migration + writer PHP + cogs-monthly-compile.ts TS) **+ ui** (month-end toggle on the saisie form) **+ webapp-testing** (smoke the census-mode write).
- **#3 SEQUENCING — CONFIRMED:** ship operational fix TODAY (June not closing today; May immutable/correct). Discriminator = NEXT work item, MUST land + be May-regression-verified BEFORE any `cogs-monthly-compile --apply --month 2026-06`.
