## 🔴 ANCHOR TIEBREAK BUG — `MAX(id)` ≠ latest COUNT → stale-count inflates the anchor (LOCALIZED 2026-06-12, PM read-only probe; operator-flagged via DOAF).
**Operator audit 2026-06-12: "DOAF (Double Oat 20L keg) is NOT 83 across all stocks — inflated."** PM live-probe CONFIRMS 83 IS the bug, ground truth = 45. ROOT CAUSE: `fg_stock_compute()` / `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` define the per-(sku,location) anchor as **`MAX(id)` among `is_active=1`**, NOT `MAX(counted_at)`. When a location has >1 active count and they were INSERTED out of count-date order, `MAX(id)` picks the row with the highest **autoincrement id**, which is NOT necessarily the latest **physical count**.
- **DOAF (sku_id_fk=20, recipe_id=30, format_id=15 Keg 20L, scope='base') live rows:** loc1 Production = id27 (April, inactive) + **id377 counted 2026-05-31 qty 46 (active)** + **id286 counted 2026-06-08 qty 8 (active)**; loc2 Zeubi/Logistique = id209 counted 06-08 qty 36; loc3 Taproom = id320 counted 06-09 qty 1; loc4 Nausikraft = none.
- **The defect:** loc1 `MAX(id)=377` → anchor uses the 05-31 count of **46**, IGNORING the genuinely-later 06-08 count of **8** (id286 < id377 because the May row was entered AFTER the June row). Anchor = 46+36+1 = **83 (WRONG)**. Correct anchor (latest count = `MAX(counted_at)`, tiebreak `MAX(id)`) = 8+36+1 = **45**.
- **Why `MAX(id)` was chosen:** it was a same-day tiebreak (Task A / Option-2, `created_at`-as-tiebreak narrative). It is RIGHT for two counts on the SAME date, WRONG as the PRIMARY order key — count recency must be `counted_at` FIRST, then id as the same-date tiebreak. The arc header (L11-22 of app/fg-stock.php) literally says "anchor = latest count per (sku, location) — MAX(id) per pair" — the doc conflates "latest count" with "MAX(id)". They diverge exactly when an older-dated count is inserted later (backfill, correction, parallel-run).
- **Naive `SUM(qty) WHERE is_active=1` = 91** (all 4 active rows incl. BOTH loc1 rows double-counted) — that is the OTHER wrong number; neither 91 nor 83 is right; **45** is.
- **FIX (the correct anchor subquery):** per (sku, location), pick the row with `MAX(counted_at)`, tiebreak `MAX(id)` for same-date. NOT `MAX(id)` alone. Apply IDENTICALLY in BOTH `fg_stock_compute()` AND `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` (the §B2B invariant-coupling rule — byte-symmetric or Σcards≠Σphysique). The flow-window start (anchor_date) ALSO derives from this row's `counted_at` → fixing the tiebreak auto-fixes the depletion window. **EQUIP: sql + coder + webapp-testing.** No migration (data-layer predicate). Verify: DOAF anchor 83→45; Σcards==Σphysique held; spot-check other SKUs with >1 active count per location (correction/backfill candidates) didn't shift wrongly. 🔴 Opus verifies INDEPENDENTLY (FG/COGS-adjacent — the anchor feeds the COGS-fiche FG census).
- **⚠️ INTERACTS with the never-counted-SKU gap below (do NOT conflate):** that one is a ROW-EXISTENCE asymmetry for scope='none' SKUs; THIS one is a wrong-row pick for SKUs WITH counts. Both live in the same two functions; a combined fix pass is reasonable but they are DISTINCT defects.

## 🔴 NEVER-COUNTED-SKU ROW-EXISTENCE ASYMMETRY = the Σcards≠Σphysique gap (LOCALIZED 2026-06-12, PM read-only probe). NOT same-day; NOT a predicate boundary; tier-(c)'s "restores symmetry" claim was WRONG.
**Live state 2026-06-12: Σphysique(compute)=8177 vs Σcards(snapshot)=6255 → GAP 1922** (the operator's "22" was an earlier, smaller instance of the SAME class; magnitude grew with new ZEPV sales). Root cause is NOT a same-day cutoff and NOT the `>=`/`>` boundary — it is a **ROW-EXISTENCE asymmetry between the two functions for SKUs that have NO anchor row anywhere** (`inv_fg_stocktake` has zero active rows for them; here `stocktake_scope='none'` cuve SKUs):
- **Dominant: ZEPV (sku 61, "Cuve de service", scope='none', NEVER counted).** Two B2B `shipped` orders req 2026-06-11 (1000 + 900 = 1900). `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` Leg 1 tier (c) (strict `>` global anchor 06-09; 06-11>06-09 passes) **manufactures NEGATIVE cards from the sales side alone** — −1000 at Zeubi warehouse (ship-from) + −900 at Nausikraft consignment — Σ −1900. `fg_stock_compute()` deducts the same 1900 but the SKU **has no anchor entry, so Step 9 NEVER EMITS A ROW for it** (`!isset($byId[sku])` → dropped) → contributes **0** to Σphysique. compute=0, snapshot=−1900 → 1900 of the 1922 gap. **The −112 on the Nausikraft consignment card is purely this (sales-only negatives on a never-anchored site).**
- **Tail (the other 22): sku 62/64/66/68/69/70/71/72/74/77/297/302** — same class, 1–4 units each, never-counted cuve/keg SKUs whose handful of B2B/eshop sales the snapshot admits as small negatives while compute drops the row. **THIS tail IS the operator's original "22-unit gap."** So the headline 1922 = 1900 (ZEPV alone) + 22 (the long-standing tail).
- **WHY tier (c) did NOT fix it (the recorded reasoning at §B2B …THREE-tier (c) is mis-stated):** tier (c) only changes the *predicate boundary* to strict `>`. But ZEPV's orders are req 06-11, comfortably **>** the 06-09 global anchor — they PASS tier (c) in BOTH functions identically. The divergence is downstream of the predicate: the **snapshot emits a row whenever a leg touches a (site,sku) pair** (sales create negative rows), whereas **compute only emits rows seeded by a positive anchor**. For a never-counted SKU there is no seed → compute has no row to deduct from → 0; the snapshot has nothing but the deduction → negative. Predicate symmetry ≠ row-set symmetry. **The arc's line-560 claim "tier (c) preserves … Σcards==Σphysique for never-counted SKUs" is FALSIFIED by live data — correct it when the fix lands.**
**🔴 OPERATOR-CORRECTED RESOLUTION (2026-06-12, PM-ratified) — supersedes options (1)/(2) below.** Operator reframed + PM live-probe CONFIRMED: the 13 divergent SKUs are NOT "missing counts" — they **legitimately do not belong in the packaged-FG depletion model at all**. All 13 carry `stocktake_scope='none'` + `is_direct_sales=1` and split into two classes: **ZEPV (61)** = -V cuve, goes BBT→client direct, never passes a packaged-inventory stage (belongs in WIP/liquid COGS + beer-tax via HL, already excluded once gated); **12 tail (62/64/66/68/69/70/71/72/74/77/297/302, format_id 2=B12 / 4=4PB)** = Shopify bundle SKUs whose real packaged inventory is the COMPONENT bottles, not the bundle line. ⟹ **the FIX is to GATE the FG-depletion legs on `stocktake_scope != 'none'`** (don't deplete packaged FG by a SKU that isn't packaged-inventorised), NOT to surface them as honest negatives. This makes the derived FG view's membership predicate match the canonical fact the column already owns (one-fact-one-table; refuse-don't-NULL spirit preserved — we're not zeroing a real depletion, we're declaring non-membership).
  - **Discriminator = `stocktake_scope` (CANONICAL), NOT `is_non_stock`.** Live: `stocktake_scope` fully populated across all 182 active SKUs (base 52 / cage 42 / none 61 / single 27); **`is_non_stock=1` on ZERO rows** — it was mig 322 for T7 tap machines, but T7 was ruled OUT of `ref_skus` entirely (§② equipment ruling), so the flag is inert and the eshop leg's existing `rs.is_non_stock = 0` filter defends a class that doesn't exist. Replace that dead filter with `stocktake_scope != 'none'` (or AND them). Flag-hygiene: decide `is_non_stock` fate w/ operator (backfill-from-scope OR scrap → scrapping-backlog RULE 1); do NOT split the gate across both flags.
  - **WHICH LEGS (verified against live `app/fg-stock.php`):** GATE the 3 SALES legs — **Step 4/Leg 1 (B2B)** [ZEPV's path], **Step 5/Leg 2 (eshop)** [the 12 tail's path; replace the dead is_non_stock filter here], **Step 6/Leg 3 (taproom)** [no scope=none rows today but gate for symmetry] — in **BOTH functions, identically** (the §B2B invariant-coupling rule: predicate must stay byte-symmetric or Σcards≠Σphysique). Gate at the leg level so `salesBySiteSku` never contains a scope=none SKU → the snapshot's "sales-but-no-anchor → create row" block (~L1285-1316, the actual phantom factory) never synthesizes them. ALSO add the predicate to **Step 3 production leg** for defense (today it already excludes via run_type='cuv'/no-events). **Do NOT gate the TRANSFER leg** (unit-gated net-zero by design; scope=none SKUs shouldn't appear there, and gating risks breaking the atomic from/to pairing).
  - **🟢 SEPARATION PROVEN (the pressure-test that validates the gate):** live snapshot shows 18 negative rows / 17 SKUs = TWO classes. The gate removes ONLY the 13 scope=none phantoms (ZEPV −1900, bundles −1..−4). It correctly LEAVES UNTOUCHED the genuine honest-negatives on REAL inventoried SKUs — **ALTB(2,base −1), DGDF(9,base −3), DIB4(10,base −2/75), STI4C(52,base −6/30)** — which are the designed "shipped from a site with less attributed than was there" signal (per-order site override + transfers correct those). `scope != 'none'` cleanly splits suppress-phantom from keep-honest-negative.
**SUPERSEDED EARLIER OPTIONS (kept for context, do NOT implement):** ~~(1) compute emits a negative row for any leg-touched SKU~~ / ~~(2) snapshot suppresses sales-only negatives for never-counted SKUs~~ — both treated the 13 as un-anchored-but-belong; operator clarified they DON'T belong. The line-560 "tier (c) preserves Σcards==Σphysique for never-counted SKUs" claim stays FALSIFIED; correct it when the gate lands.
**eshop-BUNDLE COMPONENT DECOMPOSITION = DEFERRED to Phase 4 (cage engine), NOT this fix.** A bundle sale DOES consume real packaged goods (component bottles + cage + box + labels) — correct model = BOM decomposition (bundle sale → COMPONENT inventory drawdown), which is the ④-Phase 2 cage/box/COGS engine (gated on 2026-06-15 cage anchor + Shopify pickup-signal ON HOLD). **Prerequisite before ANY bundle→component build = settle the base↔single↔bundle UNIT NESTING** (24→1→12/4 ladder; which SKU is inventory-of-record) — same dimension-discipline gate as F2; a "quick" bundle→single decompose before that = the 24× collapse hazard (`942431e` class). Base/single bottles ARE inventoried + anchored (DIBBU qty 33, etc.) so the target inventory exists. **Flag the "component depletion via eshop bundles not yet reflected" gap to operator NOW — do not silently close it** (this was already the recorded ④-Phase 2 position).
**EQUIP: sql + coder + webapp-testing** (+ ui only if `?view=stock` needs blank-state handling for the now-absent rows). No migration (data-layer `app/fg-stock.php`, predicate change in both fns + dead-filter swap). Verification gate (🔴 Opus verifies INDEPENDENTLY — COGS-adjacent): (a) zero negative rows from scope=none SKUs; (b) the 4 genuine honest-negatives ALTB/DGDF/DIB4/STI4C UNCHANGED; (c) `Σ(snapshot per-sku) == compute physique per-sku` for every scope!=none SKU; (d) Σcards==Σphysique to the unit. Probe recipe (read-only, reusable): `fg_stock_compute()` Σphysique vs `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` Σtotal_units, then per-SKU diff.

## 2026-06-10 — ROLE-BASED DUAL STOCK VISUALS (physique total + team's home-site physique): PM PRE-BUILD RULING
Operator wants two figures per logged-in user on the Expéditions stock surface: **physique total** + **the physique of the user's team's home site**. Logistics (Nathan/Stéphane/Joelson) → Zeubi/warehouse; Production → Zgeg/production; Marketing (Olivier) → Taproom/pos.

**LIVE USER/SITE MODEL (PM-probed 2026-06-10 — verified, do not re-probe unless schema changes):**
- **NO `users.site_id_fk` / `home_site_id` exists.** `users` cols: role ENUM(`admin`,`operator`,`viewer`,`manager`), `manager_scope` ENUM(`production`,`logistics`,`all`) NULL, `access_preset_id_fk`→`ref_access_presets`. NO department/team/site column.
- **Team partition lives in TWO places, neither alone covers everyone:** managers carry `manager_scope` (production/logistics/all); **operators have `manager_scope=NULL`** and are partitioned ONLY by `access_preset_id_fk`. Presets: 1=manager, 2=production_operator, 3=logistics_operator, 8=marketing. Roster confirms: Nathan(8,mgr logistics)+Stéphane(9)+Joelson(10) on preset 3; Maxime/Charles/Xavier/Alex on preset 2; Olivier(19) on preset 8.
- **`ref_sites.site_type` ENUM(`production`,`warehouse`,`pos`,`consignment`)** is the clean SoT for the target-site dimension. Rows: 1 Zgeg=production, 2 Zeubi=warehouse, 3 Taproom=pos, 4 Nausikraft=consignment.

**RULING (decisive):**
1. **DERIVE team→site_type at the SoT level — do NOT hardcode names, do NOT add a `users.home_site_id_fk` migration.** The home-site is a TEAM attribute, not a per-user fact; a per-user FK would be a parallel/divergent store of something `manager_scope`+`preset` already encode. The mapping is **team → site_type**, then `ref_sites WHERE site_type=? AND is_active=1` (set-valued, exactly how `fg_stock_compute()` already derives prod sites). Mapping: **logistics→warehouse, production→production, marketing→pos**. `consignment` (Nausikraft) has no team → never a home site.
2. **Team resolution = a single helper `exp_user_home_site_type($user): ?string`** with this precedence: (i) if `manager_scope` set → `production`/`logistics`/`all`; (ii) else map `access_preset_id_fk` via `ref_access_presets.preset_key` (`production_operator`→production, `logistics_operator`→logistics, `marketing`→pos, `manager`→all). Map by **`preset_key` (the stable string), NOT the numeric id** — ids are environment data. `all`/admin/viewer/unmapped → NULL (no single home site). This reads existing columns, NO new column, NO migration. (NB: build the team→site_type map from `preset_key` + the `manager_scope`/`site_type` enums — both are stable enum vocabularies, so the only "config" is the 3-row correspondence table in PHP, which is the legitimate place for an enum↔enum mapping that has no DB home.)
3. **SOURCE the per-site physique from `fg_stock_location_snapshot()`, NOT a re-query.** It already returns `locations[]` each with `id`,`name`,`site_type`,`total_units`,`total_hl` (verified L1269-1277). The home-site figure = the snapshot location whose `site_type` == the user's home_site_type (sum if a team maps to >1 active site of that type — currently 1:1, but keep it set-valued). Physique total = the existing TOTAL strip number (`fg_stock_compute()` physique sum) — already computed. So this is a PURE RENDER-LAYER change reading two existing derivations; ZERO new compute, ZERO new store. **Confirmed: R1 single-home is untouched — no new FG-depletion path.**
4. **GRACEFUL DEFAULT for no-home-site users (admin, manager_scope=all, viewer, unmapped):** show **physique total + a compact all-sites breakdown** (the 3-4 location cards already exist on `?view=stock`; on the strip, total only with a "tous sites" affordance). NEVER fabricate a home site; NEVER hide total. Admin/Kouros wants the full picture, not one site.
5. **RENDER LOCUS — both surfaces, but reuse the snapshot:**
   - `?view=stock` header (`expeditions.php` render block ~L2591+) ALREADY calls `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` (L1653) → add the home-site highlight there for free.
   - The pinned `exp-cmd-stock-strip` on `?view=commandes` (~L2389) currently does NOT call the snapshot (only `fg_stock_compute` for `$cmdFgPhysique`, L2380). To show the home-site figure on the strip, **add a `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` call on the commandes view** (it's a pure-SELECT lib fn, operator-frequency load — acceptable, same justification as the existing extra `fg_stock_compute` calls L1963/L1986). Strip shows: **physique total + physique <home-site-name>** (use the canonical `ref_sites.name` display string from the snapshot row, e.g. "Zeubi (Logistique)", NEVER re-derive from site_type).
6. **NO-DB-NOMENCLATURE:** label with the canonical site name from `ref_sites.name` (already in the snapshot payload), not the enum (`warehouse`/`pos`) and not a hardcoded "Zeubi". The team→site_type derivation is internal; the operator sees "physique Zeubi (Logistique)".

**DIVERGENCE FLAGS:** (i) hardcoding the three names = the exact anti-pattern to refuse (ruling #1/#2 derive instead); (ii) a `users.home_site_id_fk` migration = a parallel store of team-encoded data (refused — derive from `manager_scope`+`preset_key`); (iii) re-querying per-site stock instead of reading the snapshot = a second derivation path that can drift from the cards (ruling #3 forbids); (iv) `consignment` has no team — never surfaces as a home site.

**SCOPE NOTE FOR ORCHESTRATOR — one operator choice to confirm before dispatch:** the operator named individuals but described teams; the `manager_scope`+`preset_key` derivation covers all of them today (verified). The only judgment is the no-home-site default for `manager_scope='all'` / admin (Gonzalo/Yves are production managers → production; but a future `scope='all'` manager, and Kouros-admin, get the all-sites breakdown per ruling #4). Confirm with the operator that an `all`-scope user seeing total + all-sites (not one site) is the intended behaviour. Everything else is derivable with no choice.

**EQUIP: ui + sql + coder + webapp-testing** (render-layer change in `expeditions.php` + the team→site_type helper reading `ref_access_presets`/`users`; smoke `?view=stock` and `?view=commandes` as a logistics user shows physique total + physique Zeubi; as admin shows total + all-sites). NO migration (HEAD stays 303). Files: `app/fg-stock.php` (NONE — read-only reuse), `public/modules/expeditions.php` (helper + strip + stock-header render), `public/css/expeditions.css` (strip second-figure styling, no inline CSS).

## ✅ "Activité récente" SKU ACTIVITY TIMELINE in the stock drill-down — SHIPPED + LIVE 2026-06-10 (NO migration; render-only `expeditions.php` + NEW `public/css/expeditions-sku-history.css`; SELECTIVE deploy; NOT committed — operator parallel-work tree)
4th section inside the `?view=stock` `exp-stock-ledger` drill-down, **below "Répartition par site"** (per-location block §above). Single chronological (date DESC) merged list of the SKU's last events, 3 types: customer **Order** (↓, date·client·qty), packaging **Production/Conditionnement** (↑, date·qty), stock **Mouvement** (↔ neutral, date·"from → to"·qty). Empty → muted "Aucune activité récente".
- **Architecture = exactly per PM ruling, pattern (A) bulk-bucket (NOT per-SKU WHERE):** 3 bulk queries TOTAL for the whole page regardless of SKU count, each `ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY sku_id_fk ORDER BY date DESC) <= 15` + 90-day window + historical-only (`date <= CURDATE()`); bucketed into `$timelineBySkuId`; merged + usort DESC + cap-15 at render. **NO AJAX, NO endpoint, NO second derivation path** (R1 honored — read-only, writes nothing).
- **Data sources + predicate parity:** **Orders** = `ord_order_lines×ord_orders×ref_customers`, `status<>'cancelled'` AND `order_type='customer'` (internal eshop/taproom EXCLUDED — already separate ledger legs), client=`COALESCE(NULLIF(ref_customers.name,''),'—')` escHtml'd. **Packaging** = `bd_packaging_v2` **mirroring `fg_prod_since_anchor()` predicates EXACTLY** (is_tombstoned=0, is_white_label=0, sku_id_fk IS NOT NULL, **`run_type<>'cuv'` load-bearing**, FLOOR(prod_total_units/units_per_pack)) — the ONE INTENDED divergence = anchor-cutoff dropped for the 90-day window history (code-commented). **PREDICATE-PARITY VERIFIED** packaging-vs-`fg_prod_since_anchor` (identical except anchor-cutoff) → the R3 production-divergence risk is CLOSED. **Movements** = `inv_stock_movements×ref_sites(from,to)`, is_tombstoned=0, neutral.
- **UI:** reused `.exp-ledger-*` table rhythm + NEW scoped `.exp-evt-*` / `.exp-ledger-evt--order|--pkg|--move` classes; sketch-arrow glyphs (NOT emoji); dates via `exp_fmt_date()` (day-first); type colour via row class.

### ✅ SHOPIFY-INGEST VPS REHOME — EXECUTED + LIVE + COMMITTED 2026-06-12 (OPTION 2; PHP-rewrite REJECTED). The brief's blocking premise ("VPS has NO Node/tsx toolchain") was FALSE — it's just not on the login PATH.
> **DONE:** Option 2 executed exactly as ruled. `/opt/maltytask-pipeline` synced to current HEAD (`bin/deploy.sh --apply-pipeline`; stale 05-22 copy gone, ingest md5-matches local + has shipping_lines/fulfilment_mode; npm ci ran); `secrets/shopify.env` on VPS (640, maltytask:www-data); cron `db/cron/maltytask-shopify-ingest.cron` → `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-shopify-ingest` (`*/15`, maltytask user, nvm idiom, DB 127.0.0.1:3306 via db.env, NO tunnel); **commit `5ade521`.** VPS dry-run + a real freshening run (board now seconds-fresh, 3164 eshop orders); **autonomous fire CONFIRMED** (11:00 UTC tick wrote the log, idempotent no-op). Local-WSL `*/15` tunnel crontab RETIRED — VPS cron is sole runner. The /opt-sync GATE is CLEARED (the sync IS what fixed the stale-script hazard the ruling flagged). Ruling rationale retained below for provenance.
> Trigger "shopify rehome"/"rehome ingest"/"shopify cron VPS"/"php rewrite shopify"/"node on VPS" → read THIS block first.
**LIVE-VERIFIED VPS GROUND TRUTH (2026-06-12, ssh maltyweb):**
- **Node IS on the VPS** under nvm: `/var/www/maltytask/.nvm/nvm.sh` → **node v22.22.2**; **tsx binary present** at `/opt/maltytask-pipeline/node_modules/.bin/tsx`. `which node` empty ONLY because nvm isn't on the login PATH — the `document-ingest`/`ingest-recap` crons ALREADY invoke it via `NVM_DIR=/var/www/maltytask/.nvm bash -c '. nvm.sh && node_modules/.bin/tsx …'`. So the "PHP-only box" framing is wrong: it's a DUAL PHP+Node(nvm)+Python3 box.
- **The maltytask PIPELINE repo is ALREADY deployed to the VPS at `/opt/maltytask-pipeline`** (lib + scripts + node_modules + secrets + package.json) — SEPARATE from the PHP app at `/var/www/maltytask`. **`scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts` is ALREADY PRESENT there** (`/opt/maltytask-pipeline/scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts`, 23516 bytes, dated 2026-05-22). The script doesn't need porting — it's on the box.
- **The TS ingest is ALREADY VPS-runnable verbatim:** it connects via `lib/repos/mysql-pool.ts` which reads `DB_HOST`/`DB_PORT` from env; the pool's own doc comment says *"On the VPS itself DB_PORT=3306 (direct, no tunnel)."* On the VPS, MySQL is local → NO tunnel, NO 13306. Two env vars (`SHOPIFY_STORE`/`SHOPIFY_ADMIN_TOKEN`) + a VPS `secrets/shopify.env` (mode 640, www-data group, NOT committed) are all that's missing. line-idempotency already fixed (`bac5501`).
- **The RE-1 / BC external-API-pull pattern on the VPS is PYTHON, not PHP** — `maltytask-bc-sales` cron runs `scripts/python/ingest_bc_sales_ledger.py` (OAuth2 client-credentials against `login.microsoftonline.com`, `requests` + `pymysql` localhost:3306, watermark anti-join, ON DUPLICATE KEY idempotency, creds `config/bc.env` keys BC_TENANT_ID/CLIENT_ID/CLIENT_SECRET/ENVIRONMENT, mode 640). It is currently DISABLED-pending-smoke. So there is NO "PHP-on-VPS external-API-pull" pattern to converge with — the established external-pull connector pattern is a stand-alone Python/`requests` cron. Converging Shopify onto a *PHP* skeleton would mean inventing a 3rd pattern, not reusing one.
**RULING:** **Option 2 — rehome the proven TS ingest as `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-shopify-ingest`** running from `/opt/maltytask-pipeline` (mirror the `document-ingest` cron's nvm-bash idiom + a flock), DB_HOST=127.0.0.1 DB_PORT=3306, with `secrets/shopify.env` landed on the VPS. **Option 1 (PHP rewrite) REJECTED:** it would reimplement a mature, COGS-adjacent, fulfilment-fact-bearing classifier (`shipping_lines→fulfilment_mode`, the canonical pickup-signal list per [[feedback_canonical_list_call_not_copy]]) in PHP/curl with real regression risk on a proven path — and gain NOTHING, since Node is already on the box and the script is already deployed. **Splitting the classifier across two languages is the exact divergence smell to avoid:** `fulfilment_mode` is the load-bearing pickup/delivery fact; it must stay SINGLE-HOMED in the TS ingest (one writer, one classification, `ref_shipping_methods` as the only mapping store). A PHP twin = two implementations of one fact = silent drift. **Architecture verdict:** this IS the "consume the host" pattern correctly applied — the host being consumed is the ALREADY-PRESENT `/opt/maltytask-pipeline` Node runtime + VPS cron infra, NOT a PHP rewrite. Strangler doesn't mandate PHP; it mandates the compute homing on the VPS via the standing cron mechanism, which Option 2 satisfies.
**BUILD (small, low-risk):** (1) land `secrets/shopify.env` on VPS (operator, not committed); (2) author `db/cron/maltytask-shopify-ingest.cron` (source-of-truth in maltyweb repo, deployed via `bin/deploy.sh --apply` → `/etc/cron.d/`) mirroring the `document-ingest` nvm idiom: `*/15` or `*/30`, user=`maltytask`, `flock -n /tmp/maltytask-shopify-ingest.lock`, `cd /opt/maltytask-pipeline && HOME=… NVM_DIR=/var/www/maltytask/.nvm bash -c '. $NVM_DIR/nvm.sh && DB_HOST=127.0.0.1 DB_PORT=3306 node_modules/.bin/tsx scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts --since "$(date -d "2 days ago" +%F)"' >> /var/log/maltytask/shopify-ingest.log 2>&1`; (3) ensure `/opt/maltytask-pipeline` carries the `bac5501` version of the script (it's dated 05-22 — PRE-`bac5501`; the line-idempotency/shipping_lines/`--until`-default fixes must be synced to /opt before arming — VERIFY); (4) pre-create the log (`maltytask:www-data`); (5) dry-run on VPS first (the ingest `--dry-run` ROLLBACKs); (6) keep the board freshness-chip (already shipped) — it's the staleness sentinel that justified this whole rehome and stays valuable. **OPEN op-decisions:** OK to put `shopify.env` on VPS + install the cron; pick cadence. **GATE:** sync /opt pipeline to post-`bac5501` HEAD before arming (else the rehomed cron runs the OLD pre-fix script). **SIZE:** ~S (one cron file + secret + a /opt sync + dry-run smoke), NOT the M-to-L PHP rewrite. **EQUIP: coder + sql + webapp-testing** (cron/CLI/host = coder; the freshness-chip + any board verification = webapp-testing smoke; sql only if the dry-run distribution check touches the DB). NB cross-repo: cron source lands in **maltyweb** `db/cron/`; the ingest script lives in **maltytask**/`/opt`.

### 🔑 KEY FINDING — the pickup/click&collect signal lives in `shipping_lines[].title` (LIVE Shopify-API-probed during planning), NOT a tag and NOT `fulfillment_status`.
- `fulfillment_status` is a COMPLETION-state field (a false friend for pickup-vs-ship — do NOT use it to classify mode). The ingest does **NOT currently fetch `shipping_lines`** at all.
- **Live pickup titles:** "La Tap & Shop (mercredi - samedi ; 14h-22h)", "RETRAIT A CRISSIER"/"à CRISSIER", "La Nébuleuse SA".
- **Live delivery titles:** "La Poste - Vinologue (fragile)", "Vinologue Suisse - Fragile", "Standard Suisse", "Livraison Offerte/offerte/gratuite".
- Messy free-text (team is mid-standardization) → **curated map + `review` bucket, NEVER guess** (never-guess-a-mapping canon). The plan threads this directly into the §① pickup double-deplete forward-hazard: once pickup orders carry a mode and sync into `inv_sales_orders`, they deplete via the eshop leg and the picking view READS them — they are NEVER re-created as `ord_orders` (XOR holds).

### Approved phased roadmap
- **Phase 0 — FEED FOUNDATION (buildable NOW, do FIRST; zero depletion risk):** (1) fix the ingest **line-idempotency bug** (below) FIRST; (2) capture `shipping_lines` → raw `shipping_method_title` on `inv_sales_orders`; (3) curated classification — new **`ref_shipping_methods`** (title_norm UNIQUE, `fulfilment_mode` enum pickup/delivery, seeded from the verified live titles) → ingest sets new **`inv_sales_orders.fulfilment_mode ENUM('pickup','delivery','review')`** (unknown→`review`, operator-actionable); (4) fix the hardcoded `--until 2026-05-01` (cause of the **Apr-30 data gap**) → default "now" + one backfill run + **cron the ingest on a trailing window with a flock**. Mig `320_inv_shipping_method_map.sql` (table + the 2 `inv_sales_orders` cols). NO gate.
- **Phase 1 — PER-ORDER ESHOP PICKING SURFACE (buildable now, READ-ONLY re depletion):** replace the date-aggregate eshop auto-row on the Commandes board with **per-order eshop rows** (customer, SKU pills, **pickup/delivery badge** 🏬 Retrait / 🚚 Livraison / ⚠ à classer, per-day pickup-vs-ship counters). Pure read from `inv_sales_orders`+lines (XOR trivial). Rows carry `data-eshop-order-id` (NOT `data-order-id`) so existing status JS never touches them; no actions yet. Include eshop in the cross-date search. Gate: Phase-0 `fulfilment_mode`.
- **Phase 2 — FULFILMENT TRACKING + BIDIRECTIONAL SHOPIFY WRITE-BACK (the big piece; build after 0+1):** eshop workflow state in a **dedicated 1:1 side table** `inv_sales_fulfilment` (keyed on `inv_sales_orders.id`) + `inv_sales_fulfilment_events` (append-only) — MIRRORS the `ord_orders` + `ord_order_status_events` pattern; lazy-created on first action (absent row ⇒ implicit `new`/`idle`); mode-aware lifecycle (delivery new→picking→picked→fulfilled; pickup …→ready_for_pickup→picked_up); cols incl. `shopify_sync_state` enum idle/pending/pushed/failed + `shopify_fulfillment_id` + push_error/attempts. Mig `321_inv_sales_fulfilment.sql`. UI: `exp_render_eshop_chips()` + sync badge + `public/js/eshop-fulfilment.js`. API: `public/api/eshop-fulfilment-status.php` (clone of `expeditions-status.php`; one txn = event + cache upsert + audit; push-triggering status sets `shopify_sync_state='pending'`, does NOT call Shopify inline). Worker: **`scripts/push-shopify-fulfilment.ts`** (cron+flock) drains `pending` → Shopify Admin **Fulfillment Orders API** (delivery=create fulfillment→fulfilled; pickup=ready_for_pickup→picked_up); idempotent (check open fulfillment-order + stored id; "already fulfilled"=convergence); capped retry + operator re-arm. **Reverse reconcile** via the now-idempotent ingest (`source='shopify_reconcile'`). **CONFLICT POLICY: maltyweb-wins-forward — reconcile only ever ADVANCES local to match Shopify, never reverts an operator action.** GATE: confirm the Shopify Admin token has fulfillment **write** scopes (read-only blocks write-back).
- **Phase 3 — PICKUP HARDENING + TAP MACHINES (gated on the team standardizing shipping-method names):** prune/extend `ref_shipping_methods` once names settle (drive `review`→0; admin to map unknowns without deploy; split board into Retrait/Livraison lanes). **Tap machines (T7) = NON-STOCK:** new `ref_skus.is_non_stock` flag (mig `322_*`, orthogonal-flag doctrine per mig 210); fulfillable + on the picking view but excluded from FG sum via `AND rs.is_non_stock = 0` added **SYMMETRICALLY** to the eshop leg in BOTH `fg_stock_compute()` AND `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` — verify `Σcards==Σphysique` after. (Resolves the §② "T7/Cuves = equipment, must NOT deplete FG" ruling at the SKU-config level.)
- **Phase 4 — CAGE/BOX COGS ENGINE = OUT OF SCOPE (named only).** The Stage-2 / ④ Phase-2 cage/box draw-down engine (downstream CONSUMER of this fulfilment data, gated on the 2026-06-15 cage anchor) is a SEPARATE arc, not designed here.

### Hard constraints carried (non-negotiable)
- **XOR depletion:** order ∈ `ord_orders` XOR `inv_sales_orders`, never both. Eshop fulfilment workflow creates **NO** `ord_orders` rows. The discriminator is membership in `inv_sales_orders`, not a flag we invent (§①c canon).
- **Single-homed FG derivation:** `fg_stock_compute()` is the only FG depletion. ANY filter added to its eshop leg (`app/fg-stock.php` ~L462-515) MUST be mirrored in `fg_stock_location_snapshot()` (~L814-850) or `Σcards ≠ Σphysique`. **P0/P1 add NO fg-stock filter → zero depletion risk. The only symmetric-filter change is P3 (`is_non_stock`).**
- **Raw vs computed:** `inv_sales_orders`/`inv_sales_order_lines` are `class='source'`, `corrections_policy='blocked_with_redirect'` (LIVE-VERIFIED 2026-06-10) — operator workflow state goes in the `inv_sales_fulfilment` SIDE TABLE, NEVER on the raw table. An ingest-derived `fulfilment_mode` column IS OK on `inv_sales_orders` because it's a PURE FUNCTION of the Shopify pull (same class as the existing `fulfillment_status`/`financial_status`/`period` derived cols), not operator-entered state.

### 🔴 INGEST LINE-IDEMPOTENCY BUG (Shopify side — must fix FIRST, Phase-0 item 1)
`scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts` `insertOrderBatch()` L378-384: `const wasDupe = orderRes.affectedRows === 0; if (wasDupe) { ordersDupe++; continue; }` — when an order PRE-EXISTS (INSERT IGNORE no-op), it `continue`s at ORDER level → **its lines are never re-evaluated and mutable header fields never updated.** So a re-pull of a CHANGED order silently no-ops; you can NEVER enrich existing orders with `shipping_lines`/`fulfilment_mode`, advance `fulfillment_status`, or do reverse-reconcile. **Fix: on pre-existing order, still (a) `INSERT IGNORE` the lines (already row_hash-idempotent), (b) `UPDATE` the mutable header fields (`fulfillment_status`, `shipping_method_title`, `fulfilment_mode`).** This is the SHOPIFY-side parallel of the already-recorded `import_weeklyorders.php` `ord_order_lines` UNIQUE/ODKU bug (§WeeklyOrders status one-liner) — same "header idempotent, lines/mutables not" class, different table.

### Phase-0 build facts (PM-verified live 2026-06-10)
- **MIGRATION HEAD = 319 applied (`migrate.php --status`); next free = `320`.** (Parallel sessions live — re-`--status` + `ls db/migrations` at build-start per checklist; 312 already collided once 312_drop_invoice_validate_topbar vs 312_kpi_sales — so a fresh check is mandatory.)
- **`schema_meta` for the NEW `ref_shipping_methods` table:** `table_class='reference'`, `corrections_policy='allowed'`, `upstream_hint` ≈ "Shopify shipping-method title → pickup/delivery classification map. Seed from verified live titles; add/edit via Expéditions admin or direct MySQL; unknown titles land orders in fulfilment_mode='review'." (Mirrors `ref_transporters`/`ref_customers` which are exactly `reference`/`allowed`.) ONE `schema_meta` row required per the per-new-table rule.
- **The TWO new `inv_sales_orders` columns** (`shipping_method_title` VARCHAR, `fulfilment_mode` ENUM('pickup','delivery','review')): **NO schema_meta change needed** — the table is ALREADY `class='source'`/`blocked_with_redirect`; ALTER-adding ingest-derived columns does NOT change its classification (schema_meta is per-TABLE, not per-column). Just add the columns; do not touch its schema_meta row.
- **INGEST HOST / CRON = the maltytask LOCAL host, NOT the VPS.** `ingest-shopify-orders.ts` runs `npx tsx scripts/ingest-shopify-orders.ts` on the maltytask box: it reads `secrets/shopify.env`, connects to MySQL **over the SSH tunnel (13306)** via `withConnection`/`withTransaction`, emits `logAudit` to `data/audit-log.jsonl`. It is run MANUALLY today (no cron). **There is NO existing maltytask user crontab** (`crontab -l` empty). The flock pattern to MIRROR = **`scripts/send-ingest-recap.ts`** (the only flock-guarded script; "designed to be run by a flock-guarded cron", writes preview to `/tmp`, exits 0 silently when nothing to do). Follow its lock idiom for the P0 ingest cron (and the P2 worker cron). NB: the SSH tunnel needs `-o ServerAliveInterval=30 -o ExitOnForwardFailure=yes` for an unattended cron run (existing keepalive convention).
- **APR-30 GAP cause = hardcoded `--until 2026-05-01`** in the ingest's default window (`'fulfillment_status','total_price',…` field set is fine; the date bound is the gap). Default it to "now" + run one backfill to today, THEN cron a trailing window. Dry-run-verify the backfill BEFORE going live (double-run = 0 orders/lines inserted but a changed `fulfillment_status` updates; FG totals UNCHANGED since no eshop-leg filter is added in P0).

### EQUIP — Phase-0 Sonnet build: **coder + sql** (+ webapp-testing only if P0 surfaces any rendered page — it does NOT, P0 is ingest+migration only, so coder+sql suffices). The TS edit (`ingest-shopify-orders.ts`, maltytask) = coder; the maltyweb migration `320` = sql. NB cross-repo: the migration lands in **maltyweb** (`db/migrations/`, applied via `migrate.php` on the VPS), the ingest edit lands in **maltytask** (`scripts/`, run locally over the tunnel) — two repos, one phase.

### Phase-0 gotchas (durable)
- **TS ingest edit:** preserve the `logAudit({...})` discipline — the `wasDupe` branch currently SKIPS audit; the new "update existing order" path must emit a `logAudit` event (e.g. `action:'order-updated'`) so the change shows in `data/audit-log.jsonl`. Keep `--dry-run` working (the `DryRunRollback` throw + ROLLBACK pattern at L425-434) for both the line re-eval and the header UPDATE. The order **INSERT IGNORE → upsert** change: do NOT switch the INSERT to `ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE` blindly — `row_hash` is part of the UNIQUE; a content change yields a NEW row_hash, so the upsert key must be the STABLE key (`UNIQUE(source, external_order_id)`), and the UPDATE must target only the mutable header cols (not re-stamp `created_at`/`period`). row_hash stays a change-detector, not the upsert key.
- **Migration:** MySQL 8 (no `IF NOT EXISTS` on `ADD COLUMN`; no bare SELECT in the .sql — `migrate.php` exec() leaves result sets open). FK type on `ref_shipping_methods` PK and any FK = match exactly. The `inv_sales_orders` ALTER adds 2 columns (INSTANT DDL on MySQL 8 — cheap). ENUM `fulfilment_mode` default should be `'review'` (so an un-classified order is operator-visible, never silently mis-moded). schema_meta INSERT for `ref_shipping_methods` in the same migration.

### Sequencing verdict (CONFIRMED)
- **P0 is SAFE to build + land NOW with ZERO change to `fg_stock_compute()` → zero depletion risk.** P0 adds an ingest-derived column + a classification map + cron + a bug-fix; it touches NO fg-stock leg. The first fg-stock change in the whole roadmap is P3's symmetric `is_non_stock` filter. P0+P1 ship first (immediate value, no depletion risk), then P2 (bidirectional sync, gated on the Shopify write-token scope), then P3 (gated on team name-standardization + the cage anchor).
- **Cron/backfill MUST be dry-run-verified before going live** (the ingest's `--dry-run` already ROLLBACKs; verify the `fulfilment_mode` distribution + a small `review` bucket + a double-run = 0 new rows but a changed `fulfillment_status` updates + FG totals unchanged, BEFORE arming the cron).

FK-type mismatch = our #1 migration-failure class.
- **schema_meta — MIRROR THE `ord_*` SIBLINGS, do NOT default to `'allowed'`:** `inv_sales_fulfilment` is the eshop twin of `ord_orders` → copy `ord_orders`'s schema_meta `corrections_policy` exactly; `inv_sales_fulfilment_events` is the twin of `ord_order_status_events` (append-only) → copy that row, NEVER `'allowed'` on an immutable event log. Both `table_class='operational'`; one schema_meta INSERT per table in mig 322; writer hint = "eshop-fulfilment-status.php API + future push-shopify-fulfilment.ts worker".

ROLE GATE = login-only, NO role check** (PM-verified live: `expeditions-status.php` gates purely on `current_user() !== null` → 403 if not logged in; access control is at the PAGE level via the Expéditions `ref_pages` gate, NOT in the handler). Clone that: CSRF first-gate w/ fresh-token retry hint, ONE txn (event insert + `inv_sales_fulfilment` upsert + `log_revision`), PRG/JSON. **Push-deferral CONFIRMED + load-bearing:** reaching `fulfilled`/`ready_for_pickup`/`picked_up` sets `shopify_sync_state='pending'` and returns — does NOT call Shopify inline. This is why 2A is LIVE-safe pre-scopes (nothing in 2A touches the Shopify API).

(2) **`fulfilment_mode='review'` order has NO lifecycle → handler must REFUSE advance** ("à classer d'abord"), not pick a default map (never-guess applies to lifecycle selection). ## §FG STOCKTAKE → SAISIES SURFACING + month_closed ATTRIBUTION — PM RULING 2026-06-11 (pre-build; triggered by May-2026 COGS close blocked on missing 2026-05 FG anchor)
**Context:** Closing May 2026 COGS. Of the 4 close inputs (RM closing / WIP tank_balances / sales / FG stocktake), only the **FG May-31 stocktake** is missing. Live DB (PM-probed 2026-06-11): `inv_fg_stocktake` active rows = **ONLY `month_closed='2026-06'`** (107 `maltyweb-form` counted 06-08/06-09 + 1 `manual-adjustment`); the **April anchor is GONE** (re-anchored to June) → no 2026-05 row AND no April fallback. Kouros asked: create the FG month-end stocktake and "have it sit on Saisies."

**KEY FINDING — the FG count form ALREADY EXISTS and is the canonical writer.** It is `expeditions.php?view=stocktake` (the 2026-06 rows came from it, `source='maltyweb-form'`). `inv_fg_stocktake` has **ONE writer = `expeditions.php:746` INSERT** (mig 288 generated `row_hash`; every other ref is read-only SELECT). The "absence" is purely **discoverability** — Saisies has 5 cards (packaging/racking/brewing/fermenting + **RM stocktake** `form-rm-stocktake.php`) but NO FG card. FG's count surface was built later inside the Fulfilment arc, so it never got a Saisies card.

**RULING 1 — SURFACE, don't FORK. Add a Saisies card LINKING to `expeditions.php?view=stocktake`. Do NOT factor a `form-fg-stocktake.php`; do NOT migrate the writer.** Factoring the form = a SECOND writer to a single-writer COGS-bearing table = the parallel-store divergence smell. The FG form is entangled with the Expéditions view (per-location anchor, `exp_st_scope_allowed` channel matrix, `display_family` grouping, mig-288 generated-hash UPSERT, manager-backdate, freshness chips) — re-homing is large surface, zero canonical benefit. Saisies is a **card-grid of LINKS (discovery hub)**, not a rule that every count form physically lives there (RM's own module is incidental). The racking split-card already links OUT (`form-racking.php` "Saisie classique →") — same pattern. `inv_fg_stocktake` stays Fulfilment-owned; Saisies gains a 6th card "Inventaire produits finis (PF)" → `/modules/expeditions.php?view=stocktake`. Additive — nothing superseded, no scrapping.

**RULING 2 — CORRECT the operator's premise: RM does NOT auto-attribute early-next-month counts to the prior month.** RM gives an explicit `period` month-picker (`form-rm-stocktake.php` L28-32, default = current month) and the operator CHOOSES `2026-05`. FG instead derives `month_closed = substr(counted_at,0,7)` (`expeditions.php:785`) with NO override. So the real inconsistency = **"FG has no period control; RM does"** — NOT "RM has a −1-month rule." Fix = give FG the SAME operator lever (explicit, default-but-overridable `month_closed` field), NOT a silent "if day ≤ N attribute to prior month" heuristic (= a guessed COGS-impacting attribution; would silently mis-file a legitimately-late June count into May). **Explicit operator choice over silent inference on a COGS key, always.** Note: managers CAN already backdate FG (`$stDefaultCountedAt = $stSelDate` for managers; operators always today) — so the May close is reachable today with `counted_at=2026-05-31`.

**SEQUENCING:**
- **Phase 0 (NO build — unblock May NOW):** Kouros opens `?view=stocktake`, manager-date = `2026-05-31`, enters the May-31 FG census → `month_closed='2026-05'`. ⚠️ **Per-SKU anchor means a PARTIAL May census silently leaves some SKUs anchored elsewhere — enter a COMPLETE May set.** ⚠️ **If no real May-31 physical count exists (only the June-8 one), that is a DATA-AVAILABILITY question — do NOT synthesize a May close from June data; surface it to Kouros for an explicit nearest-count decision (never-guess-COGS line).**
- **Phase 1 (small follow-up build):** Saisies 6th card → `?view=stocktake`. `saisies.php` + `saisies.css` only; NO mig, NO writer/schema change. RULE 3: card links to `expeditions` (already tour-covered) and `saisies` is tour-special-cased — check the tour saisies-chapter form-card map; dispatch tour-steward only if `tour-gap-check.php` flags. **EQUIP: ui + coder + webapp-testing.**
- **Phase 2 (small, deferrable — the durable RM/FG consistency fix):** explicit operator-chosen `month_closed` field on the FG form (default `substr(counted_at,0,7)`, overridable) mirroring RM's period picker — lets an operator count June 1-2 and attribute to May WITHOUT backdating the physical count date. `month_closed` column already exists → NO schema change, populate-path change only. **EQUIP: ui + coder + webapp-testing.**
- Phases 1 & 2 independent; BOTH safe to defer past the May close. **Do NOT gate the May close on either.**

**DIVERGENCE FLAGS:** (1) refuse any `form-fg-stocktake.php` = 2nd writer to single-writer COGS table; (2) no silent prior-month heuristic; (3) partial-May-census trap (per-SKU anchor); (4) don't fabricate a May count from June data.

NO positive credit term — not `+loose_units`, not `+from_qty×upp`, not a `+to_sku` term.** Live comment verbatim: *"Net contribution: −from_qty on from_sku_id (base box only)… Do NOT add a positive term for to_sku here."* WHY: the countable FG universe = scope ∈ {base, cage} only; everything a repack PRODUCES (the bundle `to_sku`, the loose remainder) lands in scope='none' SKUs already excluded by the `stocktake_scope <> 'none'` JOIN (the `d9f7976` gate). So opening a base box removes the WHOLE box (shipped portion + remainder) from countable FG → correct FG delta = `−from_qty × base_upp` bottle-equiv, achieved by `−1 box` and nothing else. **The struck `+loose_units→single` credit is BOTH unresolvable AND wrong-signed:** live events open ALT4 (recipe 6) → produce EPH24PB (id=75, scope='none' 4-pack) — the loose remainder is NOT ALTBU singles, and crediting the scope='single' ALTBU (countable) would mint phantom countable inventory no physical count reconciles. `loose_units`/`to_*` stay EVENT-ROW METADATA, never arithmetic inputs (live code already ignores them — verified). **NO eshop-leg bundle→single/component decomposition** — that is the deferred Phase-4 cage-COGS engine (OUT OF SCOPE), and adding it would DOUBLE-COUNT against the operator-confirmed `inv_repack_events` row (which is the SOLE stock mover for a box-open, written by `expeditions-repack.php`). Eshop leg KEEPS its `<> 'none'` exclusion. MUST land byte-symmetric in BOTH fns (R1 lockstep) — but symmetric on the `−from_qty` leg, no credit.

## §BC↔ord_orders PHASE 1 — ORDER INTEGRATION SCOPED + PM-RULED 2026-06-15 (pre-build; "on lance phase 1 pour sûr")
**GOAL:** Logistics double-enters every B2B order (BC + WeeklyOrders sheet). Phase 1 ELIMINATES the sheet: pull OPEN B2B BC sales orders → `ord_orders`/`ord_order_lines`/`ord_order_status_events`; logistics works them in the Expéditions "Commandes" tab (picking→BL→shipped). Net: logistics enters once (in BC), maltytask shows it. READ-ONLY toward BC. Phase 2 (input-on-maltytask → write-back to BC) = LATER arc.

**LIVE STATE VERIFIED 2026-06-15 (PM read-only probe):**
- `ord_orders` schema: `source ENUM('web','email','import')` DEFAULT 'web'; `source_ref VARCHAR(190)` **UNIQUE** (71/122 populated); `internal_channel ENUM('taproom','eshop','cage','shop')`; `status ENUM(entered,confirmed,picked,bl_printed,shipped,cancelled)` DEFAULT 'entered'; `transporter_id_fk`, `customer_id_fk`, `requested_date`, `parse_confidence`, `review_status ENUM(none,pending,accepted)`, `source_file_id_fk`. Distribution: web 16e/2c/4p/3blp/25sh/1canc; import 34e/4c/1p/32sh.
- `ord_order_lines`: `order_id_fk`, `sku_id_fk INT UNSIGNED` (RESTRICT), `qty DECIMAL(10,2)`, `line_comment`.
- `ord_order_status_events`: append-only TRUTH — `order_id_fk`, `status`, `occurred_at DATETIME def CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`, `user_id_fk`, `comment`.
- **WeeklyOrders importer = `scripts/import_weeklyorders.php` is a MANUAL one-shot** (reads `/tmp/wo-parsed.json`, dry-run default / `--apply`). **NO cron exists** — so "stop the cron" is a non-issue; just stop running it. Writes `source='import'`, `source_ref='weeklyorders:1955899648:r<N>'`.
- **BC connector already live = `scripts/python/ingest_bc_sales_ledger.py` (maltyweb deploy, user maltytask), cron `/etc/cron.d/maltytask-bc-sales` every 4h** — encodes the OData S2S OAuth2 + customer resolver (`bc_customer_no → ref_customers.id`) + SKU resolver (`ref_skus.sku_code WHERE is_active=1` → `ref_sku_aliases` → raw; `hl_resolved = qty × hl_per_unit`). REUSE these idioms verbatim.
- **`app/fg-stock.php` `fg_stock_compute()` has 3 DEPLETION LEGS:** Step 4 = `ord_orders` lines WHERE status='shipped' (ALL order_types deplete); Step 5 = eshop via `inv_sales_order_lines`/`inv_sales_orders` (Shopify); Step 6/taproom = `inv_sales_bc.qty_invoiced` channel='taproom'. **THIS is the double-deplete surface.**

**THE 7 RULINGS:**
1. **SOURCE = standard `salesOrders` API as set-driver** (29 live, doc-state-scoped, drops posted/shipped automatically; the custom `SalesOrder` web service returns stale 2020 orders = filtering liability). **Custom web service = TARGETED by-No lookup ONLY** to enrich each in-set order with `ShpfyOrderNo` + `Shipping_Agent_Code` IF the standard header lacks them. **PROBE FIRST** whether standard `salesOrders` exposes `ShpfyOrderNo` (some BC tenants surface it as a custom API field) — if yes, skip the hybrid entirely. Reuse OData idioms verbatim: S2S OAuth2 client-creds `config/bc.env`, OR-chained `$filter` at **50 ids/batch (BC rejects the `in` operator, HTTP 501)**, **nextLink paging, NO `$top`** ($top suppresses @odata.nextLink → silent truncation). `Shipping_Agent_Code` → `ref_transporters`.
2. **SHOPIFY DOUBLE-COUNT EXCLUSION = `ShpfyOrderNo` non-empty → EXCLUDE.** A BC sales order carrying ShpfyOrderNo IS an eshop sale already in `inv_sales_orders` (channel='eshop', deplets fg-stock Step 5). Pulling it into ord_orders double-counts on the board AND in fg-stock. Belt-braces: ALSO exclude system customers `1080` (eshop privé) + `3822` (taproom) — a B2B open order should never be for them. Net filter = `ShpfyOrderNo empty AND Sell_to_Customer_No NOT IN (1080,3822)`. No other channel leak today (Lightspeed has no feed).
3. **CUTOVER = sequenced cut, NO dual-live window.** Stop running `import_weeklyorders.php`. Add ENUM val: `ALTER TABLE ord_orders MODIFY source ENUM('web','email','import','bc') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'web';`. BC orders key `source='bc'`, `source_ref='bc:<BC OrderNo>'` (e.g. `bc:ORD201126`) — `source_ref` already UNIQUE → idempotent upsert. **Existing web/import rows AGE OUT — do NOT migrate/reconcile** (50 import + 16 web = real operator-worked orders; shipped ones won't reappear as open BC orders since BC closes on full shipment). The ~39 genuinely-open import/web rows MAY collide with the open BC set → 1st dry-run **match-report flags (customer, requested_date, lines) collisions** → operator decides per-row (cancel legacy vs skip BC pull). NEVER auto-merge. After one operator backlog-clear pass, BC is sole feed.
4. **🔴 CRUX — STATUS PRESERVATION on recurring pull.** Single rule: *the BC pull is a HEADER/LINE refresher gated on `status IN('entered','confirmed')`; status + status_events are OPERATOR-OWNED and NEVER written by the pull.* On INSERT: create order (status='entered') + lines + ONE 'entered' event. On re-pull of existing (matched by source_ref): UPDATE only `customer_id_fk`/`requested_date`/`transporter_id_fk`/`comment`/line qtys+SKUs — DO NOT write `status`, DO NOT append a status event. Freeze lines once status >= 'picked' (a BC line edit must not silently change what's being picked → flag divergence to review). `Completely_Shipped=true` / order leaves the open BC set = a **reconciliation SIGNAL surfaced on the board** ("BC reports shipped"), NOT an auto-advance/cancel — auto-advancing would (a) write unauthorized status and (b) fire fg-stock depletion on a pull not an operator action (wrong lane). Order leaving the open set must NOT delete/cancel the local row (it's mid-fulfilment locally).
5. **SKU RESOLUTION = `(Item_No, Unit_of_Measure_Code)` → ref_skus.** Item No ALONE is insufficient (same beer item ships in multiple formats; UoM code e.g. 24B selects the format/SKU). Ledger connector resolved on bare Item_No only because the ledger export is already SKU-grain; an ORDER line is item+UoM. Build/confirm a `(bc_item, bc_uom) → sku_id` resolver, reuse `ref_sku_aliases` where it already encodes the combination. **REFUSE-DON'T-NULL:** an unresolved line does NOT create a `sku_id_fk=NULL` line (RESTRICT FK forbids it anyway; a NULL line silently under-picks + under-deplets). Emit a self-sufficient review-CSV row (order No + raw item + UoM + qty, same pattern as the ledger connector's unresolved-SKU CSV) and hold the order out of apply OR apply flagged `review_status='pending'` with the bad line surfaced — operator-decided, NEVER guess item+UoM→SKU from a pattern.
6. **REFRESH = VPS cron `*/15`** (match `maltytask-shopify-ingest` cadence; open set tiny ~29 + operationally hot — logistics wants new orders visible fast; do NOT use the ledger's 4h). User maltytask, `--apply`, log to `/var/log/maltytask/`. NOT local. Webhook = Phase-2-era nicety, don't build now.
7. **MIGRATION = ONE:** the `source` ENUM extension above (MySQL-8, no IF NOT EXISTS; ENUM extension is INSTANT). `source_ref` UNIQUE already exists. **No new table → no schema_meta row.** Possibly a small `bc_uom→format` lookup if not derivable via aliases — prefer reusing `ref_sku_aliases` over a new table; confirm in build. Pre-flight: `migrate.php --status` (head was 345 at last check — RE-VERIFY, parallel sessions lead), next free number, no bare SELECT.

**DIVERGENCE FLAGS:**
- **🔴 #1 fg-stock DOUBLE-DEPLETE (live, concrete):** a Shopify-origin BC order leaking into ord_orders + getting shipped depletes BOTH Step 4 (ord_orders) AND Step 5 (eshop/Shopify) → physical FG under-counts. The ShpfyOrderNo exclusion (ruling 2) is exactly what prevents it. Same hazard class as the 2026-06-12 eshop-repack/stale-fg-stock.php double-deplete incident. **OPUS MUST INDEPENDENTLY VERIFY** the no-double-deplete invariant before done (COGS/inventory-bearing; a sub-agent PASS = a claim): assert no `ord_orders.source='bc'` row maps to a BC order with ShpfyOrderNo; spot-check an eshop order does NOT appear on the Commandes board.
- **Status clobber on re-pull** (ruling 4) — guarded by the header/line-only refresher gate.
- **NULL/guessed SKU line** (ruling 5) — refuse-don't-NULL + review CSV.
- **Parallel sale-side store drift:** `ord_orders` (open-operational) vs `inv_sales_ledger` (posted-fiscal) are DISJOINT facts joined only by BC order No — different lifecycle stages. Don't let anyone "reconcile" ord_orders qty against ledger qty as same fact. Burn engine (semaines_stock) keeps reading the ledger, NOT ord_orders.
- **off-trade / sale_class = customer attribute** (`ref_customers`) — ignore on the order pull (already ruled in WeeklyOrders arc); don't leak channel classification onto ord_orders.

**SCOPE = tight 3-4 working days** — OData/auth/customer-resolver/SKU-alias-resolver/ord_* tables/status-event model/Commandes board/match-report-dry-run discipline all REUSED. New = one connector (model on `ingest_bc_sales_ledger.py` + `import_weeklyorders.php`), one ENUM mig, the cron, the item+UoM→SKU resolver. Two well-defined seams (Shopify exclusion, status-preserving upsert). Only stretch risk = open-order collision reconciliation = one-time operator pass.
**BUILD SEQUENCE:** (a) probe standard salesOrders for ShpfyOrderNo → decide hybrid; (b) ENUM mig; (c) connector dry-run → match-report (Shopify-excluded set, customer/SKU resolution, collisions flagged); (d) Kouros reviews unmatched/collisions; (e) `--apply`; (f) cron `*/15`; (g) Opus-verify fg-stock no-double-deplete invariant.
**EQUIP coder+sql+webapp-testing** (Sonnet codes; status-preserving upsert is the careful part; webapp-testing smokes that Commandes shows BC orders + does NOT show eshop orders, read-only vs prod). Trigger "phase 1"/"BC order"/"salesOrders"/"ShpfyOrderNo"/"ord_orders BC"/"WeeklyOrders cutover"/"order integration" → READ this section.
